He said, “My Lord, prison is more desirable to me than what they call me to. Unless You turn their scheming away from me, I may yield to them, and become one of the ignorant.” (Quran, 12:33)
Thereupon his Lord answered him, and diverted their scheming away from him. He is the Hearer, the Knower. (Quran, 12:34)
Then it occurred to them, after they had seen the signs, to imprison him for a while. (Quran, 12:35)
Two youth entered the prison with him. One of them said, “I see myself pressing wine.” The other said, “I see myself carrying bread on my head, from which the birds are eating. Tell us their interpretation—we see that you are one of the righteous.” (Quran, 12:36)
He said, “No food is served to you, but I have informed you about it before you have received it. That is some of what my Lord has taught me. I have forsaken the tradition of people who do not believe in Allah; and regarding the Hereafter, they are deniers.” (Quran, 12:37)
“And I have followed the faith of my forefathers, Abraham, and Isaac, and Jacob. It is not for us to associate anything with Allah. This is by virtue of Allah’s grace upon us and upon the people, but most people do not give thanks. (Quran, 12:38)
“O My fellow inmates, are diverse lords better, or Allah, the One, the Supreme?” (Quran, 12:39)
“You do not worship, besides Him, except names you have named, you and your ancestors, for which Allah has sent down no authority. Judgment belongs to none but Allah. He has commanded that you worship none but Him. This is the right religion, but most people do not know. (Quran, 12:40)
“O my fellow inmates! One of you will serve his master wine; while the other will be crucified, and the birds will eat from his head. Thus the matter you are inquiring about is settled.” (Quran, 12:41)
And he said to the one he thought would be released, “Mention me to your master.” But Satan caused him to forget mentioning him to his master, so he remained in prison for several years. (Quran, 12:42)
The king said, “I see seven fat cows being eaten by seven lean ones, and seven green spikes, and others dried up. O elders, explain to me my vision, if you are able to interpret visions.” (Quran, 12:43)
They said, “Jumbles of dreams, and we know nothing of the interpretation of dreams.” (Quran, 12:44)
The one who was released said, having remembered after a time, “I will inform you of its interpretation, so send me out.” (Quran, 12:45)
“Joseph, O man of truth, inform us concerning seven fat cows being eaten by seven lean ones, and seven green spikes, and others dried up, so that I may return to the people, so that they may know.” (Quran, 12:46)
He said, “You will farm for seven consecutive years. But whatever you harvest, leave it in its spikes, except for the little that you eat.” (Quran, 12:47)
Then after that will come seven difficult ones, which will consume what you have stored for them, except for the little that you have preserved. (Quran, 12:48)
Then after that will come a year that brings relief to the people, and during which they will press. (Quran, 12:49)
The king said, “Bring him to me.” And when the envoy came to him, he said, “Go back to your master, and ask him about the intentions of the women who cut their hands; my Lord is well aware of their schemes.” (Quran, 12:50)
He said, “What was the matter with you, women, when you tried to seduce Joseph?” They said, “Allah forbid! We knew of no evil committed by him.” The governor’s wife then said, “Now the truth is out. It was I who tried to seduce him, and he is telling the truth.” (Quran, 12:51)
“This is that he may know that I did not betray him in secret, and that Allah does not guide the scheming of the betrayers.” (Quran, 12:52)
“Yet I do not claim to be innocent. The soul commands evil, except those on whom my Lord has mercy. Truly my Lord is Forgiving and Merciful.” (Quran, 12:53)
The king said, “Bring him to me, and I will reserve him for myself.” And when he spoke to him, he said, “This day you are with us established and secure.” (Quran, 12:54)
He said, “Put me in charge of the storehouses of the land; I am honest and knowledgeable.” (Quran, 12:55)
And thus We established Joseph in the land, to live therein wherever he wished. We touch with Our mercy whomever We will, and We never waste the reward of the righteous. (Quran, 12:56)
But the reward of the Hereafter is better for those who believe and observed piety. (Quran, 12:57)
And Joseph's brothers came, and entered into his presence. He recognized them, but they did not recognize him. (Quran, 12:58)
When he provided them with their provisions, he said, “Bring me a brother of yours from your father. Do you not see that I fill up the measure, and I am the best of hosts?” (Quran, 12:59)
“But if you do not bring him to me, you will have no measure from me, and you will not come near me.” (Quran, 12:60)
They said, “We will solicit him from his father. We will surely do.” (Quran, 12:61)
He said to his servants, “Put their goods in their saddlebags; perhaps they will recognize them when they return to their families, and maybe they will come back.” (Quran, 12:62)
When they returned to their father, they said, “O father, we were denied measure, but send our brother with us, and we will obtain measure. We will take care of him.” (Quran, 12:63)
He said, “Shall I trust you with him, as I trusted you with his brother before? Allah is the Best Guardian, and He is the Most Merciful of the merciful.” (Quran, 12:64)
And when they opened their baggage, they found that their goods were returned to them. They said, “Father, what more do we want? Here are our goods, returned to us. We will provide for our family, and protect our brother, and have an additional camel-load. This is easy commerce.” (Quran, 12:65)
He said, “I will not send him with you, unless you give me a pledge before Allah that you will bring him back to me, unless you get trapped.” And when they gave him their pledge, he said, “Allah is witness to what we say.” (Quran, 12:66)
And he said, “O my sons, do not enter by one gate, but enter by different gates. I cannot avail you anything against Allah. The decision rests only with Allah. On Him I rely, and on Him let the reliant rely.” (Quran, 12:67)
And when they entered as their father had instructed them, it did not avail them anything against Allah; it was just a need in the soul of Jacob, which he carried out. He was a person of knowledge inasmuch as We had taught him, but most people do not know. (Quran, 12:68)
And when they entered into the presence of Joseph, he embraced his brother, and said, “I am your brother; do not be saddened by what they used to do.” (Quran, 12:69)
Then, when he provided them with their provisions, he placed the drinking-cup in his brother’s saddlebag. Then an announcer called out, “O people of the caravan, you are thieves.” (Quran, 12:70)
They said, as they came towards them, “What are you missing?” (Quran, 12:71)
They said, “We are missing the king’s goblet. Whoever brings it will have a camel-load; and I personally guarantee it.” (Quran, 12:72)
They said, “By Allah, you know we did not come to cause trouble in the land, and we are not thieves.” (Quran, 12:73)
They said, “What shall be his punishment, if you are lying?” (Quran, 12:74)
They said, “His punishment, if it is found in his bag: he will belong to you. Thus we penalize the guilty.” (Quran, 12:75)
So he began with their bags, before his brother's bag. Then he pulled it out of his brother’s bag. Thus We devised a plan for Joseph; he could not have detained his brother under the king’s law, unless Allah so willed. We elevate by degrees whomever We will; and above every person of knowledge, there is one more learned. (Quran, 12:76)
They said, “If he has stolen, a brother of his has stolen before.” But Joseph kept it to himself, and did not reveal it to them. He said, “You are in a worse situation, and Allah is Aware of what you allege.” (Quran, 12:77)
They said, “O noble prince, he has a father, a very old man, so take one of us in his place. We see that you are a good person.” (Quran, 12:78)
He said, “Allah forbid that we should arrest anyone except him in whose possession we found our property; for then we would be unjust.” (Quran, 12:79)
And when they despaired of him, they conferred privately. Their eldest said, “Don’t you know that your father received a pledge from you before Allah, and in the past you failed with regard to Joseph? I will not leave this land until my father permits me, or Allah decides for me; for He is the Best of Deciders.” (Quran, 12:80)
“Go back to your father, and say, ‘Our father, your son has stolen. We testify only to what we know, and we could not have prevented the unforeseen.’” (Quran, 12:81)
“Ask the town where we were, and the caravan in which we came. We are being truthful.” (Quran, 12:82)
He said, “Rather, your souls have contrived something for you. Patience is a virtue. Perhaps Allah will bring them all back to me. He is the Knowing, the Wise.” (Quran, 12:83)
Then he turned away from them, and said, “O my bitterness for Joseph.” And his eyes turned white from sorrow, and he became depressed. (Quran, 12:84)
They said, “By Allah, you will not stop remembering Joseph, until you have ruined your health, or you have passed away.” (Quran, 12:85)
He said, “I only complain of my grief and sorrow to Allah, and I know from Allah what you do not know.” (Quran, 12:86)
“O my sons, go and inquire about Joseph and his brother, and do not despair of Allah's comfort. None despairs of Allah's comfort except the disbelieving people.” (Quran, 12:87)
Then, when they entered into his presence, they said, “Mighty governor, adversity has befallen us, and our family. We have brought scant merchandise. But give us full measure, and be charitable towards us—Allah rewards the charitable.” (Quran, 12:88)
He said, “Do you realize what you did with Joseph and his brother, in your ignorance?” (Quran, 12:89)
They said, “Is that you, Joseph?” He said, “I am Joseph, and this is my brother. Allah has been gracious to us. He who practices piety and patience—Allah never fails to reward the righteous.” (Quran, 12:90)
They said, “By Allah, Allah has preferred you over us. We were definitely in the wrong.” (Quran, 12:91)
He said, “There is no blame upon you today. Allah will forgive you. He is the Most Merciful of the merciful.” (Quran, 12:92)
“Take this shirt of mine, and lay it over my father’s face, and he will recover his sight. And bring your whole family to me.” (Quran, 12:93)
As the caravan set out, their father said, “I sense the presence of Joseph, though you may think I am senile.” (Quran, 12:94)
They said, “By Allah, you are still in your old confusion.” (Quran, 12:95)
Then, when the bearer of good news arrived, he laid it over his face, and he regained his sight. He said, “Did I not say to you that I know from Allah what you do not know?” (Quran, 12:96)
They said, “Father, pray for the forgiveness of our sins; we were indeed at fault.” (Quran, 12:97)
He said, “I will ask my Lord to forgive you. He is the Forgiver, the Most Merciful.” (Quran, 12:98)
Then, when they entered into the presence of Joseph, he embraced his parents, and said, “Enter Egypt, Allah willing, safe and secure.” (Quran, 12:99)
And he elevated his parents on the throne, and they fell prostrate before him. He said, “Father, this is the fulfillment of my vision of long ago. My Lord has made it come true. He has blessed me, when he released me from prison, and brought you out of the wilderness, after the devil had sown conflict between me and my brothers. My Lord is Most Kind towards whomever He wills. He is the All-knowing, the Most Wise.” (Quran, 12:100)
“My Lord, You have given me some authority, and taught me some interpretation of events. Initiator of the heavens and the earth; You are my Protector in this life and in the Hereafter. Receive my soul in submission, and unite me with the righteous.” (Quran, 12:101)
This is news from the past that We reveal to you. You were not present with them when they plotted and agreed on a plan. (Quran, 12:102)
But most people, for all your eagerness, are not believers. (Quran, 12:103)
You ask them no wage for it. It is only a reminder for all mankind. (Quran, 12:104)
How many a sign in the heavens and the earth do they pass by, paying no attention to them? (Quran, 12:105)
And most of them do not believe in Allah unless they associate others. (Quran, 12:106)
Do they feel secure that a covering of Allah’s punishment will not come upon them, or that the Hour will not come upon them suddenly, while they are unaware? (Quran, 12:107)
Say, “This is my way; I invite to Allah, based on clear knowledge—I and whoever follows me. Glory be to Allah; and I am not of the polytheists.” (Quran, 12:108)
We did not send before you except men, whom We inspired, from the people of the towns. Have they not roamed the earth and seen the consequences for those before them? The Home of the Hereafter is better for those who are righteous. Do you not understand? (Quran, 12:109)
Until, when the messengers have despaired, and thought that they were rejected, Our help came to them. We save whomever We will, and Our severity is not averted from the guilty people. (Quran, 12:110)
In their stories is a lesson for those who possess intelligence. This is not a fabricated tale, but a confirmation of what came before it, and a detailed explanation of all things, and guidance, and mercy for people who believe. (Quran, 12:111)
Alif, Lam, Meem, Ra. These are the signs of the Scripture. What is revealed to you from your Lord is the truth, but most people do not believe. (Quran, 13:1)
Allah is He who raised the heavens without pillars that you can see, and then settled on the Throne. And He regulated the sun and the moon, each running for a specified period. He manages all affairs, and He explains the signs, that you may be certain of the meeting with your Lord. (Quran, 13:2)
And it is He who spread the earth, and placed in it mountains and rivers. And He placed in it two kinds of every fruit. He causes the night to overlap the day. In that are signs for people who reflect. (Quran, 13:3)
On earth are adjacent terrains, and gardens of vines, and crops, and date-palms, from the same root or from distinct roots, irrigated with the same water. We make some taste better than others. In that are proofs for people who reason. (Quran, 13:4)
Should you wonder—the real wonder is their saying: “When we have become dust, will we be in a new creation?” Those are they who defied their Lord. Those are they who will have yokes around their necks. Those are the inhabitants of the Fire, where they will remain forever. (Quran, 13:5)
And they urge you to hasten evil before good, though examples have passed away before them. Your Lord is full of forgiveness towards the people for their wrongdoings, yet your Lord is severe in retribution. (Quran, 13:6)
Those who disbelieve say, “Why was a miracle not sent down to him from his Lord?” You are only a warner, and to every community is a guide. (Quran, 13:7)
Allah knows what every female bears, and every increase and decrease of the wombs. With Him, everything is by measure. (Quran, 13:8)
The Knower of the Invisible and the Visible; the Grand, the Supreme. (Quran, 13:9)
It is the same; whether one of you conceals his speech, or declares it; whether he goes into hiding by night, or goes out by day. (Quran, 13:10)
He has a succession; before him and behind him, protecting him by Allah’s command. Allah does not change the condition of a people until they change what is within themselves. And if Allah wills any hardship for a people, there is no turning it back; and apart from Him they have no protector. (Quran, 13:11)
It is He who shows you the lightening, causing fear and hope. And He produces the heavy clouds. (Quran, 13:12)
The thunder praises His glory, and so do the angels, in awe of Him. And He sends the thunderbolts, striking with them whomever He wills. Yet they argue about Allah, while He is Tremendous in might. (Quran, 13:13)
To Him belongs the call to truth. Those they call upon besides Him do not respond to them with anything—except as someone who stretches his hands towards water, so that it may reach his mouth, but it does not reach it. The prayers of the unbelievers are only in vain. (Quran, 13:14)
To Allah prostrates everyone in the heavens and the earth, willingly or unwillingly, as do their shadows, in the morning and in the evening. (Quran, 13:15)
Say, “Who is the Lord of the heavens and the earth?” Say, “Allah.” Say, “Have you taken besides Him protectors, who have no power to profit or harm even themselves?” Say, “Are the blind and the seeing equal? Or are darkness and light equal? Or have they assigned to Allah associates, who created the likes of His creation, so that the creations seemed to them alike? Say, “Allah is the Creator of all things, and He is The One, the Irresistible.” (Quran, 13:16)
He sends down water from the sky, and riverbeds flow according to their capacity. The current carries swelling froth. And from what they heat in fire of ornaments or utensils comes a similar froth. Thus Allah exemplifies truth and falsehood. As for the froth, it is swept away, but what benefits the people remains in the ground. Thus Allah presents the analogies. (Quran, 13:17)
For those who respond to their Lord is the best. But as for those who do not respond to Him, even if they possessed everything on earth, and twice as much, they could not redeem themselves with it. Those will have the worst reckoning; and their home is Hell—a miserable destination. (Quran, 13:18)
Is he who knows that what was revealed to you from your Lord is the truth, like him who is blind? Only those who reason will remember. (Quran, 13:19)
Those who fulfill the promise to Allah, and do not violate the agreement. (Quran, 13:20)
And those who join what Allah has commanded to be joined, and fear their Lord, and dread the dire reckoning. (Quran, 13:21)
And those who patiently seek the presence of their Lord, and pray regularly, and spend from Our provisions to them, secretly and openly, and repel evil with good. These will have the Ultimate Home. (Quran, 13:22)
Everlasting Gardens, which they will enter, along with the righteous among their parents, and their spouses, and their descendants. And the angels will enter upon them from every gate. (Quran, 13:23)
“Peace be upon you, because you endured patiently. How excellent is the Final Home.” (Quran, 13:24)
As for those who violate the promise to Allah, after pledging to keep it, and sever what Allah has commanded to be joined, and spread corruption on earth—these, the curse will be upon them, and they will have the Worst Home. (Quran, 13:25)
Allah dispenses the provisions to whomever He wills, and restricts. And they delight in the worldly life; yet the worldly life, compared to the Hereafter, is only enjoyment. (Quran, 13:26)
Those who disbelieve say, “If only a miracle was sent down to him from his Lord.” Say, “Allah leads astray whomever He wills, and He guides to Himself whoever repents.” (Quran, 13:27)
Those who believe, and whose hearts find comfort in the remembrance of Allah. Surely, it is in the remembrance of Allah that hearts find comfort.” (Quran, 13:28)
For those who believe and do righteous deeds—for them is happiness and a beautiful return. (Quran, 13:29)
Thus We sent you among a community before which other communities have passed away, that you may recite to them what We revealed to you. Yet they deny the Benevolent One. Say, “He is my Lord; there is no god but He; in Him I trust, and to Him is my repentance.” (Quran, 13:30)
Even if there were a Quran, by which mountains could be set in motion, or by which the earth could be shattered, or by which the dead could be made to speak. In fact, every decision rests with Allah. Did the believers not give up and realize that had Allah willed, He would have guided all humanity? Disasters will continue to strike those who disbelieve, because of their deeds, or they fall near their homes, until Allah’s promise comes true. Allah never breaks a promise. (Quran, 13:31)
Messengers before you were ridiculed, but I granted the disbelievers respite, and then I seized them. What a punishment it was! (Quran, 13:32)
Is He who is watchful over the deeds of every soul? Yet they ascribe associates to Allah. Say, “Name them! Or are you informing Him of something on earth He does not know, or is it a show of words?” In fact, the scheming of those who disbelieve is made to appear good to them, and they are averted from the path. Whomever Allah misguides has no guide. (Quran, 13:33)
There is for them torment in the worldly life, but the torment of the Hereafter is harsher. And they have no defender against Allah. (Quran, 13:34)
The likeness of the Garden promised to the righteous: rivers flowing beneath it; its food is perpetual, and so is its shade. Such is the sequel for those who guard against evil, but the sequel of the disbelievers is the Fire. (Quran, 13:35)
Those to whom We gave the Scripture rejoice in what was revealed to you, while some factions reject parts of it. Say, “I am commanded to worship Allah, and to never associate anything with Him. To Him I invite, and to Him is my return.” (Quran, 13:36)
Thus We revealed it an Arabic code of law. Were you to follow their desires, after the knowledge that has come to you, you would have neither ally nor defender against Allah. (Quran, 13:37)
We sent messengers before you, and We assigned for them wives and offspring. No messenger could bring a sign except with the permission of Allah. For every era is a scripture. (Quran, 13:38)
Allah abolishes whatever He wills, and He affirms. With Him is the source of the Scripture. (Quran, 13:39)
Whether We show you some of what We have promised them, or We cause you to die—your duty is to inform, and Ours is the reckoning. (Quran, 13:40)
Do they not see how We deal with the earth, diminishing it at its edges? Allah judges; and nothing can hold back His judgment. And He is quick to settle accounts. (Quran, 13:41)
Those before them planned, but the entire plan is up to Allah. He knows what every soul earns. Those who disbelieve will know to whom the Ultimate Home is. (Quran, 13:42)
Those who disbelieve say, “You are not a messenger.” Say, “Allah is a sufficient witness between me and you, and whoever has knowledge of the Scripture.” (Quran, 13:43)
Alif, Lam, Ra. A Scripture that We revealed to you, that you may bring humanity from darkness to light—with the permission of their Lord—to the path of the Almighty, the Praiseworthy. (Quran, 14:1)
Allah—to whom belongs what is in the heavens and the earth. And woe to the disbelievers from a severe torment. (Quran, 14:2)
Those who prefer the present life to the Hereafter, and repel from the path of Allah, and seek to make it crooked—these are far astray. (Quran, 14:3)
We never sent any messenger except in the language of his people, to make things clear for them. Allah leads astray whom He wills, and guides whom He wills. He is the Mighty, the Wise. (Quran, 14:4)
We sent Moses with Our signs: “Bring your people out of darkness into light, and remind them of the Days of Allah.” In that are signs for every patient and thankful person.” (Quran, 14:5)
Moses said to his people, “Remember Allah’s blessings upon you, as He delivered you from the people of Pharaoh, who inflicted on you terrible suffering, slaughtering your sons while sparing your daughters. In that was a serious trial from your Lord.” (Quran, 14:6)
And when your Lord proclaimed: “If you give thanks, I will grant you increase; but if you are ungrateful, My punishment is severe.” (Quran, 14:7)
And Moses said, “Even if you are ungrateful, together with everyone on earth—Allah is in no need, Worthy of Praise.” (Quran, 14:8)
Has not the story reached you, of those before you, the people of Noah, and Aad, and Thamood—and those after them? None knows them except Allah. Their messengers came to them with the clear proofs, but they tried to silence them, and said, “We reject what you are sent with, and we are in serious doubt regarding what you are calling us to.” (Quran, 14:9)
Their messengers said, “Is there any doubt about Allah, Maker of the heavens and the earth? He calls you to forgive you your sins, and to defer you until a stated term.” They said, “You are only humans like us; you want to turn us away from what our ancestors worshiped; so bring us a clear proof.” (Quran, 14:10)
Their messengers said to them, “We are only humans like you, but Allah favors whomever He wills from among His servants. We cannot possibly show you any proof, except by leave of Allah. In Allah let the faithful put their trust.” (Quran, 14:11)
“And why should we not trust in Allah, when He has guided us in our ways? We will persevere in the face of your persecution. And upon Allah the reliant should rely.” (Quran, 14:12)
Those who disbelieved said to their messengers, “We will expel you from our land, unless you return to our religion.” And their Lord inspired them: “We will destroy the wrongdoers.” (Quran, 14:13)
“And We will settle you in the land after them. That is for him who fears My Majesty, and fears My threats.” (Quran, 14:14)
And they prayed for victory, and every stubborn tyrant came to disappointment. (Quran, 14:15)
Beyond him lies Hell, and he will be given to drink putrid water. (Quran, 14:16)
He will guzzle it, but he will not swallow it. Death will come at him from every direction, but he will not die. And beyond this is relentless suffering. (Quran, 14:17)
The likeness of those who disbelieve in their Lord: their works are like ashes, in a fierce wind, on a stormy day. They have no control over anything they have earned. That is the utmost misguidance. (Quran, 14:18)
Do you not see that Allah created the heavens and the earth with truth? If He wills, He can do away with you, and bring a new creation. (Quran, 14:19)
And that is not difficult for Allah. (Quran, 14:20)
They will emerge before Allah, altogether. The weak will say to those who were proud, “We were your followers, can you protect us at all against Allah’s punishment?” They will say, “Had Allah guided us, we would have guided you. It is the same for us; whether we mourn, or are patient; there is no asylum for us.” (Quran, 14:21)
And Satan will say, when the issue is settled, “Allah has promised you the promise of truth, and I promised you, but I failed you. I had no authority over you, except that I called you, and you answered me. So do not blame me, but blame yourselves. I cannot come to your aid, nor can you come to my aid. I reject your associating with me in the past. The wrongdoers will have a torment most painful.” (Quran, 14:22)
But those who believed and did good deeds will be admitted into gardens beneath which rivers flow, to remain therein forever, by leave of their Lord. Their greeting therein will be: “Peace.” (Quran, 14:23)
Do you not see how Allah presents a parable? A good word is like a good tree—its root is firm, and its branches are in the sky. (Quran, 14:24)
It yields its fruits every season by the will of its Lord. Allah presents the parables to the people, so that they may reflect. (Quran, 14:25)
And the parable of a bad word is that of a bad tree—it is uprooted from the ground; it has no stability. (Quran, 14:26)
Allah gives firmness to those who believe, with the firm word, in this life, and in the Hereafter. And Allah leads the wicked astray. Allah does whatever He wills. (Quran, 14:27)
Have you not seen those who exchanged the blessing of Allah with blasphemy, and landed their people into the house of perdition? (Quran, 14:28)
Hell—they will roast in it. What a miserable settlement. (Quran, 14:29)
And they set up rivals to Allah, in order to lead away from His path. Say, “Enjoy yourselves; your destination is the Fire.” (Quran, 14:30)
Tell My servants who have believed to perform the prayers, and to give from what We have given them, secretly and publicly, before a Day comes in which there is neither trading nor friendship. (Quran, 14:31)
Allah is He Who created the heavens and the earth, and sends down water from the sky, and with it produces fruits for your sustenance. And He committed the ships to your service, sailing through the sea by His command, and He committed the rivers to your service. (Quran, 14:32)
And He committed the sun and the moon to your service, both continuously pursuing their courses, and He committed the night and the day to your service. (Quran, 14:33)
And He has given you something of all what you asked. And if you were to count Allah’s blessings, you would not be able to enumerate them. The human being is unfair and ungrateful. (Quran, 14:34)
Recall that Abraham said, “O my Lord, make this land peaceful, and keep me and my sons from worshiping idols.” (Quran, 14:35)
“My Lord, they have led many people astray. Whoever follows me belongs with me; and whoever disobeys me—You are Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 14:36)
“Our Lord, I have settled some of my offspring in a valley of no vegetation, by Your Sacred House, our Lord, so that they may perform the prayers. So make the hearts of some people incline towards them, and provide them with fruits, that they may be thankful.” (Quran, 14:37)
“Our Lord, You know what we conceal and what we reveal. And nothing is hidden from Allah, on earth or in the heaven.” (Quran, 14:38)
“Praise be to Allah, Who has given me, in my old age, Ishmael and Isaac. My Lord is the Hearer of Prayers.” (Quran, 14:39)
“My Lord, make me one who performs the prayer, and from my offspring. Our Lord, accept my supplication.” (Quran, 14:40)
“Our Lord, forgive me, and my parents, and the believers, on the Day the Reckoning takes place.” (Quran, 14:41)
Do not ever think that Allah is unaware of what the wrongdoers do. He only defers them until a Day when the sights stare. (Quran, 14:42)
Their necks outstretched, their heads upraised, their gaze unblinking, their hearts void. (Quran, 14:43)
And warn mankind of the Day when the punishment will come upon them, and the wicked will say, “Our Lord, defer us for a little while, and we will answer Your call and follow the messengers.” Did you not swear before that there will be no passing away for you? (Quran, 14:44)
And you inhabited the homes of those who wronged themselves, and it became clear to you how We dealt with them, and We cited for you the examples. (Quran, 14:45)
They planned their plans, but their plans are known to Allah, even if their plans can eliminate mountains. (Quran, 14:46)
Do not ever think that Allah will break His promise to His messengers. Allah is Strong, Able to Avenge. (Quran, 14:47)
On the Day when the earth is changed into another earth, and the heavens, and they will emerge before Allah, the One, the Irresistible. (Quran, 14:48)
On that Day, you will see the sinners bound together in chains. (Quran, 14:49)
Their garments made of tar, and the Fire covering their faces. (Quran, 14:50)
That Allah may repay each soul according to what it has earned. Allah is Quick in reckoning. (Quran, 14:51)
This is a proclamation for mankind, that they may be warned thereby, and know that He is One Allah, and that people of understanding may remember. (Quran, 14:52)
Alif, Lam, Ra. These are the Verses of the Book; a Quran that makes things clear. (Quran, 15:1)
Perhaps those who disbelieve will wish they had been Muslims. (Quran, 15:2)
Leave them to eat, and enjoy, and be lulled by hope. They will find out. (Quran, 15:3)
We have never destroyed a town unless it had a set time. (Quran, 15:4)
No nation can bring its time forward, nor can they delay it. (Quran, 15:5)
And they said, “O you who received the message, you are insane.” (Quran, 15:6)
Why do you not bring us the angels, if you are truthful?” (Quran, 15:7)
We do not send the angels down except with reason, and they will not be held back. (Quran, 15:8)
Surely We revealed the Message, and We will surely preserve it. (Quran, 15:9)
We sent others before you, to the former communities. (Quran, 15:10)
But no messenger came to them, but they ridiculed him. (Quran, 15:11)
Thus We slip it into the hearts of the guilty. (Quran, 15:12)
They do not believe in it, though the ways of the ancients have passed away. (Quran, 15:13)
Even if We opened for them a gateway into the sky, and they began to ascend through it. (Quran, 15:14)
They would still say, “Our eyes are hallucinating; in fact, we are people bewitched.” (Quran, 15:15)
We placed constellations in the sky, and made them beautiful to the beholders. (Quran, 15:16)
And We guarded them from every outcast devil. (Quran, 15:17)
Except one who steals a hearing, and is followed by a visible projectile. (Quran, 15:18)
We spread the earth, and placed stabilizers in it, and in it We grew all things in proper measure. (Quran, 15:19)
And in it We created livelihoods for you, and for those for whom you are not the providers. (Quran, 15:20)
There is not a thing but with Us are its stores, and We send it down only in precise measure. (Quran, 15:21)
We send the fertilizing winds; and send down water from the sky, and give it to you to drink, and you are not the ones who store it. (Quran, 15:22)
It is We who give life and cause death, and We are the Inheritors. (Quran, 15:23)
And We know those of you who go forward, and We know those who lag behind. (Quran, 15:24)
It is your Lord who will gather them together. He is the Wise, the Knowing. (Quran, 15:25)
We created the human being from clay, from molded mud. (Quran, 15:26)
And the jinn We created before, from piercing fire. (Quran, 15:27)
Your Lord said to the angels, “I am creating a human being from clay, from molded mud.” (Quran, 15:28)
“When I have formed him, and breathed into him of My spirit, fall down prostrating before him.” (Quran, 15:29)
So the angels prostrated themselves, all together. (Quran, 15:30)
Except for Satan. He refused to be among those who prostrated themselves. (Quran, 15:31)
He said, “O Satan, what kept you from being among those who prostrated themselves?” (Quran, 15:32)
He said, “I am not about to prostrate myself before a human being, whom You created from clay, from molded mud.” (Quran, 15:33)
He said, “Then get out of here, for you are an outcast”. (Quran, 15:34)
“And the curse will be upon you until the Day of Judgment.” (Quran, 15:35)
He said, “My Lord, reprieve me until the Day they are resurrected.” (Quran, 15:36)
He said, “You are of those reprieved.” (Quran, 15:37)
“Until the Day of the time appointed.” (Quran, 15:38)
He said, “My Lord, since You have lured me away, I will glamorize for them on earth, and I will lure them all away.” (Quran, 15:39)
“Except for Your sincere servants among them.” (Quran, 15:40)
He said, “This is a right way with Me.” (Quran, 15:41)
“Over My servants you have no authority, except for the sinners who follow you.” (Quran, 15:42)
And Hell is the meeting-place for them all. (Quran, 15:43)
“It has seven doors; for each door is an assigned class.” (Quran, 15:44)
But the righteous will be in gardens with springs. (Quran, 15:45)
“Enter it in peace and security.” (Quran, 15:46)
And We will remove all ill-feelings from their hearts—brothers and sisters, on couches facing one another. (Quran, 15:47)
No fatigue will ever touch them therein, nor will they be asked to leave it. (Quran, 15:48)
Inform My servants that I am the Forgiver, the Merciful. (Quran, 15:49)
And that My punishment is the painful punishment. (Quran, 15:50)
And inform them of the guests of Abraham. (Quran, 15:51)
When they entered upon him, and said, “Peace.” He said, “We are wary of you.” (Quran, 15:52)
They said, “Do not fear; we bring you good news of a boy endowed with knowledge.” (Quran, 15:53)
He said, “Do you bring me good news, when old age has overtaken me? What good news do you bring?” (Quran, 15:54)
They said, “We bring you good news in truth, so do not despair.” (Quran, 15:55)
He said, “And who despairs of his Lord’s mercy but the lost?” (Quran, 15:56)
He said, “So what is your business, O envoys?” (Quran, 15:57)
They said, “We were sent to a sinful people.” (Quran, 15:58)
“Except for the family of Lot; we will save them all.” (Quran, 15:59)
“Except for his wife.” We have determined that she will be of those who lag behind. (Quran, 15:60)
And when the envoys came to the family of Lot. (Quran, 15:61)
He said, “You are a people unknown to me.” (Quran, 15:62)
They said, “We bring you what they have doubts about.” (Quran, 15:63)
“We bring you the truth, and we are truthful.” (Quran, 15:64)
“Travel with your family at the dead of the night, and follow up behind them, and let none of you look back, and proceed as commanded.” (Quran, 15:65)
And We informed him of Our decree: the last remnant of these will be uprooted by early morning. (Quran, 15:66)
And the people of the town came joyfully. (Quran, 15:67)
He said, “These are my guests, so do not embarrass me.” (Quran, 15:68)
“And fear Allah, and do not disgrace me.” (Quran, 15:69)
They said, “Did we not forbid you from strangers?” (Quran, 15:70)
He said, “These are my daughters, if you must.” (Quran, 15:71)
By your life, they were blundering in their drunkenness. (Quran, 15:72)
So the Blast struck them at sunrise. (Quran, 15:73)
And We turned it upside down, and rained down upon them stones of baked clay. (Quran, 15:74)
Surely in that are lessons for those who read signs. (Quran, 15:75)
And it is on an existing road. (Quran, 15:76)
Surely in that is a sign for the believers. (Quran, 15:77)
The people of the Woods were also wrongdoers. (Quran, 15:78)
So We took revenge upon them. Both are clearly documented. (Quran, 15:79)
The people of the Rock also rejected the messengers. (Quran, 15:80)
We gave them Our revelations, but they turned away from them. (Quran, 15:81)
They used to carve homes in the mountains, feeling secure. (Quran, 15:82)
But the Blast struck them in the morning. (Quran, 15:83)
All they had acquired was of no avail to them. (Quran, 15:84)
We did not create the heavens and the earth, and what lies between them, except with truth. The Hour is coming, so forgive with gracious forgiveness. (Quran, 15:85)
Your Lord is the All-Knowing Creator. (Quran, 15:86)
We have given you seven of the pairs, and the Grand Quran. (Quran, 15:87)
Do not extend your eyes towards what We have bestowed on some couples of them to enjoy, and do not grieve over them, and lower your wing to the believers. (Quran, 15:88)
And say, “I am the clear warner.” (Quran, 15:89)
Just as We sent down to the separatists. (Quran, 15:90)
Those who made the Quran obsolete. (Quran, 15:91)
By your Lord, we will question them all. (Quran, 15:92)
About what they used to do. (Quran, 15:93)
So proclaim openly what you are commanded, and turn away from the polytheists. (Quran, 15:94)
We are enough for you against the mockers. (Quran, 15:95)
Those who set up another god with Allah. They will come to know. (Quran, 15:96)
We are aware that your heart is strained by what they say. (Quran, 15:97)
So glorify the praise of your Lord, and be among those who bow down. (Quran, 15:98)
And worship your Lord in order to attain certainty. (Quran, 15:99)
The command of Allah has come, so do not rush it. Glory be to Him; exalted above what they associate. (Quran, 16:1)
He sends down the angels with the Spirit by His command, upon whom He wills of His servants: “Give warning that there is no god but Me, and fear Me.” (Quran, 16:2)
He created the heavens and the earth with justice. He is exalted above the associations they attribute. (Quran, 16:3)
He created the human being from a drop of fluid, yet he becomes an open adversary. (Quran, 16:4)
And the livestock—He created them for you. In them are warmth and benefits for you, and of them you eat. (Quran, 16:5)
And there is beauty in them for you, when you bring them home, and when you drive them to pasture. (Quran, 16:6)
And they carry your loads to territory you could not have reached without great hardship. Your Lord is Clement and Merciful. (Quran, 16:7)
And the horses, and the mules, and the donkeys—for you to ride, and for luxury. And He creates what you do not know. (Quran, 16:8)
It is for Allah to point out the paths, but some of them are flawed. Had He willed, He could have guided you all. (Quran, 16:9)
It is He Who sends down for you from the sky water. From it is drink, and with it grows vegetation for grazing. (Quran, 16:10)
And He produces for you grains with it, and olives, and date-palms, and grapes, and all kinds of fruits. Surely in that is a sign for people who think. (Quran, 16:11)
And He regulated for you the night and the day; and the sun, and the moon, and the stars are disposed by His command. Surely in that are signs for people who ponder. (Quran, 16:12)
And whatsoever He created for you on earth is of diverse colors. Surely in that is a sign for people who are mindful. (Quran, 16:13)
And it is He who made the sea to serve you, that you may eat from it tender meat, and extract from it ornaments that you wear. And you see the ships plowing through it, as you seek His bounties, so that you may give thanks. (Quran, 16:14)
And he cast mountains on the earth, lest it shifts with you; and rivers, and roads, so that you may be guided. (Quran, 16:15)
And landmarks. And by the stars they guide themselves. (Quran, 16:16)
Is He who creates like him who does not create? Will you not take a lesson? (Quran, 16:17)
And if you tried to enumerate the favors of Allah, you will not be able to count them. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 16:18)
And Allah knows what you hide and what you disclose. (Quran, 16:19)
Those they invoke besides Allah create nothing, but are themselves created. (Quran, 16:20)
They are dead, not alive; and they do not know when they will be resurrected. (Quran, 16:21)
Your Allah is one Allah. As for those who do not believe in the Hereafter, their hearts are in denial, and they are arrogant. (Quran, 16:22)
Without a doubt, Allah knows what they conceal and what they reveal. He does not like the arrogant. (Quran, 16:23)
And when it is said to them, “What has your Lord sent down?” They say, “Legends of the ancients.” (Quran, 16:24)
So let them carry their loads complete on the Day of Resurrection, and some of the loads of those they misguided without knowledge. Evil is what they carry. (Quran, 16:25)
Those before them also schemed, but Allah took their structures from the foundations, and the roof caved in on them. The punishment came at them from where they did not perceive. (Quran, 16:26)
Then, on the Day of Resurrection, He will disgrace them, and say, “Where are My associates for whose sake you used to dispute?” Those who were given knowledge will say, “Today shame and misery are upon the disbelievers.” (Quran, 16:27)
Those wronging their souls while the angels are taking them away—they will propose peace: “We did no wrong.” Yes you did. Allah is aware of what you used to do.” (Quran, 16:28)
Enter the gates of Hell, to dwell therein forever. Miserable is the residence of the arrogant. (Quran, 16:29)
And it will be said to those who maintained piety, “What has your Lord revealed?” They will say, “Goodness.” To those who do good in this world is goodness, and the Home of the Hereafter is even better. How wonderful is the residence of the pious. (Quran, 16:30)
The Gardens of Perpetuity, which they will enter, beneath which rivers flow, where they will have whatever they desire. Thus Allah rewards the pious. (Quran, 16:31)
Those who are in a wholesome state when the angels take them—will say, “Peace be upon you; enter Paradise, for what you used to do.” (Quran, 16:32)
Are they but waiting for the angels to come to them, or for the command of your Lord to arrive? Those before them did likewise. Allah did not wrong them, but they used to wrong their own souls. (Quran, 16:33)
So the evils of their deeds assailed them, and what they used to ridicule engulfed them. (Quran, 16:34)
The idolaters say, “Had Allah willed, we would not have worshiped anything besides Him, neither us, nor our ancestors, nor would we have prohibited anything besides His prohibitions.” Those before them did likewise. Are the messengers responsible for anything but clear communication? (Quran, 16:35)
To every community We sent a messenger: “Worship Allah, and avoid idolatry.” Some of them Allah guided, while others deserved misguidance. So travel through the earth, and see what the fate of the deniers was. (Quran, 16:36)
Even though you may be concerned about their guidance, Allah does not guide those who misguide. And they will have no saviors. (Quran, 16:37)
And they swear by Allah with their most solemn oaths, “Allah will not resurrect anyone who dies.” Yes indeed, it is a promise binding on Him, but most people do not know. (Quran, 16:38)
To clarify for them what they differed about, and for the faithless to know that they were liars. (Quran, 16:39)
When We intend for something to happen, We say to it, “Be,” and it becomes. (Quran, 16:40)
Those who emigrate for Allah’s sake after being persecuted, We will settle them in a good place in this world; but the reward of the Hereafter is greater, if they only knew. (Quran, 16:41)
Those who endure patiently, and in their Lord they put their trust. (Quran, 16:42)
We did not send before you except men whom We inspired. So ask the people of knowledge, if you do not know. (Quran, 16:43)
With the clarifications and the scriptures. And We revealed to you the Reminder, that you may clarify to the people what was revealed to them, and that they may reflect. (Quran, 16:44)
Do those who scheme evils feel secure that Allah will not cause the earth to cave in with them, or that the punishment will not come upon them from where they do not perceive? (Quran, 16:45)
Or that He will not seize them during their activities? And they will not be able to prevent it. (Quran, 16:46)
Or that He will not seize them while in dread? Your Lord is Gentle and Merciful. (Quran, 16:47)
Have they not observed what Allah has created? Their shadows revolve from the right and the left, bowing to Allah as they shrink away. (Quran, 16:48)
To Allah bows down everything in the heavens and everything on earth—every living creature, and the angels, and without being proud. (Quran, 16:49)
They fear their Lord above them, and they do what they are commanded. (Quran, 16:50)
Allah has said: “Do not take two gods; He is only One Allah; so fear only Me.” (Quran, 16:51)
To Him belongs everything in the heavens and the earth; and to Him obedience is due always. Do you, then, fear anyone other than Allah? (Quran, 16:52)
Whatever blessing you have is from Allah. And when harm touches you, it is to Him that you groan. (Quran, 16:53)
But when He lifts the harm from you, some of you associate others with their Lord. (Quran, 16:54)
To show ingratitude for what We have given them. Enjoy yourselves. You will soon know. (Quran, 16:55)
And they allocate, to something they do not know, a share of what We have provided for them. By Allah, you will be questioned about what you have been inventing. (Quran, 16:56)
And they attribute to Allah daughters—exalted is He—and for themselves what they desire. (Quran, 16:57)
And when one of them is given news of a female infant, his face darkens, and he chokes with grief. (Quran, 16:58)
He hides from the people because of the bad news given to him. Shall he keep it in humiliation, or bury it in the dust? Evil is the decision they make. (Quran, 16:59)
Those who do not believe in the Hereafter set a bad example, while Allah sets the Highest Example. He is the Mighty, the Wise. (Quran, 16:60)
If Allah were to hold mankind for their injustices, He would not leave upon it a single creature, but He postpones them until an appointed time. Then, when their time arrives, they will not delay it by one hour, nor will they advance it. (Quran, 16:61)
And they attribute to Allah what they themselves dislike, while their tongues utter the lie that theirs is the goodness. Without a doubt, for them is the Fire, and they will be neglected. (Quran, 16:62)
By Allah, We sent messengers to communities before you, but Satan made their deeds appear alluring to them. He is their master today, and they will have a painful punishment. (Quran, 16:63)
We revealed to you the Scripture only to clarify for them what they differ about, and guidance and mercy for people who believe. (Quran, 16:64)
Allah sends down water from the sky, with which He revives the earth after its death. In this is a sign for people who listen. (Quran, 16:65)
And there is a lesson for you in cattle: We give you a drink from their bellies, from between waste and blood, pure milk, refreshing to the drinkers. (Quran, 16:66)
And from the fruits of date-palms and grapevines, you derive sugar and wholesome food. In this is a sign for people who understand. (Quran, 16:67)
And your Lord inspired the bee: “Set up hives in the mountains, and in the trees, and in what they construct.” (Quran, 16:68)
Then eat of all the fruits, and go along the pathways of your Lord, with precision. From their bellies emerges a fluid of diverse colors, containing healing for the people. Surely in this is a sign for people who reflect. (Quran, 16:69)
Allah created you; then He takes you away. Some of you will be brought back to the worst age, so that he will no longer know anything, after having acquired knowledge. Allah is Omniscient and Omnipotent. (Quran, 16:70)
Allah has favored some of you over others in livelihood. Those who are favored would not give their properties to their servants, to the extent of making them partners in it. Will they then renounce Allah’s blessings? (Quran, 16:71)
Allah has given you mates from among yourselves; and has produced for you, from your mates, children and grandchildren; and has provided you with good things. Will they then believe in falsehood, and refuse Allah’s favors? (Quran, 16:72)
And yet they serve besides Allah what possesses no provisions for them in the heavens, nor on earth, nor are they capable. (Quran, 16:73)
So do not cite the examples for Allah. Allah knows, and you do not know. (Quran, 16:74)
Allah cites the example of a bonded slave, who has no power over anything; and someone to whom We have given plentiful provision, from which he gives secretly and openly. Are they equal in comparison? All praise belongs to Allah, but most of them do not know. (Quran, 16:75)
And Allah cites the example of two men: one of them dumb, unable to do anything, and is a burden on his master; whichever way he directs him, he achieves nothing good. Is he equal to him who commands justice, and is on a straight path? (Quran, 16:76)
To Allah belongs the unseen of the heavens and the earth. The coming of the Hour is only as the twinkling of the eye, or even nearer. Allah has power over everything. (Quran, 16:77)
Allah brought you out of your mothers’ wombs, not knowing anything; and He gave you the hearing, and the eyesight, and the brains; that you may give thanks. (Quran, 16:78)
Have they not seen the birds, flying in the midst of the sky? None sustains them except Allah. In this are signs for people who believe. (Quran, 16:79)
And Allah has given you in your homes habitats for you, and has provided for you out of the hides of livestock portable homes for you, so you can use them when you travel, and when you camp; and from their wool, and fur, and hair, furnishings and comfort for a while. (Quran, 16:80)
And Allah has made for you shade out of what He has created, and has given you resorts in the mountains, and has given you garments to protect you from the heat, and garments to protect you from your violence. Thus He completes His blessings upon you, so that you may submit. (Quran, 16:81)
But if they turn away, your only duty is clear communication. (Quran, 16:82)
They recognize Allah’s blessing, but then deny it, as most of them are ungrateful. (Quran, 16:83)
On the Day when We raise up a witness from every community—those who disbelieved will not be permitted, nor will they be excused. (Quran, 16:84)
When those who did wrong see the punishment, it will not be lightened for them, nor will they be reprieved. (Quran, 16:85)
And when the idolaters see their associates, they will say, “Our Lord, these are our associates whom we used to invoke besides You.” They will strike back at them with the saying, “Surely you are liars.” (Quran, 16:86)
On that Day they will offer their submission to Allah, and what they had invented will abandon them. (Quran, 16:87)
Those who disbelieve and obstruct from Allah’s path—We will add punishment to their punishment, on account of the mischief they used to make. (Quran, 16:88)
On the Day when We raise in every community a witness against them, from among them, and bring you as a witness against these. We have revealed to you the Book, as an explanation of all things, and guidance, and mercy and good news for those who submit. (Quran, 16:89)
Allah commands justice, and goodness, and generosity towards relatives. And He forbids immorality, and injustice, and oppression. He advises you, so that you may take heed. (Quran, 16:90)
Fulfill Allah’s covenant when you make a covenant, and do not break your oaths after ratifying them. You have made Allah your guarantor, and Allah knows what you do. (Quran, 16:91)
And do not be like her who unravels her yarn, breaking it into pieces, after she has spun it strongly. Nor use your oaths as means of deception among you, because one community is more prosperous than another. Allah is testing you thereby. On the Day of Resurrection, He will make clear to you everything you had disputed about. (Quran, 16:92)
Had Allah willed, He would have made you one congregation, but He leaves astray whom He wills, and He guides whom He wills. And you will surely be questioned about what you used to do. (Quran, 16:93)
And do not use your oaths to deceive one another, so that a foot may not slip after being firm, and you taste misery because you hindered from Allah’s path, and incur a terrible torment. (Quran, 16:94)
And do not exchange Allah’s covenant for a small price. What is with Allah is better for you, if you only knew. (Quran, 16:95)
What you have runs out, but what is with Allah remains. We will reward those who are patient according to the best of their deeds. (Quran, 16:96)
Whoever works righteousness, whether male or female, while being a believer, We will grant him a good life—and We will reward them according to the best of what they used to do. (Quran, 16:97)
When you read the Quran, seek refuge with Allah from Satan the outcast. (Quran, 16:98)
He has no authority over those who believe and trust in their Lord. (Quran, 16:99)
His authority is only over those who follow him, and those who associate others with Him. (Quran, 16:100)
When We substitute a verse in place of another verse—and Allah knows best what He reveals—they say, “You are an impostor.” But most of them do not know. (Quran, 16:101)
Say, “The Holy Spirit has brought it down from your Lord, truthfully, in order to stabilize those who believe, and as guidance and good news for those who submit.” (Quran, 16:102)
We are well aware that they say, “It is a human being who is teaching him.” But the tongue of him they allude to is foreign, while this is a clear Arabic tongue. (Quran, 16:103)
Those who do not believe in Allah’s revelations—Allah will not guide them, and for them is a painful punishment. (Quran, 16:104)
It is those who do not believe in Allah’s revelations who fabricate falsehood. These are the liars. (Quran, 16:105)
Whoever renounces faith in Allah after having believed—except for someone who is compelled, while his heart rests securely in faith—but whoever willingly opens up his heart to disbelief—upon them falls wrath from Allah, and for them is a tremendous torment. (Quran, 16:106)
That is because they have preferred the worldly life to the Hereafter, and because Allah does not guide the people who refuse. (Quran, 16:107)
It is they whom Allah has sealed their hearts, and their hearing, and their sight. It is they who are the heedless. (Quran, 16:108)
There is no doubt that in the Hereafter they will be the losers. (Quran, 16:109)
But then your Lord—for those who emigrated after being persecuted, then struggled and persevered—your Lord thereafter is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 16:110)
On the Day when every soul will come pleading for itself, and every soul will be paid in full for what it has done, and they will not be wronged. (Quran, 16:111)
And Allah cites the example of a town that was secure and peaceful, with its livelihood coming to it abundantly from every direction. But then it turned unappreciative of Allah’s blessings, so Allah made it taste the robe of hunger and fear, because of what they used to craft. (Quran, 16:112)
A messenger from among them had come to them, but they denounced him, so the punishment seized them in the midst of their wrongdoing. (Quran, 16:113)
Eat of the lawful and good things Allah has provided for you, and be thankful for Allah’s blessings, if it is Him that you serve. (Quran, 16:114)
He has forbidden you carrion, and blood, and the flesh of swine, and anything consecrated to other than Allah. But if anyone is compelled by necessity, without being deliberate or malicious, then Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 16:115)
And do not say of falsehood asserted by your tongues, “This is lawful, and this is unlawful,” in order to invent lies and attribute them to Allah. Those who invent lies and attribute them to Allah will not succeed. (Quran, 16:116)
A brief enjoyment—then they will have a painful punishment. (Quran, 16:117)
For those who are Jews, We have prohibited what We related to you before. We did not wrong them, but they used to wrong their own selves. (Quran, 16:118)
But towards those who do wrongs in ignorance, and then repent afterwards and reform, your Lord thereafter is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 16:119)
Abraham was an exemplary leader, devoted to Allah, a monotheist, and was not of the polytheists. (Quran, 16:120)
Thankful for His blessings. He chose him, and guided him to a straight path. (Quran, 16:121)
And We gave him goodness in this world, and in the Hereafter he will be among the righteous. (Quran, 16:122)
Then We inspired you: “Follow the religion of Abraham, the Monotheist. He was not an idol-worshiper.” (Quran, 16:123)
The Sabbath was decreed only for those who differed about it. Your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection regarding their differences. (Quran, 16:124)
Invite to the way of your Lord with wisdom and good advice, and debate with them in the most dignified manner. Your Lord is aware of those who stray from His path, and He is aware of those who are guided. (Quran, 16:125)
If you were to retaliate, retaliate to the same degree as the injury done to you. But if you resort to patience—it is better for the patient. (Quran, 16:126)
So be patient. Your patience is solely from Allah. And do not grieve over them, and do not be stressed by their schemes. (Quran, 16:127)
Allah is with those who are righteous and those who are virtuous. (Quran, 16:128)
Glory to Him who journeyed His servant by night, from the Sacred Mosque, to the Farthest Mosque, whose precincts We have blessed, in order to show him of Our wonders. He is the Listener, the Beholder. (Quran, 17:1)
And We gave Moses the Scripture, and made it a guide for the Children of Israel: Take none for protector other than Me. (Quran, 17:2)
The descendants of those We carried with Noah. He was an appreciative servant. (Quran, 17:3)
And We conveyed to the Children of Israel in the Scripture: You will commit evil on earth twice, and you will rise to a great height. (Quran, 17:4)
When the first of the two promises came true, We sent against you servants of Ours, possessing great might, and they ransacked your homes. It was a promise fulfilled. (Quran, 17:5)
Then We gave you back your turn against them, and supplied you with wealth and children, and made you more numerous. (Quran, 17:6)
If you work righteousness, you work righteousness for yourselves; and if you commit evil, you do so against yourselves. Then, when the second promise comes true, they will make your faces filled with sorrow, and enter the Temple as they entered it the first time, and utterly destroy all that falls into their power. (Quran, 17:7)
Perhaps your Lord will have mercy on you. But if you revert, We will revert. We have made Hell a prison for the disbelievers. (Quran, 17:8)
This Quran guides to what is most upright; and it gives good news to the believers who do good deeds, that they will have a great reward. (Quran, 17:9)
And those who do not believe in the Hereafter—We have prepared for them a painful punishment. (Quran, 17:10)
The human being prays for evil as he prays for good. The human being is very hasty. (Quran, 17:11)
We have made the night and the day two wonders. We erased the wonder of the night, and made the wonder of the day revealing, that you may seek bounty from your Lord, and know the number of years, and the calculation. We have explained all things in detail. (Quran, 17:12)
For every person We have attached his fate to his neck. And on the Day of Resurrection, We will bring out for him a book which he will find spread open. (Quran, 17:13)
“Read your book; today there will be none but yourself to call you to account.” (Quran, 17:14)
Whoever is guided—is guided for his own good. And whoever goes astray—goes astray to his detriment. No burdened soul carries the burdens of another, nor do We ever punish until We have sent a messenger. (Quran, 17:15)
When We decide to destroy a town, We command its affluent ones, they transgress in it, so the word becomes justified against it, and We destroy it completely. (Quran, 17:16)
How many generations have We destroyed after Noah? Your Lord is sufficient as Knower and Beholder of the sins of his servants. (Quran, 17:17)
Whoever desires the fleeting life, We expedite for him what We decide to give him, to whomever We desire. Then We consign him to Hell, where he will roast, condemned and defeated. (Quran, 17:18)
But whoever desires the Hereafter, and pursues it as it should be pursued, while he is a believer; these—their effort will be appreciated. (Quran, 17:19)
To all—these and those—We extend from the gifts of your Lord. The gifts of your Lord are not restricted. (Quran, 17:20)
See how We have favored some of them over others; yet the Hereafter is greater in ranks, and greater in favors. (Quran, 17:21)
Do not set up another god with Allah, lest you become condemned and damned. (Quran, 17:22)
Your Lord has commanded that you worship none but Him, and that you be good to your parents. If either of them or both of them reach old age with you, do not say to them a word of disrespect, nor scold them, but say to them kind words. (Quran, 17:23)
And lower to them the wing of humility, out of mercy, and say, “My Lord, have mercy on them, as they raised me when I was a child.” (Quran, 17:24)
Your Lord knows best what is in your minds. If you are righteous—He is Forgiving to the obedient. (Quran, 17:25)
And give the relative his rights, and the poor, and the wayfarer, and do not squander wastefully. (Quran, 17:26)
The extravagant are brethren of the devils, and the devil is ever ungrateful to his Lord. (Quran, 17:27)
But if you turn away from them, seeking mercy from your Lord which you hope for, then say to them words of comfort. (Quran, 17:28)
And do not keep your hand tied to your neck, nor spread it out fully, lest you end up liable and regretful. (Quran, 17:29)
Your Lord expands the provision for whomever He wills, and restricts it. He is fully Informed, Observant of His servants. (Quran, 17:30)
And do not kill your children for fear of poverty. We provide for them, and for you. Killing them is a grave sin. (Quran, 17:31)
And do not come near adultery. It is immoral, and an evil way. (Quran, 17:32)
And do not kill the soul which Allah has made sacred, except in the course of justice. If someone is killed unjustly, We have given his next of kin certain authority. But he should not be excessive in killing, for he will be supported. (Quran, 17:33)
And do not go near the orphan’s property, except with the best of intentions, until he has reached his maturity. And honor your pledge, because the pledge involves responsibility. (Quran, 17:34)
And give full measure when you measure, and weigh with accurate scales. That is fair, and the best determination. (Quran, 17:35)
And do not occupy yourself with what you have no knowledge of. The hearing, and the sight, and the brains—all these will be questioned. (Quran, 17:36)
And do not walk proudly on earth. You can neither pierce the earth, nor can you match the mountains in height. (Quran, 17:37)
The evil of all these is disliked by your Lord. (Quran, 17:38)
That is some of the wisdom your Lord has revealed to you. Do not set up with Allah another god, or else you will be thrown in Hell, rebuked and banished. (Quran, 17:39)
Has your Lord favored you with sons, while choosing for Himself daughters from among the angels? You are indeed saying a terrible thing. (Quran, 17:40)
We have explained in this Quran in various ways, that they may remember, but it only adds to their rebellion. (Quran, 17:41)
Say, “If there were other gods with Him, as they say, they would have sought a way to the Lord of the Throne.” (Quran, 17:42)
Be He glorified. He is exalted, far above what they say. (Quran, 17:43)
Praising Him are the seven heavens, and the earth, and everyone in them. There is not a thing that does not glorify Him with praise, but you do not understand their praises. He is indeed Forbearing and Forgiving. (Quran, 17:44)
When you read the Quran, We place between you and those who do not believe in the Hereafter an invisible barrier. (Quran, 17:45)
And We drape veils over their hearts, preventing them from understanding it, and heaviness in their ears. And when you mention your Lord alone in the Quran, they turn their backs in aversion. (Quran, 17:46)
We know well what they listen to, when they listen to you, as they conspire, when the wrongdoers say, “You only follow a man bewitched.” (Quran, 17:47)
Note what they compared you to. They are lost, and unable to find a way. (Quran, 17:48)
And they say, “When we have become bones and fragments, shall we really be resurrected as a new creation?” (Quran, 17:49)
Say, “Even if you become rocks or iron. (Quran, 17:50)
Or some substance, which, in your minds, is even harder.” Then they will say, “Who will restore us?” Say, “The One who originated you the first time.” Then they will nod their heads at you, and say, “When will it be?” Say, “Perhaps it will be soon.” (Quran, 17:51)
On the Day when He calls you, you will respond with His praise, and you will realize that you stayed only a little. (Quran, 17:52)
Tell My servants to say what is best. Satan sows discord among them. Satan is to man an open enemy. (Quran, 17:53)
Your Lord knows you best. If He wills, He will have mercy on you; and if He wills, He will punish you. We did not send you as their advocate. (Quran, 17:54)
Your Lord knows well everyone in the heavens and the earth. We have given some prophets advantage over others; and to David We gave the Psalms. (Quran, 17:55)
Say, “Call upon those you claim besides Him. They have no power to relieve your adversity, nor can they change it.” (Quran, 17:56)
Those they call upon are themselves seeking means of access to their Lord, vying to be nearer, and hoping for His mercy, and fearing His punishment. The punishment of your Lord is to be dreaded. (Quran, 17:57)
There is no city but We will destroy before the Day of Resurrection, or punish it with a severe punishment. This is inscribed in the Book. (Quran, 17:58)
Nothing prevents Us from sending miraculous signs, except that the ancients called them lies. We gave Thamood the she-camel, a visible sign, but they mistreated her. We do not send the signs except to instill reverence. (Quran, 17:59)
We said to you that your Lord encompasses humanity. We did not make the vision We showed you, except as a test for the people, and the tree cursed in the Quran. We frighten them, but that only increases their defiance. (Quran, 17:60)
When We said to the angels, “Bow down before Adam,” they bowed down, except for Satan. He said, “Shall I bow down before someone You created from mud?” (Quran, 17:61)
He said, “Do You see this one whom You have honored more than me? If You reprieve me until the Day of Resurrection, I will bring his descendants under my sway, except for a few.” (Quran, 17:62)
He said, “Begone! Whoever of them follows you—Hell is your reward, an ample reward.” (Quran, 17:63)
“And entice whomever of them you can with your voice, and rally against them your cavalry and your infantry, and share with them in wealth and children, and make promises to them.” But Satan promises them nothing but delusion. (Quran, 17:64)
“As for My devotees, you have no authority over them.” Your Lord is an adequate Guardian. (Quran, 17:65)
Your Lord is He who propels for you the ships at sea, that you may seek of His bounty. He is towards you Most Merciful. (Quran, 17:66)
When harm afflicts you at sea, those you pray to vanish, except for Him. But when He saves you to land, you turn away. The human being is ever thankless. (Quran, 17:67)
Are you confident that He will not cause a track of land to cave in beneath you, or unleash a tornado against you, and then you find no protector? (Quran, 17:68)
Or are you confident that He will not return you to it once again, and unleash a hurricane against you, and drown you for your ingratitude? Then you will find no helper against Us. (Quran, 17:69)
We have honored the Children of Adam, and carried them on land and sea, and provided them with good things, and greatly favored them over many of those We created. (Quran, 17:70)
On the Day when We call every people with their leader. Whoever is given his record in his right hand—these will read their record, and they will not be wronged one bit. (Quran, 17:71)
But whoever is blind in this, he will be blind in the Hereafter, and further astray from the way. (Quran, 17:72)
They almost lured you away from what We have revealed to you, so that you would invent something else in Our name. In that case, they would have taken you for a friend. (Quran, 17:73)
Had We not given you stability, you might have inclined towards them a little. (Quran, 17:74)
Then We would have made you taste double in life, and double at death; then you would have found for yourself no helper against Us. (Quran, 17:75)
They almost provoked you, to expel you from the land. In that case, they would not have lasted after you, except briefly. (Quran, 17:76)
The tradition of the messengers We sent before you—you will find no change in Our rules. (Quran, 17:77)
Perform the prayer at the decline of the sun, until the darkness of the night; and the Quran at dawn. The Quran at dawn is witnessed. (Quran, 17:78)
And keep vigil with it during parts of the night, as an extra prayer. Perhaps your Lord will raise you to a laudable position. (Quran, 17:79)
And say, “My Lord, lead me in through an entry of truth, and lead me out through an exit of truth, and grant me from You a supporting power.” (Quran, 17:80)
And say, “The truth has come, and falsehood has withered away; for falsehood is bound to wither away.” (Quran, 17:81)
We send down in the Quran healing and mercy for the believers, but it increases the wrongdoers only in loss. (Quran, 17:82)
When We bless the human being, he turns away and distances himself. But when adversity touches him, he is in despair. (Quran, 17:83)
Say, “Each does according to his disposition. Your Lord knows best who is better guided in the way.” (Quran, 17:84)
And they ask you about the Spirit. Say, “The Spirit belongs to the domain of my Lord; and you were given only little knowledge.” (Quran, 17:85)
If We willed, We could take away what We revealed to you. Then you will find for yourself no protecting guardian against Us. (Quran, 17:86)
Except through a mercy from your Lord. His favors upon you have been great. (Quran, 17:87)
Say, “If mankind and jinn came together to produce the like of this Quran, they could never produce the like of it, even if they backed up one another.” (Quran, 17:88)
We have displayed for mankind in this Quran every kind of similitude, but most people insist on denying the truth. (Quran, 17:89)
And they said, “We will not believe in you unless you make a spring burst from the ground for us. (Quran, 17:90)
Or you have a garden of palms and vines; then cause rivers to gush pouring through them. (Quran, 17:91)
Or make the sky fall on us in pieces, as you claim, or bring Allah and the angels before us. (Quran, 17:92)
Or you possess a house of gold. Or you ascend into the sky. Even then, we will not believe in your ascension, unless you bring down for us a book that we can read.” Say, “Glory be to my Lord. Am I anything but a human messenger?” (Quran, 17:93)
Nothing prevented the people from believing, when guidance has come to them, except that they said, “Did Allah send a human messenger?” (Quran, 17:94)
Say, “If there were angels on earth, walking around in peace, We would have sent down to them from heaven an angel messenger.” (Quran, 17:95)
Say, “Allah is enough witness between you and me. He is fully aware of His servants, and He sees them well.” (Quran, 17:96)
Whomever Allah guides is the guided one. And whomever He leaves astray—for them you will find no protectors apart from Him. And We will gather them on the Day of Resurrection, on their faces, blind, dumb, and deaf. Their abode is Hell; whenever it abates, We intensify the blaze for them. (Quran, 17:97)
This is their repayment for having blasphemed against Our revelations, and having said, “Shall we, when we have become bones and fragments, be resurrected as a new creation?” (Quran, 17:98)
Do they not consider that Allah, Who created the heavens and the earth, is Able to create the likes of them? He has assigned for them a term, in which there is no doubt. But the wrongdoers persist in denying the truth. (Quran, 17:99)
Say, “If you possessed the treasuries of my Lord’s mercy, you would have withheld them for fear of spending.” The human being has always been stingy. (Quran, 17:100)
We gave Moses nine clear signs—ask the Children of Israel. When he went to them, Pharaoh said to him, “I think that you, Moses, are bewitched.” (Quran, 17:101)
He said, “You know that none sent these down except the Lord of the heavens and the earth—eye openers; and I think that you, Pharaoh, are doomed.” (Quran, 17:102)
He resolved to scare them off the land, but We drowned him, and those with him, altogether. (Quran, 17:103)
After him, We said to the Children of Israel, “Inhabit the land, and when the promise of the Hereafter arrives, We will bring you all together.” (Quran, 17:104)
With the truth We sent it down, and with the truth it descended. We sent you only as a bearer of good news and a warner. (Quran, 17:105)
A Quran which We unfolded gradually, that you may recite to the people over time. And We revealed it in stages. (Quran, 17:106)
Say, “Believe in it, or do not believe.” Those who were given knowledge before it, when it is recited to them, they fall to their chins, prostrating. (Quran, 17:107)
And they say, “Glory to our Lord. The promise of our Lord is fulfilled.” (Quran, 17:108)
And they fall to their chins, weeping, and it adds to their humility. (Quran, 17:109)
Say, “Call Him Allah, or call Him the Most Merciful. Whichever name you use, to Him belong the Best Names.” And be neither loud in your prayer, nor silent in it, but follow a course in between. (Quran, 17:110)
And say, “Praise be to Allah, who has not begotten a son, nor has He a partner in sovereignty, nor has He an ally out of weakness, and glorify Him constantly.” (Quran, 17:111)
Praise be to Allah, who revealed the Book to His servant, and allowed in it no distortion. (Quran, 18:1)
Valuable—to warn of severe punishment from Himself; and to deliver good news to the believers who do righteous deeds, that they will have an excellent reward. (Quran, 18:2)
In which they will abide forever. (Quran, 18:3)
And to warn those who say, “Allah has begotten a son.” (Quran, 18:4)
They have no knowledge of this, nor did their forefathers. Grave is the word that comes out of their mouths. They say nothing but a lie. (Quran, 18:5)
Perhaps you may destroy yourself with grief, chasing after them, if they do not believe in this information. (Quran, 18:6)
We made what is upon the earth an ornament for it, to test them as to which of them is best in conduct. (Quran, 18:7)
And We will turn what is on it into barren waste. (Quran, 18:8)
Did you know that the People of the Cave and the Inscription were of Our wondrous signs? (Quran, 18:9)
When the youths took shelter in the cave, they said, “Our Lord, give us mercy from Yourself, and bless our affair with guidance.” (Quran, 18:10)
Then We sealed their ears in the cave for a number of years. (Quran, 18:11)
Then We awakened them to know which of the two groups could better calculate the length of their stay. (Quran, 18:12)
We relate to you their story in truth. They were youths who believed in their Lord, and We increased them in guidance. (Quran, 18:13)
And We strengthened their hearts, when they stood up and said, “Our Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth; we will not call on any god besides Him, for then we would have spoken an outrage.” (Quran, 18:14)
“These people, our people, have taken to themselves gods other than Him. Why do they not bring a clear proof concerning them? Who, then, does greater wrong than he who invents lies and attributes them to Allah?” (Quran, 18:15)
“Now that you have withdrawn from them, and from what they worship besides Allah, take shelter in the cave. And your Lord will unfold His mercy for you, and will set your affair towards ease.” (Quran, 18:16)
You would have seen the sun, when it rose, veering away from their cave towards the right, and when it sets, moving away from them to the left, as they lay in the midst of the cave. That was one of Allah’s wonders. He whom Allah guides is truly guided; but he whom He misguides, for him you will find no directing friend. (Quran, 18:17)
You would think them awake, although they were asleep. And We turned them over to the right, and to the left, with their dog stretching its paws across the threshold. Had you looked at them, you would have turned away from them in flight, and been filled with fear of them. (Quran, 18:18)
Even so, We awakened them, so that they may ask one another. A speaker among them said, “How long have you stayed?” They said, “We have stayed a day, or part of a day.” They said, “Your Lord knows best how long you have stayed.” “Send one of you to the city, with this money of yours, and let him see which food is most suitable, and let him bring you some provision thereof. And let him be gentle, and let no one become aware of you.” (Quran, 18:19)
“If they discover you, they will stone you, or force you back into their religion; then you will never be saved.” (Quran, 18:20)
So it was, that We caused them to be discovered, that they would know that the promise of Allah is true, and that of the Hour there is no doubt. As they were disputing their case among themselves, they said, “Build over them a building.” Their Lord knows best about them. Those who prevailed over their case said, “We will set up over them a place of worship.” (Quran, 18:21)
They will say, “Three, and their fourth being their dog.” And they will say, “Five, and their sixth being their dog,” guessing at the unknown.
