And they will say, “Seven, and their eighth being their dog.” Say, “My Lord knows best their number.” None knows them except a few. So do not argue concerning them except with an obvious argument, and do not consult any of them about them. (Quran, 18:22)
And never say about anything, “I will do that tomorrow.” (Quran, 18:23)
Without saying, “If Allah wills.” And remember your Lord if you forget, and say, “Perhaps my Lord will guide me to nearer than this in integrity.” (Quran, 18:24)
And they stayed in their cave for three hundred years, adding nine. (Quran, 18:25)
Say, “Allah knows best how long they stayed.” His is the mystery of the heavens and the earth. By Him you see and hear. They have no guardian apart from Him, and He shares His Sovereignty with no one. (Quran, 18:26)
And recite what was revealed to you from the Book of your Lord. There is no changing His words, and you will find no refuge except in Him. (Quran, 18:27)
And content yourself with those who pray to their Lord morning and evening, desiring His Presence. And do not turn your eyes away from them, desiring the glitter of this world. And do not obey him whose heart We have made heedless of Our remembrance—so he follows his own desires—and his priorities are confused. (Quran, 18:28)
And say, “The truth is from your Lord. Whoever wills—let him believe. And whoever wills—let him disbelieve”. We have prepared for the unjust a Fire, whose curtains will hem them in. And when they cry for relief, they will be relieved with water like molten brass, which scalds the faces. What a miserable drink, and what a terrible place. (Quran, 18:29)
As for those who believe and lead a righteous life—We will not waste the reward of those who work righteousness. (Quran, 18:30)
These will have the Gardens of Eden, beneath which rivers flow. Reclining on comfortable furnishings, they will be adorned with bracelets of gold, and will wear green garments of silk and brocade. What a wonderful reward, and what an excellent resting-place. (Quran, 18:31)
And cite for them the parable of two men. To one of them We gave two gardens of vine, and We surrounded them with palm-trees, and We placed between them crops. (Quran, 18:32)
Both gardens produced their harvest in full, and suffered no loss. And We made a river flow through them. (Quran, 18:33)
And thus he had abundant fruits. He said to his friend, as he conversed with him, “I am wealthier than you, and greater in manpower.” (Quran, 18:34)
And he entered his garden, wronging himself. He said, “I do not think this will ever perish.” (Quran, 18:35)
“And I do not think the Hour is coming. And even if I am returned to my Lord, I will find something better than this in return.” (Quran, 18:36)
His friend said to him, as he conversed with him, “Are you being ungrateful to Him who created you from dust, then from a sperm-drop, then evolved you into a man? (Quran, 18:37)
But as for me, He is Allah, my Lord, and I never associate with my Lord anyone. (Quran, 18:38)
When you entered your garden, why did you not say, “As Allah wills; there is no power except through Allah”? Although you see me inferior to you in wealth and children. (Quran, 18:39)
Perhaps my Lord will give me something better than your garden, and release upon it thunderbolts from the sky, so it becomes barren waste. (Quran, 18:40)
Or its water will sink into the ground, and you will be unable to draw it.” (Quran, 18:41)
And ruin closed in on his crops, and so he began wringing his hands over what he had invested in it, as it lays fallen upon its trellises. And he was saying, “I wish I never associated anyone with my Lord.” (Quran, 18:42)
He had no faction to help him besides Allah, and he was helpless. (Quran, 18:43)
That is because authority belongs to Allah, the True. He is Best in rewarding, and Best in requiting. (Quran, 18:44)
And cite for them the parable of the present life: it is like water that We send down from the sky; the plants of the earth absorb it; but then it becomes debris, scattered by the wind. Allah has absolute power over everything. (Quran, 18:45)
Wealth and children are the adornments of the present life. But the things that last, the virtuous deeds, are better with your Lord for reward, and better for hope. (Quran, 18:46)
On the Day when We set the mountains in motion; and you see the earth emerging; and We gather them together, and leave none of them behind. (Quran, 18:47)
They will be presented before your Lord in a row. “You have come to Us as We created you the first time. Although you claimed We would not set a meeting for you.” (Quran, 18:48)
And the book will be placed, and you will see the sinners fearful of its contents. And they will say, “Woe to us! What is with this book that leaves nothing, small or big, but it has enumerated it?” They will find everything they had done present. Your Lord does not wrong anyone. (Quran, 18:49)
We said to the angels, “Bow down to Adam.” So they bowed down, except for Satan. He was of the jinn, and he defied the command of his Lord. Will you take him and his offspring as lords instead of Me, when they are an enemy to you? Evil is the exchange for the wrongdoers. (Quran, 18:50)
I did not call them to witness the creation of the heavens and the earth, nor their own creation; and I do not take the misleaders for assistants. (Quran, 18:51)
On the Day when He will say, “Call on My partners whom you have claimed.” They will call on them, but they will not answer them. And We will place between them a barrier. (Quran, 18:52)
And the sinners will see the Fire, and will realize that they will tumble into it. They will find no deliverance from it. (Quran, 18:53)
We have elaborated in this Quran for the people every kind of example, but the human being is a most argumentative being. (Quran, 18:54)
What prevented people from accepting faith, when guidance has come to them, and from seeking their Lord’s forgiveness? Unless they are waiting for the precedent of the ancients to befall them, or to have the punishment come upon them face to face. (Quran, 18:55)
We send the messengers only as deliverers of good news and warners. Those who disbelieve argue with false argument, in order to defeat the truth thereby. They take My Verses, and the warnings, for a joke. (Quran, 18:56)
Who does greater wrong than he, who, when reminded of his Lord’s revelations, turns away from them, and forgets what his hands have put forward? We have placed coverings over their hearts, lest they understand it, and heaviness in their ears. And if you call them to guidance, they will not be guided, ever. (Quran, 18:57)
Your Lord is the Forgiver, Possessor of Mercy. Were He to call them to account for what they have earned, He would have hastened the punishment for them. But they have an appointment from which they will find no escape. (Quran, 18:58)
And these towns—We destroyed them when they committed injustices, and We set for their destruction an appointed time. (Quran, 18:59)
Recall when Moses said to his servant, “I will not give up until I reach the junction of the two rivers, even if it takes me years.” (Quran, 18:60)
Then, when they reached the junction between them, they forgot about their fish. It found its way into the river, slipping away. (Quran, 18:61)
When they went further, he said to his servant, “Bring us our lunch; we were exposed in our travel to much fatigue.” (Quran, 18:62)
He said, “Do you remember when we rested by the rock? I forgot about the fish. It was only the devil who made me forget it. And so it found its way to the river, amazingly.” (Quran, 18:63)
He said, “This is what we were seeking.” And so they turned back retracing their steps. (Quran, 18:64)
Then they came upon a servant of Ours, whom We had blessed with mercy from Us, and had taught him knowledge from Our Own. (Quran, 18:65)
Moses said to him, “May I follow you, so that you may teach me some of the guidance you were taught?” (Quran, 18:66)
He said, “You will not be able to endure with me. (Quran, 18:67)
And how will you endure what you have no knowledge of?” (Quran, 18:68)
He said, “You will find me, Allah willing, patient; and I will not disobey you in any order of yours.” (Quran, 18:69)
He said, “If you follow me, do not ask me about anything, until I myself make mention of it to you.” (Quran, 18:70)
So they set out. Until, when they had boarded the boat, he holed it. He said, “Did you hole it, to drown its passengers? You have done something awful.” (Quran, 18:71)
He said, “Did I not tell you that you will not be able to endure with me?” (Quran, 18:72)
He said, “Do not rebuke me for forgetting, and do not make my course difficult for me.” (Quran, 18:73)
Then they set out. Until, when they encountered a boy, he killed him. He said, “Did you kill a pure soul, who killed no one? You have done something terrible.” (Quran, 18:74)
He said, “Did I not tell you that you will not be able to endure with me?” (Quran, 18:75)
He said, “If I ask you about anything after this, then do not keep company with me. You have received excuses from me.” (Quran, 18:76)
So they set out. Until, when they reached the people of a town, they asked them for food, but they refused to offer them hospitality. There they found a wall about to collapse, and he repaired it. He said, “If you wanted, you could have obtained a payment for it.” (Quran, 18:77)
He said, “This is the parting between you and me. I will tell you the interpretation of what you were unable to endure. (Quran, 18:78)
As for the boat, it belonged to paupers working at sea. I wanted to damage it because there was a king coming after them seizing every boat by force. (Quran, 18:79)
As for the boy, his parents were believers, and we feared he would overwhelm them with oppression and disbelief. (Quran, 18:80)
So we wanted their Lord to replace him with someone better in purity, and closer to mercy. (Quran, 18:81)
And as for the wall, it belonged to two orphaned boys in the city. Beneath it was a treasure that belonged to them. Their father was a righteous man. Your Lord wanted them to reach their maturity, and then extract their treasure—as a mercy from your Lord. I did not do it of my own accord. This is the interpretation of what you were unable to endure.” (Quran, 18:82)
And they ask you about Zul-Qarnain. Say, “I will tell you something about him.” (Quran, 18:83)
We established him on earth, and gave him all kinds of means. (Quran, 18:84)
He pursued a certain course. (Quran, 18:85)
Until, when he reached the setting of the sun, he found it setting in a murky spring, and found a people in its vicinity. We said, “O Zul-Qarnain, you may either inflict a penalty, or else treat them kindly.” (Quran, 18:86)
He said, “As for him who does wrong, we will penalize him, then he will be returned to his Lord, and He will punish him with an unheard-of torment. (Quran, 18:87)
“But as for him who believes and acts righteously, he will have the finest reward, and We will speak to him of Our command with ease.” (Quran, 18:88)
Then he pursued a course. (Quran, 18:89)
Until, when he reached the rising of the sun, he found it rising on a people for whom We had provided no shelter from it. (Quran, 18:90)
And so it was. We had full knowledge of what he had. (Quran, 18:91)
Then he pursued a course. (Quran, 18:92)
Until, when he reached the point separating the two barriers, he found beside them a people who could barely understand what is said. (Quran, 18:93)
They said, “O Zul-Qarnain, the Gog and Magog are spreading chaos in the land. Can we pay you, to build between us and them a wall?” (Quran, 18:94)
He said, “What my Lord has empowered me with is better. But assist me with strength, and I will build between you and them a dam.” (Quran, 18:95)
“Bring me blocks of iron.” So that, when he had leveled up between the two cliffs, he said, “Blow.” And having turned it into a fire, he said, “Bring me tar to pour over it.” (Quran, 18:96)
So they were unable to climb it, and they could not penetrate it. (Quran, 18:97)
He said, “This is a mercy from my Lord. But when the promise of my Lord comes true, He will turn it into rubble, and the promise of my Lord is always true.” (Quran, 18:98)
On that Day, We will leave them surging upon one another. And the Trumpet will be blown, and We will gather them together. (Quran, 18:99)
On that Day, We will present the disbelievers to Hell, all displayed. (Quran, 18:100)
Those whose eyes were screened to My message, and were unable to hear. (Quran, 18:101)
Do those who disbelieve think that they can take My servants for masters instead of Me? We have prepared Hell for the hospitality of the faithless. (Quran, 18:102)
Say, “Shall We inform you of the greatest losers in their works?” (Quran, 18:103)
“Those whose efforts in this world are misguided, while they assume that they are doing well.” (Quran, 18:104)
It is they who rejected the communications of their Lord, and the encounter with Him. So their works are in vain. And on the Day of Resurrection, We will consider them of no weight. (Quran, 18:105)
That is their requital—Hell—on account of their disbelief, and their taking My revelations and My messengers in mockery. (Quran, 18:106)
As for those who believe and do righteous deeds, they will have the Gardens of Paradise for hospitality. (Quran, 18:107)
Abiding therein forever, without desiring any change therefrom. (Quran, 18:108)
Say, “If the ocean were ink for the words of my Lord, the ocean would run out, before the words of my Lord run out,” even if We were to bring the like of it in addition to it. (Quran, 18:109)
Say, “I am only a human being like you, being inspired that your god is One Allah. Whoever hopes to meet his Lord, let him work righteousness, and never associate anyone with the service of his Lord.” (Quran, 18:110)
Kaf, Ha, Ya, Ayn, Saad. (Quran, 19:1)
A mention of the mercy of your Lord towards His servant Zechariah. (Quran, 19:2)
When he called on his Lord, a call in seclusion. (Quran, 19:3)
He said, “My Lord, my bones have become feeble, and my hair is aflame with gray, and never, Lord, have I been disappointed in my prayer to you. (Quran, 19:4)
“And I fear for my dependents after me, and my wife is barren. So grant me, from Yourself, an heir. (Quran, 19:5)
To inherit me, and inherit from the House of Jacob, and make him, my Lord, pleasing.” (Quran, 19:6)
“O Zechariah, We give you good news of a son, whose name is John, a name We have never given before.” (Quran, 19:7)
He said, “My Lord, how can I have a son, when my wife is barren, and I have become decrepit with old age?” (Quran, 19:8)
He said, “It will be so, your Lord says, ‘it is easy for me, and I created you before, when you were nothing.’” (Quran, 19:9)
He said, “My Lord, give me a sign.” He said, “Your sign is that you will not speak to the people for three nights straight.” (Quran, 19:10)
And he came out to his people, from the sanctuary, and signaled to them to praise morning and evening. (Quran, 19:11)
“O John, hold on to the Scripture firmly,” and We gave him wisdom in his youth. (Quran, 19:12)
And tenderness from Us, and innocence. He was devout. (Quran, 19:13)
And kind to his parents; and he was not a disobedient tyrant. (Quran, 19:14)
And peace be upon him the day he was born, and the day he dies, and the Day he is raised alive. (Quran, 19:15)
And mention in the Scripture Mary, when she withdrew from her people to an eastern location. (Quran, 19:16)
She screened herself away from them, and We sent to her Our spirit, and He appeared to her as an immaculate human. (Quran, 19:17)
She said, “I take refuge from you in the Most Merciful, should you be righteous.” (Quran, 19:18)
He said, “I am only the messenger of your Lord, to give you the gift of a pure son.” (Quran, 19:19)
She said, “How can I have a son, when no man has touched me, and I was never unchaste?” (Quran, 19:20)
He said, “Thus said your Lord, `It is easy for Me, and We will make him a sign for humanity, and a mercy from Us. It is a matter already decided.'“ (Quran, 19:21)
So she carried him, and secluded herself with him in a remote place. (Quran, 19:22)
The labor-pains came upon her, by the trunk of a palm-tree. She said, “I wish I had died before this, and been completely forgotten.” (Quran, 19:23)
Whereupon he called her from beneath her: “Do not worry; your Lord has placed a stream beneath you. (Quran, 19:24)
And shake the trunk of the palm-tree towards you, and it will drop ripe dates by you.” (Quran, 19:25)
“So eat, and drink, and be consoled. And if you see any human, say, ‘I have vowed a fast to the Most Gracious, so I will not speak to any human today.'“ (Quran, 19:26)
Then she came to her people, carrying him. They said, “O Mary, you have done something terrible. (Quran, 19:27)
O sister of Aaron, your father was not an evil man, and your mother was not a whore.” (Quran, 19:28)
So she pointed to him. They said, “How can we speak to an infant in the crib?” (Quran, 19:29)
He said, “I am the servant of Allah. He has given me the Scripture, and made me a prophet. (Quran, 19:30)
And has made me blessed wherever I may be; and has enjoined on me prayer and charity, so long as I live. (Quran, 19:31)
And kind to my mother, and He did not make me a disobedient rebel. (Quran, 19:32)
So Peace is upon me the day I was born, and the day I die, and the Day I get resurrected alive.” (Quran, 19:33)
That is Jesus son of Mary—the Word of truth about which they doubt. (Quran, 19:34)
It is not for Allah to have a child—glory be to Him. To have anything done, He says to it, “Be,” and it becomes. (Quran, 19:35)
“Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so worship Him. That is a straight path.” (Quran, 19:36)
But the various factions differed among themselves. So woe to those who disbelieve from the scene of a tremendous Day. (Quran, 19:37)
Listen to them and watch for them the Day they come to Us. But the wrongdoers today are completely lost. (Quran, 19:38)
And warn them of the Day of Regret, when the matter will be concluded. Yet they are heedless, and they do not believe. (Quran, 19:39)
It is We who will inherit the earth and everyone on it, and to Us they will be returned. (Quran, 19:40)
And mention in the Scripture Abraham. He was a man of truth, a prophet. (Quran, 19:41)
He said to his father, “O my father, why do you worship what can neither hear, nor see, nor benefit you in any way? (Quran, 19:42)
O my father, there has come to me knowledge that never came to you. So follow me, and I will guide you along a straight way. (Quran, 19:43)
O my father, do not worship the devil. The devil is disobedient to the Most Gracious. (Quran, 19:44)
O my father, I fear that a punishment from the Most Gracious will afflict you, and you become an ally of the devil.” (Quran, 19:45)
He said, “Are you renouncing my gods, O Abraham? If you do not desist, I will stone you. So leave me alone for a while.” (Quran, 19:46)
He said, “Peace be upon you. I will ask my Lord to forgive you; He has been Kind to me. (Quran, 19:47)
And I will withdraw from you, and from what you pray to instead of Allah. And I will pray to my Lord, and I hope I will not be disappointed in my prayer to my Lord.” (Quran, 19:48)
When he withdrew from them, and from what they worship besides Allah, We granted him Isaac and Jacob. And each We made a prophet. (Quran, 19:49)
And We gave them freely of Our mercy, and gave them a noble reputation of truth. (Quran, 19:50)
And mention in the Scripture Moses. He was dedicated. He was a messenger and a prophet. (Quran, 19:51)
And We called him from the right side of the Mount, and brought him near in communion. (Quran, 19:52)
And We granted him, out of Our mercy, his brother Aaron, a prophet. (Quran, 19:53)
And mention in the Scripture Ishmael. He was true to his promise, and was a messenger, a prophet. (Quran, 19:54)
And he used to enjoin on his people prayer and charity, and he was pleasing to his Lord. (Quran, 19:55)
And mention in the Scripture Enoch. He was a man of truth, a prophet. (Quran, 19:56)
And We raised him to a high position. (Quran, 19:57)
These are some of the prophets Allah has blessed, from the descendants of Adam, and from those We carried with Noah, and from the descendants of Abraham and Israel, and from those We guided and selected. Whenever the revelations of the Most Gracious are recited to them, they would fall down, prostrating and weeping. (Quran, 19:58)
But they were succeeded by generations who lost the prayers and followed their appetites. They will meet perdition. (Quran, 19:59)
Except for those who repent, and believe, and act righteously. These will enter Paradise, and will not be wronged in the least. (Quran, 19:60)
The Gardens of Eden, promised by the Most Merciful to His servants in the Unseen. His promise will certainly come true. (Quran, 19:61)
They will hear no nonsense therein, but only peace. And they will have their provision therein, morning and evening. (Quran, 19:62)
Such is Paradise which We will give as inheritance to those of Our servants who are devout. (Quran, 19:63)
“We do not descend except by the command of your Lord. His is what is before us, and what is behind us, and what is between them. Your Lord is never forgetful.” (Quran, 19:64)
Lord of the heavens and the earth and what is between them. So worship Him, and persevere in His service. Do you know of anyone equal to Him? (Quran, 19:65)
And the human being says, “When I am dead, will I be brought back alive?” (Quran, 19:66)
Does the human being not remember that We created him before, when he was nothing? (Quran, 19:67)
By your Lord, We will round them up, and the devils, then We will bring them around Hell, on their knees. (Quran, 19:68)
Then, out of every sect, We will snatch those most defiant to the Most Merciful. (Quran, 19:69)
We are fully aware of those most deserving to scorch in it. (Quran, 19:70)
There is not one of you but will go down to it. This has been an unavoidable decree of your Lord. (Quran, 19:71)
Then We will rescue those who were devout, and leave the wrongdoers in it, on their knees. (Quran, 19:72)
When Our clear revelations are recited to them, those who disbelieve say to those who believe, “Which of the two parties is better in position, and superior in influence?” (Quran, 19:73)
How many a generation have We destroyed before them, who surpassed them in riches and splendor? (Quran, 19:74)
Say, “Whoever is in error, the Most Merciful will lead him on.” Until, when they see what they were promised—either the punishment, or the Hour. Then they will know who was in worse position and weaker in forces. (Quran, 19:75)
Allah increases in guidance those who accept guidance. And the things that endure—the righteous deeds—have the best reward with your Lord, and the best outcome. (Quran, 19:76)
Have you seen him who denied Our revelations, and said, “I will be given wealth and children”? (Quran, 19:77)
Did he look into the future, or did he receive a promise from the Most Merciful? (Quran, 19:78)
No indeed! We will write what he says, and will keep extending the agony for him. (Quran, 19:79)
Then We will inherit from him what he speaks of, and he will come to Us alone. (Quran, 19:80)
And they took, besides Allah, other gods, to be for them a source of strength. (Quran, 19:81)
By no means! They will reject their worship of them, and become opponents to them. (Quran, 19:82)
Have you not considered how We dispatch the devils against the disbelievers, exciting them with incitement? (Quran, 19:83)
So do not hurry against them. We are counting for them a countdown. (Quran, 19:84)
On the Day when We will gather the righteous to the Most Merciful, as guests. (Quran, 19:85)
And herd the sinners into hell, like animals to water. (Quran, 19:86)
They will have no power of intercession, except for someone who has an agreement with the Most Merciful. (Quran, 19:87)
And they say, “The Most Merciful has begotten a son.” (Quran, 19:88)
You have come up with something monstrous. (Quran, 19:89)
At which the heavens almost rupture, and the earth splits, and the mountains fall and crumble. (Quran, 19:90)
Because they attribute a son to the Most Merciful. (Quran, 19:91)
It is not fitting for the Most Merciful to have a son. (Quran, 19:92)
There is none in the heavens and the earth but will come to the Most Merciful as a servant. (Quran, 19:93)
He has enumerated them, and counted them one by one. (Quran, 19:94)
And each one of them will come to Him on the Day of Resurrection alone. (Quran, 19:95)
Those who believe and do righteous deeds, the Most Merciful will give them love. (Quran, 19:96)
We made it easy in your tongue, in order to deliver good news to the righteous, and to warn with it a hostile people. (Quran, 19:97)
How many a generation have We destroyed before them? Can you feel a single one of them, or hear from them the slightest whisper? (Quran, 19:98)
Ta, Ha. (Quran, 20:1)
We did not reveal the Quran to you to make you suffer. (Quran, 20:2)
But only as a reminder for him who fears. (Quran, 20:3)
A revelation from He who created the earth and the high heavens. (Quran, 20:4)
The Most Merciful; on the Throne He settled. (Quran, 20:5)
To Him belongs everything in the heavens and the earth, and everything between them, and everything beneath the soil. (Quran, 20:6)
If you speak aloud—He knows the secret, and the most hidden. (Quran, 20:7)
Allah, there is no god but He, His are the Most Beautiful Names. (Quran, 20:8)
Has the story of Moses reached you? (Quran, 20:9)
When he saw a fire, he said to his family, “Stay; I have noticed a fire; Perhaps I can bring you a torch therefrom, or find some guidance by the fire.” (Quran, 20:10)
Then, when he reached it, he was called, “O Moses. (Quran, 20:11)
I—I am your Lord. Take off your shoes. You are in the sacred valley of Tuwa. (Quran, 20:12)
I have chosen you, so listen to what is revealed. (Quran, 20:13)
I—I am Allah. There is no Allah but I. So serve Me, and practice the prayer for My remembrance. (Quran, 20:14)
The Hour is coming—but I keep it almost hidden—so that each soul will be paid for what it endeavors. (Quran, 20:15)
And do not let him who denies it and follows his desire turn you away from it, lest you fall. (Quran, 20:16)
And what is that in your right-hand, O Moses?” (Quran, 20:17)
He said, “This is my staff. I lean on it, and herd my sheep with it, and I have other uses for it.” (Quran, 20:18)
He said, “Throw it, O Moses.” (Quran, 20:19)
So he threw it—thereupon it became a moving serpent. (Quran, 20:20)
He said, “Take hold of it, and do not fear. We will restore it to its original condition. (Quran, 20:21)
And press your hand to your side; it will come out white, without a blemish—another sign. (Quran, 20:22)
That We may show you some of Our greatest signs. (Quran, 20:23)
Go to Pharaoh; He has transgressed.” (Quran, 20:24)
He said, “My Lord, put my heart at peace for me. (Quran, 20:25)
And ease my task for me. (Quran, 20:26)
And untie the knot from my tongue. (Quran, 20:27)
So they can understand my speech. (Quran, 20:28)
And appoint an assistant for me, from my family. (Quran, 20:29)
Aaron, my brother. (Quran, 20:30)
Strengthen me with him. (Quran, 20:31)
And have him share in my mission. (Quran, 20:32)
That we may glorify You much. (Quran, 20:33)
And remember You much. (Quran, 20:34)
You are always watching over us.” (Quran, 20:35)
He said, “You are granted your request, O Moses. (Quran, 20:36)
We had favored you another time. (Quran, 20:37)
When We inspired your mother with the inspiration. (Quran, 20:38)
`Put him in the chest; then cast him into the river. The river will wash him to shore, where an enemy of Mine and an enemy of his will pick him up. And I have bestowed upon you love from Me, so that you may be reared before My eye. (Quran, 20:39)
When your sister walked along, and said, ‘Shall I tell you about someone who will take care of him?' So We returned you to your mother, that she may be comforted, and not sorrow. And you killed a person, but We saved you from stress; and We tested you thoroughly. And you stayed years among the people of Median. Then you came back, as ordained, O Moses. (Quran, 20:40)
And I made you for Myself. (Quran, 20:41)
Go, you and your brother, with My signs, and do not neglect My remembrance. (Quran, 20:42)
Go to Pharaoh. He has tyrannized. (Quran, 20:43)
But speak to him nicely. Perhaps he will remember, or have some fear.” (Quran, 20:44)
They said, “Lord, we fear he may persecute us, or become violent.” (Quran, 20:45)
He said, “Do not fear, I am with you, I hear and I see. (Quran, 20:46)
Approach him and say, `We are the messengers of your Lord; so let the Children of Israel go with us, and do not torment them. We bring you a sign from your Lord, and peace be upon him who follows guidance. (Quran, 20:47)
It was revealed to us that the punishment falls upon him who disbelieves and turns away.'“ (Quran, 20:48)
He said, “Who is your Lord, O Moses.” (Quran, 20:49)
He said, “Our Lord is He who gave everything its existence, then guided it.” (Quran, 20:50)
He said, “What about the first generations?” (Quran, 20:51)
He said, “Knowledge thereof is with my Lord, in a Book. My Lord never errs, nor does He forget.” (Quran, 20:52)
He who made the earth a habitat for you; and traced in it routes for you; and sent down water from the sky, with which We produce pairs of diverse plants. (Quran, 20:53)
Eat and pasture your livestock. In that are signs for those with understanding. (Quran, 20:54)
From it We created you, and into it We will return you, and from it We will bring you out another time. (Quran, 20:55)
We showed him Our signs, all of them, but he denied and refused. (Quran, 20:56)
He said, “Did you come to us to drive us out of our land with your magic, O Moses? (Quran, 20:57)
We will produce for you magic like it; so make an appointment between us and you, which we will not miss—neither us, nor you—in a central place.” (Quran, 20:58)
He said, “Your appointment is the day of the festival, so let the people be gathered together at mid-morning.” (Quran, 20:59)
Pharaoh turned away, put together his plan, and then came back. (Quran, 20:60)
Moses said to them, “Woe to you. Do not fabricate lies against Allah, or He will destroy you with a punishment. He who invents lies will fail.” (Quran, 20:61)
They disagreed among themselves over their affair, and conferred secretly. (Quran, 20:62)
They said, “These two are magicians who want to drive you out of your land with their magic, and to abolish your exemplary way of life. (Quran, 20:63)
So settle your plan, and come as one front. Today, whoever gains the upper hand will succeed.” (Quran, 20:64)
They said, “O Moses, either you throw, or we will be the first to throw.” (Quran, 20:65)
He said, “You throw.” And suddenly, their ropes and sticks appeared to him, because of their magic, to be crawling swiftly. (Quran, 20:66)
So Moses felt apprehensive within himself. (Quran, 20:67)
We said, “Do not be afraid, you are the uppermost. (Quran, 20:68)
Now throw down what is in your right hand—it will swallow what they have crafted. What they have crafted is only a magician’s trickery. But the magician will not succeed, no matter what he does.” (Quran, 20:69)
And the magicians fell down prostrate. They said, “We have believed in the Lord of Aaron and Moses.” (Quran, 20:70)
He said, “Did you believe in him before I have given you permission? He must be your chief, who has taught you magic. I will cut off your hands and your feet on alternate sides, and I will crucify you on the trunks of the palm-trees. Then you will know which of us is more severe in punishment, and more lasting.” (Quran, 20:71)
They said, “We will not prefer you to the proofs that have come to us, and Him who created us. So issue whatever judgment you wish to issue. You can only rule in this lowly life. (Quran, 20:72)
We have believed in our Lord, so that He may forgive us our sins, and the magic you have compelled us to practice. Allah is Better, and more Lasting.” (Quran, 20:73)
Whoever comes to his Lord guilty, for him is Hell, where he neither dies nor lives. (Quran, 20:74)
But whoever comes to Him a believer, having worked righteousness—these will have the highest ranks. (Quran, 20:75)
The Gardens of Perpetuity, beneath which rivers flow, dwelling therein forever. That is the reward for him who purifies himself. (Quran, 20:76)
And We inspired Moses: “Travel by night with My servants, and strike for them a dry path across the sea, not fearing being overtaken, nor worrying.” (Quran, 20:77)
Pharaoh pursued them with his troops, but the sea overwhelmed them, and completely engulfed them. (Quran, 20:78)
Pharaoh misled his people, and did not guide them. (Quran, 20:79)
O Children of Israel! We have delivered you from your enemy, and promised you by the right side of the Mount, and sent down to you manna and quails. (Quran, 20:80)
Eat of the good things We have provided for you, but do not be excessive therein, lest My wrath descends upon you. He upon whom My wrath descends has fallen. (Quran, 20:81)
And I am Forgiving towards him who repents, believes, acts righteously, and then remains guided. (Quran, 20:82)
“And what made you rush ahead of your people, O Moses?” (Quran, 20:83)
He said, “They are following in my footsteps; and I hurried on to You, my Lord, that you may be pleased.” (Quran, 20:84)
He said, “We have tested your people in your absence, and the Samarian misled them.” (Quran, 20:85)
So Moses returned to his people, angry and disappointed. He said, “O my people, did your Lord not promise you a good promise? Was the time too long for you? Or did you want wrath from your Lord to descend upon you, so you broke your promise to me?” (Quran, 20:86)
They said, “We did not break our promise to you by our choice, but we were made to carry loads of the people’s ornaments, and we cast them in. That was what the Samarian suggested.” (Quran, 20:87)
So he produced for them a calf—a mere body which lowed. And they said, “This is your god, and the god of Moses, but he has forgotten.” (Quran, 20:88)
Did they not see that it cannot return a word to them, and has no power to harm them or benefit them? (Quran, 20:89)
Aaron had said to them before, “O my people, you are being tested by this. And your Lord is the Merciful, so follow me, and obey my command.” (Quran, 20:90)
They said, “We will not give up our devotion to it, until Moses returns to us.” (Quran, 20:91)
He said, “O Aaron, what prevented you, when you saw them going astray. (Quran, 20:92)
From following me? Did you disobey my command?” (Quran, 20:93)
He said, “Son of my mother, do not seize me by my beard or my head. I feared you would say, `You have caused division among the Children of Israel, and did not regard my word.'“ (Quran, 20:94)
He said, “What do you have to say, O Samarian?” (Quran, 20:95)
He said, “I saw what they did not see, so I grasped a handful from the Messenger’s traces, and I flung it away. Thus my soul prompted me.” (Quran, 20:96)
He said, “Begone! Your lot in this life is to say, ‘No contact.’ And you have an appointment that you will not miss. Now look at your god that you remained devoted to—we will burn it up, and then blow it away into the sea, as powder.” (Quran, 20:97)
Surely your god is Allah, the One besides whom there is no other god. He comprehends everything in knowledge. (Quran, 20:98)
Thus We narrate to you reports of times gone by; and We have given you a message from Our Presence. (Quran, 20:99)
Whoever turns away from it will carry on the Day of Resurrection a burden. (Quran, 20:100)
Abiding therein forever. And wretched is their burden on the Day of Resurrection. (Quran, 20:101)
On the Day when the Trumpet is blown—We will gather the sinners on that Day, blue. (Quran, 20:102)
Murmuring among themselves: “You have lingered only for ten.” (Quran, 20:103)
We are fully aware of what they say, when the most exemplary of them in conduct will say, “You have lingered only a day.” (Quran, 20:104)
And they ask you about the mountains. Say, “My Lord will crumble them utterly.” (Quran, 20:105)
And leave them desolate waste. (Quran, 20:106)
You will see in them neither crookedness, nor deviation.” (Quran, 20:107)
On that Day, they will follow the caller, without any deviation. Voices will be hushed before the Merciful, and you will hear nothing but murmur. (Quran, 20:108)
On that Day, intercession will not avail, except for him permitted by the Merciful, and whose words He has approved. (Quran, 20:109)
He knows what is before them and what is behind them, and they cannot comprehend Him in their knowledge. (Quran, 20:110)
Faces will be humbled before the Living, the Eternal. Whoever carries injustice will despair. (Quran, 20:111)
But whoever has done righteous deeds, while being a believer—will fear neither injustice, nor grievance. (Quran, 20:112)
Thus We have revealed it an Arabic Quran, and We have diversified the warnings in it, that perhaps they would become righteous, or it may produce a lesson for them. (Quran, 20:113)
Exalted is Allah, the True King. Do not be hasty with the Quran before its inspiration to you is concluded, and say, “My Lord, increase me in knowledge.” (Quran, 20:114)
And We covenanted with Adam before, but he forgot, and We found in him no resolve. (Quran, 20:115)
And when We said to the angels, “Bow down to Adam.” They bowed down, except for Satan; he refused. (Quran, 20:116)
We said, “O Adam, this is an enemy to you and to your wife. So do not let him make you leave the Garden, for then you will suffer. (Quran, 20:117)
In it you will never go hungry, nor be naked. (Quran, 20:118)
Nor will you be thirsty in it, nor will you swelter.” (Quran, 20:119)
But Satan whispered to him. He said, “O Adam, shall I show you the Tree of Immortality, and a kingdom that never decays?” (Quran, 20:120)
And so they ate from it; whereupon their bodies became visible to them, and they started covering themselves with the leaves of the Garden. Thus Adam disobeyed his Lord, and fell. (Quran, 20:121)
But then his Lord recalled him, and pardoned him, and guided him. (Quran, 20:122)
He said, “Go down from it, altogether; some of you enemies of some others. But whenever guidance comes to you from Me, whoever follows My guidance, will not go astray, nor suffer. (Quran, 20:123)
But whoever turns away from My Reminder, for him is a confined life. And We will raise him on the Day of Resurrection blind.” (Quran, 20:124)
He will say, “My Lord, why did You raise me blind, though I was seeing?” (Quran, 20:125)
He will say, “Just as Our revelations came to you, and you forgot them, today you will be forgotten.” (Quran, 20:126)
Thus We recompense him who transgresses and does not believe in the revelations of his Lord. The punishment of the Hereafter is more severe, and more lasting. (Quran, 20:127)
Is it not instructive to them, how many generations before them We destroyed, in whose settlements they walk? Surely in that are signs for people of understanding. (Quran, 20:128)
Were it not for a word that issued from your Lord, the inevitable would have happened, but there is an appointed term. (Quran, 20:129)
So bear patiently what they say, and celebrate the praises of your Lord before the rising of the sun, and before its setting. And during the hours of the night glorify Him, and at the borders of the day, that you may be satisfied. (Quran, 20:130)
And do not extend your glance towards what We have given some classes of them to enjoy—the splendor of the life of this world—that We may test them thereby. Your Lord’s provision is better, and more lasting. (Quran, 20:131)
And exhort your people to pray, and patiently adhere to it. We ask of you no sustenance, but it is We who sustain you. The good ending is that for righteousness. (Quran, 20:132)
And they say, “Why does he not bring us a miracle from his Lord?” Were they not given enough miracles in the former scriptures? (Quran, 20:133)
Had We destroyed them with a punishment before him, they would have said, “Our Lord, if only You had sent us a messenger, we would have followed Your revelations before we were humiliated and disgraced.” (Quran, 20:134)
Say, “Everybody is waiting, so wait. You will know who the people of the straight path are, and who is rightly-guided. (Quran, 20:135)
Mankind’s reckoning has drawn near, but they turn away heedlessly. (Quran, 21:1)
No fresh reminder comes to them from their Lord, but they listen to it playfully. (Quran, 21:2)
Their hearts distracted, the wrongdoers confer secretly, “Is this anything but a mortal like you? Will you take to sorcery, with open-eyes?” (Quran, 21:3)
He said, “My Lord knows what is said in the heaven and the earth; and He is the Hearer, the Knower.” (Quran, 21:4)
And they said, “A jumble of dreams,” and, “He made it up,” and, “He is a poet,” “let him bring us a sign, like those sent to the ancients.” (Quran, 21:5)
None of the towns We destroyed before them had believed. Will they, then, believe? (Quran, 21:6)
We did not send before you except men, whom We inspired. Ask the people of knowledge, if you do not know. (Quran, 21:7)
We did not make them mere bodies that ate no food, nor were they immortal. (Quran, 21:8)
Then We fulfilled Our promise to them, and We saved them together with whomever We willed, and We destroyed the extravagant. (Quran, 21:9)
We have sent down to you a Book, containing your message. Do you not understand? (Quran, 21:10)
How many a guilty town have We crushed, and established thereafter another people? (Quran, 21:11)
Then, when they sensed Our might, they started running away from it. (Quran, 21:12)
Do not run, but come back to your luxuries, and to your homes, that you may be questioned. (Quran, 21:13)
They said, “Woe to us; we were unfair.” (Quran, 21:14)
This continued to be their cry, until We made them silent ashes. (Quran, 21:15)
We did not create the sky and the earth and what is between them for amusement. (Quran, 21:16)
If We wanted amusement, We could have found it within Us, were We to do so. (Quran, 21:17)
In fact, We hurl the truth against falsehood, and it crushes it, so it vanishes. Woe unto you, for what you describe. (Quran, 21:18)
To Him belongs everyone in the heavens and the earth. Those near Him are not too proud to worship Him, nor do they waver. (Quran, 21:19)
They praise night and day, without ever tiring. (Quran, 21:20)
Or have they taken to themselves gods from the earth who resurrect? (Quran, 21:21)
If there were in them gods other than Allah, they would have gone to ruin. So glory be to Allah, Lord of the Throne, beyond what they allege. (Quran, 21:22)
He will not be questioned about what He does, but they will be questioned. (Quran, 21:23)
Or have they taken, besides Him, other gods? Say, “Bring your proof. This is a message for those with me, and a message of those before me.” But most of them do not know the truth, so they turn away. (Quran, 21:24)
We never sent a messenger before you without inspiring him that: “There is no god but I, so worship Me.” (Quran, 21:25)
And they say, “The Most Merciful has taken to himself a son.” Be He glorified; they are but honored servants. (Quran, 21:26)
They never speak before He has spoken, and they only act on His command. (Quran, 21:27)
He knows what is before them, and what is behind them; and they do not intercede except for him whom He approves; and they tremble in awe of Him. (Quran, 21:28)
And whoever of them says, “I am a god besides Him,” We will reward him with Hell. Thus We reward the wrongdoers. (Quran, 21:29)
Do the disbelievers not see that the heavens and the earth were one mass, and We tore them apart? And We made from water every living thing. Will they not believe? (Quran, 21:30)
And We placed on earth stabilizers, lest it sways with them, and We placed therein signposts and passages, that they may be guided. (Quran, 21:31)
And We made the sky a protected ceiling; yet they turn away from its wonders. (Quran, 21:32)
It is He who created the night and the day, and the sun and the moon; each floating in an orbit. (Quran, 21:33)
We did not grant immortality to any human being before you. Should you die, are they then the immortal? (Quran, 21:34)
Every soul will taste death. We burden you with adversity and prosperity—a test. And to Us you will be returned. (Quran, 21:35)
When those who disbelieve see you, they treat you only with ridicule: “Is this the one who mentions your gods?” And they reject the mention of the Merciful. (Quran, 21:36)
The human being was created of haste. I will show you My signs, so do not seek to rush Me. (Quran, 21:37)
And they say, “When will this promise come true, if you are truthful?” (Quran, 21:38)
If those who disbelieve only knew, when they cannot keep the fire off their faces and off their backs, and they will not be helped. (Quran, 21:39)
In fact, it will come upon them suddenly, and bewilder them. They will not be able to repel it, and they will not be reprieved. (Quran, 21:40)
Messengers before you were also ridiculed, but those who jeered were surrounded by what they had ridiculed. (Quran, 21:41)
Say, “Who guards you against the Merciful by night and by day?” But they turn away from the mention of their Lord. (Quran, 21:42)
Or do they have gods who can defend them against Us? They cannot help themselves, nor will they be protected from Us. (Quran, 21:43)
We have given these enjoyments, and their ancestors, until time grew long upon them. Do they not see how We gradually reduce the land from its extremities? Are they then the victors? (Quran, 21:44)
Say, “I am warning you through inspiration.” But the deaf cannot hear the call when they are being warned. (Quran, 21:45)
And when a breath of your Lord’s punishment touches them, they say, “Woe to us, we were truly wicked.” (Quran, 21:46)
We will set up the scales of justice for the Day of Resurrection, so that no soul will suffer the least injustice. And even if it be the weight of a mustard-seed, We will bring it up. Sufficient are We as Reckoners. (Quran, 21:47)
We gave Moses and Aaron the Criterion, and illumination, and a reminder for the righteous. (Quran, 21:48)
Those who fear their Lord in private, and are apprehensive of the Hour. (Quran, 21:49)
This too is a blessed message that We revealed. Are you going to deny it? (Quran, 21:50)
We gave Abraham his integrity formerly, and We knew him well. (Quran, 21:51)
When he said to his father and his people, “What are these statues to which you are devoted?” (Quran, 21:52)
They said, “We found our parents worshiping them.” (Quran, 21:53)
He said, “You and your parents are in evident error.” (Quran, 21:54)
They said, “Are you telling us the truth, or are you just playing?” (Quran, 21:55)
He said, “Your Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, the One who created them, and I bear witness to that. (Quran, 21:56)
“By Allah, I will have a plan for your statues after you have gone away.” (Quran, 21:57)
So he reduced them into pieces, except for their biggest, that they may return to it. (Quran, 21:58)
They said, “Who did this to our gods? He is certainly one of the wrongdoers.” (Quran, 21:59)
They said, “We heard a youth mentioning them. He is called Abraham.” (Quran, 21:60)
They said, “Bring him before the eyes of the people, so that they may witness.” (Quran, 21:61)
They said, “Are you the one who did this to our gods, O Abraham?” (Quran, 21:62)
He said, “But it was this biggest of them that did it. Ask them, if they can speak.” (Quran, 21:63)
Then they turned to one another, and said, “You yourselves are the wrongdoers.” (Quran, 21:64)
But they reverted to their old ideas: “You certainly know that these do not speak.” (Quran, 21:65)
He said, “Do you worship, instead of Allah, what can neither benefit you in anything, nor harm you? (Quran, 21:66)
Fie on you, and on what you worship instead of Allah. Do you not understand?” (Quran, 21:67)
They said, “Burn him and support your gods, if you are going to act.” (Quran, 21:68)
We said, “O fire, be coolness and safety upon Abraham.” (Quran, 21:69)
They planned to harm him, but We made them the worst losers. (Quran, 21:70)
And We delivered him, and Lot, to the land that We blessed for all people. (Quran, 21:71)
And We granted him Isaac and Jacob as a gift; and each We made righteous. (Quran, 21:72)
And We made them leaders, guiding by Our command; and We inspired them to do good works, and to observe the prayer, and to give out charity. They were devoted servants to Us. (Quran, 21:73)
And Lot—We gave him judgment and knowledge, and We delivered him from the town that practiced the abominations. They were wicked and perverted people. (Quran, 21:74)
And We admitted him into Our mercy; for He was one of the righteous. (Quran, 21:75)
And Noah, when he called before. So We answered him, and delivered him and his family from the great disaster. (Quran, 21:76)
And We supported him against the people who rejected Our signs. They were an evil people, so We drowned them all. (Quran, 21:77)
And David and Solomon, when they gave judgment in the case of the field, when some people’s sheep wandered therein by night; and We were witnesses to their judgment. (Quran, 21:78)
And so We made Solomon understand it, and to each We gave wisdom and knowledge. And We subjected the mountains along with David to sing Our praises, and the birds as well—surely We did. (Quran, 21:79)
And We taught him the making of shields for you, to protect you from your violence. Are you, then, appreciative? (Quran, 21:80)
And to Solomon the stormy wind, blowing at His command towards the land that We have blessed. We are aware of everything. (Quran, 21:81)
And of the devils were some that dived for him, and performed other, lesser tasks. But We kept them restrained. (Quran, 21:82)
And Job, when he cried out to his Lord: “Great harm has afflicted me, and you are the Most Merciful of the merciful.” (Quran, 21:83)
So We answered him, lifted his suffering, and restored his family to him, and their like with them—a mercy from Us, and a reminder for the worshipers. (Quran, 21:84)
And Ishmael, and Enoch, and Ezekiel; each was one of the steadfast. (Quran, 21:85)
And We admitted them into Our mercy. They were among the righteous. (Quran, 21:86)
And Jonah, when he stormed out in fury, thinking We had no power over him. But then He cried out in the darkness, “There is no god but You! Glory to You! I was one of the wrongdoers!” (Quran, 21:87)
So We answered him, and saved him from the affliction. Thus We save the faithful. (Quran, 21:88)
And Zechariah, when he called out to his Lord, “My Lord, do not leave me alone, even though you are the Best of heirs.” (Quran, 21:89)
So We answered him, and gave him John. And We cured his wife for him. They used to vie in doing righteous deeds, and used to call on Us in love and awe, and they used to humble themselves to Us. (Quran, 21:90)
And she who guarded her virginity. We breathed into her of Our spirit, and made her and her son a sign to the world. (Quran, 21:91)
This community of yours is one community, and I am your Lord, so worship Me. (Quran, 21:92)
But they splintered themselves into factions. They will all return to Us. (Quran, 21:93)
Whoever does righteous deeds, and is a believer, his effort will not be denied. We are writing it down for him. (Quran, 21:94)
There is a ban on the town that We had destroyed—that they will not return. (Quran, 21:95)
Until, when Gog and Magog are let loose, and they swarm down from every mound. (Quran, 21:96)
The promise of truth has drawn near. The eyes of those who disbelieved will stare in horror: “Woe to us. We were oblivious to this. In fact, we were wrongdoers.” (Quran, 21:97)
You and what you worship besides Allah are fuel for Hell. You will descend into it. (Quran, 21:98)
Had these been gods, they would not have descended into it. All will abide in it. (Quran, 21:99)
In it they will wail. In it they will not hear. (Quran, 21:100)
As for those who deserved goodness from Us—these will be kept away from it. (Quran, 21:101)
They will not hear its hissing, and they will forever abide in what their hearts desire. (Quran, 21:102)
The Supreme Fear will not worry them, and the angels will receive them: “This is your Day which you were promised.” (Quran, 21:103)
On the Day when We fold the heaven, like the folding of a book. Just as We began the first creation, We will repeat it—a promise binding on Us. We will act. (Quran, 21:104)
We have written in the Psalms, after the Reminder, that the earth will be inherited by My righteous servants. (Quran, 21:105)
Indeed, in this is a message for people who worship. (Quran, 21:106)
We did not send you except as mercy to mankind. (Quran, 21:107)
Say, “It is revealed to me that your Allah is One Allah. Are you going to submit?” (Quran, 21:108)
But if they turn away, say, “I have informed you sufficiently. Although I do not know whether what you are promised is near or far.” (Quran, 21:109)
He knows what is said openly, and He knows what you conceal. (Quran, 21:110)
“And I do not know whether it is perhaps a trial for you, and an enjoyment for a while.” (Quran, 21:111)
He said, “My Lord, judge with justice.” And, “Our Lord is the Gracious, Whose help is sought against what you allege.” (Quran, 21:112)
O people, be conscious of your Lord. The quaking of the Hour is a tremendous thing. (Quran, 22:1)
On the Day when you will see it: every nursing mother will discard her infant, and every pregnant woman will abort her load, and you will see the people drunk, even though they are not drunk—but the punishment of Allah is severe. (Quran, 22:2)
Among the people is he who argues about Allah without knowledge, and follows every defiant devil. (Quran, 22:3)
It was decreed for him, that whoever follows him—he will misguide him, and lead him to the torment of the Blaze. (Quran, 22:4)
O people! If you are in doubt about the Resurrection—We created you from dust, then from a small drop, then from a clinging clot, then from a lump of flesh, partly developed and partly undeveloped. In order to clarify things for you. And We settle in the wombs whatever We will for a designated term, and then We bring you out as infants, until you reach your full strength. And some of you will pass away, and some of you will be returned to the vilest age, so that he may not know, after having known. And you see the earth still; but when We send down water on it, it vibrates, and swells, and grows all kinds of lovely pairs. (Quran, 22:5)
That is because Allah is the truth, and because He gives life to the dead, and because He is Capable of everything. (Quran, 22:6)
And because the Hour is coming—there is no doubt about it—and because Allah will resurrect those in the graves. (Quran, 22:7)
And among the people is he who argues about Allah without knowledge, or guidance, or an enlightening scripture. (Quran, 22:8)
Turning aside in contempt, to lead away from the path of Allah. He will have humiliation in this world, and on the Day of Resurrection We will make him taste the agony of burning. (Quran, 22:9)
That is for what your hands have advanced, and because Allah is not unjust to the servants. (Quran, 22:10)
And among the people is he who worships Allah on edge. When something good comes his way, he is content with it. But when an ordeal strikes him, he makes a turnaround. He loses this world and the next. That is the obvious loss. (Quran, 22:11)
He invokes, instead of Allah, what can neither harm him nor benefit him. That is the far straying. (Quran, 22:12)
He invokes one whose harm is closer than his benefit. What a miserable master. What a miserable companion. (Quran, 22:13)
Allah will admit those who believe and do righteous deeds into Gardens beneath which rivers flow. Allah does whatever He wills. (Quran, 22:14)
Whoever thinks that Allah will not help him in this life and in the Hereafter—let him turn to heaven, then sever, and see if his cunning eliminates what enrages him. (Quran, 22:15)
Thus We revealed it as clarifying signs, and Allah guides whomever He wills. (Quran, 22:16)
Those who believe, and those who are Jewish, and the Sabeans, and the Christians, and the Zoroastrians, and the Polytheists—Allah will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection. Allah is witness to all things. (Quran, 22:17)
Do you not realize that to Allah prostrates everyone in the heavens and everyone on earth, and the sun, and the moon, and the stars, and the mountains, and the trees, and the animals, and many of the people? But many are justly deserving of punishment. Whomever Allah shames, there is none to honor him. Allah does whatever He wills. (Quran, 22:18)
Here are two adversaries feuding regarding their Lord. As for those who disbelieve, garments of fire will be tailored for them, and scalding water will be poured over their heads. (Quran, 22:19)
Melting their insides and their skins. (Quran, 22:20)
And they will have maces of iron. (Quran, 22:21)
Whenever they try to escape the gloom, they will be driven back to it: “Taste the suffering of burning.” (Quran, 22:22)
But Allah will admit those who believe and do good deeds into Gardens beneath which rivers flow. They will be decorated therein with bracelets of gold and pearls, and their garments therein will be of silk. (Quran, 22:23)
They were guided to purity of speech. They were guided to the path of the Most Praised. (Quran, 22:24)
As for those who disbelieve and repel from Allah’s path and from the Sacred Mosque—which We have designated for all mankind equally, whether residing therein or passing through—and whoever seeks to commit sacrilege therein—We will make him taste of a painful punishment. (Quran, 22:25)
We showed Abraham the location of the House: “Do not associate anything with Me; and purify My House for those who circle around, and those who stand to pray, and those who kneel and prostrate.” (Quran, 22:26)
And announce the pilgrimage to humanity. They will come to you on foot, and on every transport. They will come from every distant point. (Quran, 22:27)
That they may witness the benefits for themselves, and celebrate the name of Allah during the appointed days, for providing them with the animal livestock. So eat from it, and feed the unfortunate poor. (Quran, 22:28)
Then let them perform their acts of cleansing, and fulfill their vows, and circle around the Ancient House. (Quran, 22:29)
All that. Whoever venerates the sanctities of Allah—it is good for him with his Lord. All livestock are permitted to you, except what is recited to you. So stay away from the abomination of idols, and stay away from perjury. (Quran, 22:30)
Being true to Allah, without associating anything with Him. Whoever associates anything with Allah—it is as though he has fallen from the sky, and is snatched by the birds, or is swept away by the wind to a distant abyss. (Quran, 22:31)
So it is. Whoever venerates the sacraments of Allah—it is from the piety of the hearts. (Quran, 22:32)
In them are benefits for you until a certain time. Then their place is by the Ancient House. (Quran, 22:33)
We have appointed a rite for every nation, that they may commemorate Allah’s name over the livestock He has provided for them. Your Allah is One Allah, so to Him submit, and announce good news to the humble. (Quran, 22:34)
Those whose hearts tremble when Allah is mentioned, and those who endure what has befallen them, and those who perform the prayer and spend from what We have provided for them. (Quran, 22:35)
We have made the animal offerings emblems of Allah for you. In them is goodness for you. So pronounce Allah’s name upon them as they line up. Then, when they have fallen on their sides, eat of them and feed the contented and the beggar. Thus We have subjected them to you, that you may be thankful. (Quran, 22:36)
Neither their flesh, nor their blood, ever reaches Allah. What reaches Him is the righteousness from you. Thus He subdued them to you, that you may glorify Allah for guiding you. And give good news to the charitable. (Quran, 22:37)
Allah defends those who believe. Allah does not love any ungrateful traitor. (Quran, 22:38)
Permission is given to those who are fought against, and Allah is Able to give them victory. (Quran, 22:39)
Those who were unjustly evicted from their homes, merely for saying, “Our Lord is Allah.” Were it not that Allah repels people by means of others: monasteries, churches, synagogues, and mosques—where the name of Allah is mentioned much—would have been demolished. Allah supports whoever supports Him. Allah is Strong and Mighty. (Quran, 22:40)
Those who, when We empower them in the land, observe the prayer, and give regular charity, and command what is right, and forbid what is wrong. To Allah belongs the outcome of events. (Quran, 22:41)
If they deny you—before them the people of Noah, and Aad, and Thamood also denied. (Quran, 22:42)
And the people of Abraham, and the people of Lot. (Quran, 22:43)
And the inhabitants of Median. And Moses was denied. Then I reprieved those who disbelieved, but then I seized them. So how was My rejection? (Quran, 22:44)
How many a town have We destroyed while it was doing wrong? They lie in ruins; with stilled wells, and lofty mansions. (Quran, 22:45)
Have they not journeyed in the land, and had minds to reason with, or ears to listen with? It is not the eyes that go blind, but it is the hearts, within the chests, that go blind. (Quran, 22:46)
And they ask you to hasten the punishment. But Allah never breaks His promise. A day with your Lord is like a thousand years of your count. (Quran, 22:47)
How many a town have I reprieved, although it was unjust? Then I seized it. To Me is the destination. (Quran, 22:48)
Say, “O people, I am only a plain warner to you.” (Quran, 22:49)
Those who believe and work righteousness—for them is forgiveness and a generous provision. (Quran, 22:50)
But those who strive against Our revelations—these are the inmates of Hell. (Quran, 22:51)
We never sent a messenger before you, or a prophet, but when he had a desire Satan interfered in his wishes. But Allah nullifies what Satan interjects, and Allah affirms His revelations. Allah is Omniscient and Wise. (Quran, 22:52)
In order to make Satan’s suggestions a trial for those whose hearts are diseased, and those whose hearts are hardened. The wrongdoers are in profound discord. (Quran, 22:53)
And so that those endowed with knowledge may know that it is the truth from your Lord, and so believe in it, and their hearts soften to it. Allah guides those who believe to a straight path. (Quran, 22:54)
Those who disbelieve will continue to be hesitant about it, until the Hour comes upon them suddenly, or there comes to them the torment of a desolate Day. (Quran, 22:55)
Sovereignty on that Day belongs to Allah; He will judge between them. Those who believe and do good deeds will be in the Gardens of Bliss. (Quran, 22:56)
But those who disbelieve and reject Our revelations—these will have a humiliating punishment. (Quran, 22:57)
Those who emigrate in Allah’s cause, then get killed, or die, Allah will provide them with fine provisions. Allah is the Best of Providers. (Quran, 22:58)
He will admit them an admittance that will please them. Allah is Knowing and Clement. (Quran, 22:59)
That is so! Whoever retaliates similarly to the affliction he was made to suffer, and then he is wronged again, Allah will definitely assist him. Allah is Pardoning and Forgiving. (Quran, 22:60)
That is because Allah merges the night into the day, and He merges the day into the night, and because Allah is Hearing and Seeing. (Quran, 22:61)
That is because Allah is the Reality, and what they invoke besides Him is vanity, and because Allah is the Sublime, the Grand. (Quran, 22:62)
Do you not see that Allah sends down water from the sky, and the land becomes green? Allah is Kind and Aware. (Quran, 22:63)
To Him belongs everything in the heavens and everything on earth. Allah is the Rich, the Praised. (Quran, 22:64)
Do you not see that Allah made everything on earth subservient to you? How the ships sail at sea by His command? That He holds up the sky lest it falls on earth—except by His permission? Allah is Gracious towards the people, Most Merciful. (Quran, 22:65)
And it is He who gives you life, then makes you die, then revives you. The human being is unappreciative. (Quran, 22:66)
For every congregation We have appointed acts of devotion, which they observe. So do not let them dispute with you in this matter. And invite to your Lord; you are upon a straight guidance. (Quran, 22:67)
But if they dispute with you, say, “Allah is fully aware of what you do.” (Quran, 22:68)
Allah will judge between you on the Day of Resurrection regarding what you disagree about. (Quran, 22:69)
Do you not know that Allah knows everything in the heavens and the earth? This is in a book. That is easy for Allah. (Quran, 22:70)
Yet they worship, besides Allah, things for which He sent down no warrant, and what they have no knowledge of. There is no savior for the transgressors. (Quran, 22:71)
And when Our Clear Verses are recited to them, you will recognize disgust on the faces of those who disbelieve. They nearly assault those who recite to them Our Verses. Say, “Shall I inform you of something worse than that? The Fire! Allah has promised it to those who disbelieve. And what a wretched outcome!” (Quran, 22:72)
O people! A parable is presented, so listen to it: Those you invoke besides Allah will never create a fly, even if they banded together for that purpose. And if the fly steals anything from them, they cannot recover it from it. Weak are the pursuer and the pursued. (Quran, 22:73)
They do not value Allah as He should be valued. Allah is Strong and Powerful. (Quran, 22:74)
Allah chooses messengers from among the angels, and from among the people. Allah is Hearing and Seeing. (Quran, 22:75)
He knows what is before them, and what is behind them. To Allah all matters are referred. (Quran, 22:76)
O you who believe! Kneel, and prostrate, and worship your Lord, and do good deeds, so that you may succeed. (Quran, 22:77)
And strive for Allah, with the striving due to Him. He has chosen you, and has not burdened you in religion—the faith of your father Abraham. It is he who named you Muslims before, and in this. So that the Messenger may be a witness over you, and you may be witnesses over the people. So pray regularly, and give regular charity, and cleave to Allah. He is your Protector. What an excellent Protector, and what an excellent Helper. (Quran, 22:78)
Successful are the believers. (Quran, 23:1)
Those who are humble in their prayers. (Quran, 23:2)
Those who avoid nonsense. (Quran, 23:3)
Those who work for charity. (Quran, 23:4)
Those who safeguard their chastity. (Quran, 23:5)
Except from their spouses, or their dependents—for they are free from blame. (Quran, 23:6)
But whoever seeks anything beyond that—these are the transgressors. (Quran, 23:7)
Those who are faithful to their trusts and pledges. (Quran, 23:8)
Those who safeguard their prayers. (Quran, 23:9)
These are the inheritors. (Quran, 23:10)
Who will inherit Paradise, wherein they will dwell forever. (Quran, 23:11)
We created man from an extract of clay. (Quran, 23:12)
Then We made him a seed, in a secure repository. (Quran, 23:13)
Then We developed the seed into a clot. Then We developed the clot into a lump. Then We developed the lump into bones. Then We clothed the bones with flesh. Then We produced it into another creature. Most Blessed is Allah, the Best of Creators. (Quran, 23:14)
Then, after that, you will die. (Quran, 23:15)
Then, on the Day of Resurrection, you will be resurrected. (Quran, 23:16)
We created above you seven pathways, and We are never heedless of the creation. (Quran, 23:17)
And We sent down water from the sky in proper quantity, and settled it in the ground, and We are Able to take it away. (Quran, 23:18)
With it We produce for you gardens of palms and vines, yielding abundant fruit for you to eat. (Quran, 23:19)
And a tree springing out of Mount Sinai, producing oil, and seasoning for those who eat. (Quran, 23:20)
And there is a lesson for you in livestock: We give you to drink from what is in their bellies, and you have many benefits in them, and from them you eat. (Quran, 23:21)
And on them, and on the ships, you are transported. (Quran, 23:22)
We sent Noah to his people. He said, “O my people, worship Allah, you have no deity other than Him. Will you not take heed?” (Quran, 23:23)
But the notables of his people, who disbelieved, said, “This is nothing but a human like you, who wants to gain superiority over you. Had Allah willed, He would have sent down angels. We never heard of this from our forefathers of old. (Quran, 23:24)
He is nothing but a man possessed. Just ignore him for a while.” (Quran, 23:25)
He said, “My Lord, help me, for they have rejected me.” (Quran, 23:26)
So We inspired him: “Build the Ark under Our observation and by Our inspiration. And when Our decree comes to pass, and the oven boils over, load into it two pairs of every kind, together with your family, except those of them against whom the word has already been pronounced. And do not speak to me concerning those who did wrong; for they are to be drowned.” (Quran, 23:27)
Then, when you and those with you are settled in the Ark, say, “Praise be to Allah, who has saved us from the wrongdoing people.” (Quran, 23:28)
And say, “My Lord, land me with a blessed landing, as you are the best of transporters.” (Quran, 23:29)
Surely in that are signs. We are always testing. (Quran, 23:30)
Then, after them, We established another generation. (Quran, 23:31)
And We sent among them a messenger from themselves: “Serve Allah. You have no god other than Him. Will you not be cautious?” (Quran, 23:32)
But the dignitaries of his people, those who disbelieved and denied the meeting of the Hereafter, and We had indulged them in the present life, said, “This is nothing but a human like you; he eats what you eat, and he drinks what you drink. (Quran, 23:33)
If you obey a human being like yourselves, then you will be losers. (Quran, 23:34)
Does he promise you that when you have died and become dust and bones, you will be brought out? (Quran, 23:35)
Farfetched, farfetched is what you are promised. (Quran, 23:36)
There is nothing but our life in this world. We die, and we live, and we are not resurrected. (Quran, 23:37)
He is nothing but a man, making up lies about Allah. We have no faith in him.” (Quran, 23:38)
He said, “My Lord, help me, for they have rejected me.” (Quran, 23:39)
He said, “Soon they will be filled with regret.” (Quran, 23:40)
Then the Blast struck them, justifiably, and We turned them into scum. So away with the wicked people. (Quran, 23:41)
Then, after them, We raised other generations. (Quran, 23:42)
No nation can advance its time, nor can they postpone it. (Quran, 23:43)
Then We sent Our messengers in succession. Every time a messenger came to his community, they called him a liar. So We made them follow one another, and made them history. So away with a people who do not believe. (Quran, 23:44)
Then We sent Moses and his brother Aaron, with Our signs and a clear authority. (Quran, 23:45)
To Pharaoh and his nobles, but they turned arrogant. They were oppressive people. (Quran, 23:46)
They said, “Are we to believe in two mortals like us, and their people are our slaves?” (Quran, 23:47)
So they called them liars, and thus were among those destroyed. (Quran, 23:48)
And We gave Moses the Scripture, that they may be guided. (Quran, 23:49)
And We made Mary’s son and his mother a sign, and We sheltered them on high ground with security and flowing springs. (Quran, 23:50)
O messengers, eat of the good things, and act with integrity. I am aware of what you do. (Quran, 23:51)
This nation of yours is one nation, and I am your Lord, so fear Me. (Quran, 23:52)
But they tore themselves into sects; each party happy with what they have. (Quran, 23:53)
So leave them in their bewilderment until a time. (Quran, 23:54)
Do they assume that, in furnishing them with wealth and children. (Quran, 23:55)
We race to give them the good things? In fact, they have no idea. (Quran, 23:56)
Those who, from awe of their Lord, are fearful. (Quran, 23:57)
And those who believe in their Lord’s Verses. (Quran, 23:58)
And those who associate no partners with their Lord. (Quran, 23:59)
And those who give what they give, while their hearts quake, knowing that to their Lord they will return. (Quran, 23:60)
It is they who race towards goodness. It is they who will reach it first. (Quran, 23:61)
We never burden any soul beyond its capacity. And with Us is a record that tells the truth, and they will not be wronged. (Quran, 23:62)
But their hearts are puzzled because of this; and they have deeds that do not conform to this, which they continue to perpetrate. (Quran, 23:63)
Until, when We seize the decadent among them with torment, they begin to groan. (Quran, 23:64)
Do not groan today. You will receive no help from Us. (Quran, 23:65)
My Verses were recited to you, but you turned back on your heels. (Quran, 23:66)
Arrogant towards it—talked nonsense about it—disregarded it. (Quran, 23:67)
Have they not pondered the Word? Or has there come to them what came not to their forefathers of old? (Quran, 23:68)
Or is it that they did not recognize their messenger, so they are denying him? (Quran, 23:69)
Or do they say, “He is possessed?” In fact, he brought them the truth, but most of them hate the truth. (Quran, 23:70)
If the truth conformed to their desires, the heavens, the earth, and everyone in them would have gone to ruin. In fact, We have given them their message, but they keep avoiding their message. (Quran, 23:71)
Or are you asking them for a payment? The revenue from your Lord is better, and He is the Best of providers. (Quran, 23:72)
You are inviting them to a straight path. (Quran, 23:73)
But those who do not believe in the Hereafter are swerving from the path. (Quran, 23:74)
Even if We had mercy on them, and relieved their problems, they would still blindly persist in their defiance. (Quran, 23:75)
We have already gripped them with suffering, but they did not surrender to their Lord, nor did they humble themselves. (Quran, 23:76)
Until, when We have opened before them a gate of intense agony, at once they will despair. (Quran, 23:77)
It is He who produced for you the hearing, and the eyesight, and the feelings. But little gratitude you show. (Quran, 23:78)
And it is He who multiplied you on earth, and to Him you will be gathered. (Quran, 23:79)
And it is He who gives life and brings death, and to Him is the alternation of night and day. Do you not understand? (Quran, 23:80)
But they say the like of what the ancients said. (Quran, 23:81)
They say, “After we have died, and become dust and bones, will we be resurrected? (Quran, 23:82)
We were promised this before—we and our ancestors—these are nothing but legends of the ancients.” (Quran, 23:83)
Say, “To whom does the earth belong, and everyone in it, if you happen to know?” (Quran, 23:84)
They will say, “To Allah.” Say, “Will you not reflect?” (Quran, 23:85)
Say, “Who is the Lord of the seven heavens, and Lord of the Splendid Throne?” (Quran, 23:86)
They will say, “To Allah.” Say, “Will you not become righteous?” (Quran, 23:87)
Say, “In whose hand is the dominion of all things, and He protects and cannot be protected from, if you happen to know?” (Quran, 23:88)
They will say, “To Allah.” Say, “Then are you bewitched?” (Quran, 23:89)
In fact, We have given them the truth, and they are liars. (Quran, 23:90)
Allah has never begotten a son, nor is there any god besides Him. Otherwise, each god would have taken away what it has created, and some of them would have gained supremacy over others. Glory be to Allah, far beyond what they describe. (Quran, 23:91)
The Knower of the hidden and the manifest. He is exalted, far above what they associate. (Quran, 23:92)
Say, “My Lord, if You would show me what they are promised. (Quran, 23:93)
My Lord, do not place me among the wicked people.” (Quran, 23:94)
We are surely Able to show you what We promise them. (Quran, 23:95)
Repel evil by what is better. We are aware of what they describe. (Quran, 23:96)
And say, “My Lord, I seek refuge with You from the urgings of the devils. (Quran, 23:97)
And I seek refuge with You, my Lord, lest they become present.” (Quran, 23:98)
Until, when death comes to one of them, he says, “My Lord, send me back. (Quran, 23:99)
That I may do right in what I have neglected.” By no means! It is just a word that he utters. And behind them is a barrier, until the Day they are resurrected. (Quran, 23:100)
When the Horn is blown, no relations between them will exist on that Day, and they will not ask after one another. (Quran, 23:101)
Those whose scales are heavy—those are the successful. (Quran, 23:102)
But those whose scales are light—those are they who have lost their souls; in Hell they will dwell forever. (Quran, 23:103)
The Fire lashes their faces, and therein they grimace. (Quran, 23:104)
“Were not My revelations recited to you, and you kept on rejecting them?” (Quran, 23:105)
They will say, “Our Lord, our wretchedness prevailed over us, and we were a people astray. (Quran, 23:106)
Our Lord! Bring us out of this. If we ever returned, we would truly be evil.” (Quran, 23:107)
He will say, “Be despised therein, and do not speak to Me. (Quran, 23:108)
There was a group of My servants who would say, `Our Lord, we have believed, so forgive us, and have mercy on us; You are the Best of the merciful.' (Quran, 23:109)
But you made them a target of ridicule, until they made you forget My remembrance; and you used to laugh at them. (Quran, 23:110)
Today, I have rewarded them for their endurance. They are the ones who are the triumphant.” (Quran, 23:111)
He will say, “How many years did you remain on earth?” (Quran, 23:112)
They will say, “We remained a day, or part of a day; but ask those who keep count.” (Quran, 23:113)
He will say, “You remained only for a little while, if you only knew. (Quran, 23:114)
Did you think that We created you in vain, and that to Us you will not be returned?” (Quran, 23:115)
So Exalted is Allah, the Ruler, the Real. There is no god except He, the Lord of the Noble Throne. (Quran, 23:116)
Whoever invokes another god besides Allah—he has no proof thereof—his reckoning rests with his Lord. The disbelievers will not succeed. (Quran, 23:117)
And say, “My Lord, forgive and have mercy, for You are the Best of the merciful.” (Quran, 23:118)
A chapter that We have revealed, and made obligatory, and revealed in it clear Verses, that you may take heed. (Quran, 24:1)
The adulteress and the adulterer—whip each one of them a hundred lashes, and let no pity towards them overcome you regarding Allah’s Law, if you believe in Allah and the Last Day. And let a group of believers witness their punishment. (Quran, 24:2)
The adulterer shall marry none but an adulteress or an idolatress; and the adulteress shall marry none but an adulterer or an idolater. That has been prohibited for the believers. (Quran, 24:3)
Those who accuse chaste women, then cannot bring four witnesses, whip them eighty lashes, and do not ever accept their testimony. For these are the immoral. (Quran, 24:4)
Except for those who repent afterwards, and reform; for Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 24:5)
As for those who accuse their own spouses, but have no witnesses except themselves, the testimony of one of them is equivalent to four testimonies, if he swears by Allah that he is truthful. (Quran, 24:6)
And the fifth time, that Allah’s curse be upon him, if he is a liar. (Quran, 24:7)
But punishment shall be averted from her, if she swears four times by Allah, that he is a liar. (Quran, 24:8)
And the fifth time, that Allah’s wrath be upon her, if he is truthful. (Quran, 24:9)
