Were it not for Allah’s grace upon you, and His mercy, and that Allah is Conciliatory and Wise. (Quran, 24:10)
Those who perpetrated the slander are a band of you. Do not consider it bad for you, but it is good for you. Each person among them bears his share in the sin. As for him who played the major role—for him is a terrible punishment. (Quran, 24:11)
Why, when you heard about it, the believing men and women did not think well of one another, and say, “This is an obvious lie”? (Quran, 24:12)
Why did they not bring four witnesses to testify to it? If they fail to bring the witnesses, then in Allah’s sight, they are liars. (Quran, 24:13)
Were it not for Allah’s favor upon you, and His mercy, in this world and the Hereafter, you would have suffered a great punishment for what you have ventured into. (Quran, 24:14)
When you rumored it with your tongues, and spoke with your mouths what you had no knowledge of, and you considered it trivial; but according to Allah, it is serious. (Quran, 24:15)
When you heard it, you should have said, “It is not for us to repeat this. By Your glory, this is a serious slander.” (Quran, 24:16)
Allah cautions you never to return to the like of it, if you are believers. (Quran, 24:17)
Allah explains the Verses to you. Allah is Knowing and Wise. (Quran, 24:18)
Those who love to see immorality spread among the believers—for them is a painful punishment, in this life and in the Hereafter. Allah knows, and you do not know. (Quran, 24:19)
Were it not for Allah’s grace upon you, and His mercy, and that Allah is Clement and Merciful. (Quran, 24:20)
O you who believe! Do not follow Satan’s footsteps. Whoever follows Satan’s footsteps—he advocates obscenity and immorality. Were it not for Allah’s grace towards you, and His mercy, not one of you would have been pure, ever. But Allah purifies whomever He wills. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing. (Quran, 24:21)
Those of you who have affluence and means should not refuse to give to the relatives, and the needy, and the emigrants for the sake of Allah. And let them pardon, and let them overlook. Do you not love for Allah to pardon you? Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful. (Quran, 24:22)
Those who slander honorable, innocent, believing women are cursed in this life and in the Hereafter. They will have a terrible punishment. (Quran, 24:23)
On the Day when their tongues, and their hands, and their feet will testify against them regarding what they used to do. (Quran, 24:24)
On that Day, Allah will pay them their account in full, and they will know that Allah is the Evident Reality. (Quran, 24:25)
Bad women are for bad men, and bad men are for bad women, and good women are for good men, and good men are for good women. Those are acquitted of what they say. There is forgiveness for them, and a generous provision. (Quran, 24:26)
O you who believe! Do not enter homes other than your own, until you have asked permission and greeted their occupants. That is better for you, that you may be aware. (Quran, 24:27)
And if you find no one in them, do not enter them until you are given permission. And if it is said to you, “Turn back,” then turn back. That is more proper for you. Allah is aware of what you do. (Quran, 24:28)
There is no blame on you for entering uninhabited houses, in which are belongings of yours. Allah knows what you reveal and what you conceal. (Quran, 24:29)
Tell the believing men to restrain their looks, and to guard their privates. That is purer for them. Allah is cognizant of what they do. (Quran, 24:30)
And tell the believing women to restrain their looks, and to guard their privates, and not display their beauty except what is apparent thereof, and to draw their coverings over their breasts, and not expose their beauty except to their husbands, their fathers, their husbands' fathers, their sons, their husbands' sons, their brothers, their brothers' sons, their sisters' sons, their women, what their right hands possess, their male attendants who have no sexual desires, or children who are not yet aware of the nakedness of women. And they should not strike their feet to draw attention to their hidden beauty. And repent to Allah, all of you believers, so that you may succeed. (Quran, 24:31)
And wed the singles among you, and those who are fit among your servants and maids. If they are poor, Allah will enrich them from His bounty. Allah is All-Encompassing, All-Knowing. (Quran, 24:32)
And let those who do not find the means to marry abstain, until Allah enriches them from His bounty. If any of your servants wish to be freed, grant them their wish, if you recognize some good in them. And give them of Allah’s wealth which he has given you. And do not compel your girls to prostitution, seeking the materials of this life, if they desire to remain chaste. Should anyone compel them—after their compulsion, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 24:33)
We have sent down to you clarifying revelations, and examples of those who passed on before you, and advice for the righteous. (Quran, 24:34)
Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth. The allegory of His light is that of a pillar on which is a lamp. The lamp is within a glass. The glass is like a brilliant planet, fueled by a blessed tree, an olive tree, neither eastern nor western. Its oil would almost illuminate, even if no fire has touched it. Light upon Light. Allah guides to His light whomever He wills. Allah thus cites the parables for the people. Allah is cognizant of everything. (Quran, 24:35)
In houses which Allah has permitted to be raised, and His name is celebrated therein. He is glorified therein, morning and evening. (Quran, 24:36)
By men who neither trading nor commerce distracts them from Allah’s remembrance, and from performing the prayers, and from giving alms. They fear a Day when hearts and sights are overturned. (Quran, 24:37)
Allah will reward them according to the best of what they did, and He will increase them from His bounty. Allah provides for whomever He wills without reckoning. (Quran, 24:38)
As for those who disbelieve, their works are like a mirage in a desert. The thirsty assumes it is to be water. Until, when he has reached it, he finds it to be nothing, but there he finds Allah, Who settles his account in full. Allah is swift in reckoning. (Quran, 24:39)
Or like utter darkness in a vast ocean, covered by waves, above which are waves, above which is fog. Darkness upon darkness. If he brings out his hand, he will hardly see it. He to whom Allah has not granted a light has no light. (Quran, 24:40)
Do you not realize that Allah is glorified by whatever is in the heavens and the earth, and even by the birds in formation? Each knows its prayer and its manner of praise. Allah knows well what they do. (Quran, 24:41)
To Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth, and to Allah is the ultimate return. (Quran, 24:42)
Have you not seen how Allah propels the clouds, then brings them together, then piles them into a heap, and you see rain drops emerging from its midst? How He brings down loads of hail from the sky, striking with it whomever He wills, and diverting it from whomever He wills? The flash of its lightning almost snatches the sight away. (Quran, 24:43)
Allah alternates the night and the day. In that is a lesson for those who have insight. (Quran, 24:44)
Allah created every living creature from water. Some of them crawl on their bellies, and some walk on two feet, and others walk on four. Allah creates whatever He wills. Allah is Capable of everything. (Quran, 24:45)
We sent down enlightening revelations, and Allah guides whomever He wills to a straight path. (Quran, 24:46)
And they say, “We have believed in Allah and the Messenger, and we obey,” but some of them turn away afterwards. These are not believers. (Quran, 24:47)
And when they are called to Allah and His Messenger, in order to judge between them, some of them refuse. (Quran, 24:48)
But if justice is on their side, they accept it willingly. (Quran, 24:49)
Is there sickness in their hearts? Or are they suspicious? Or do they fear that Allah may do them injustice? Or His Messenger? In fact, they themselves are the unjust. (Quran, 24:50)
The response of the believers, when they are called to Allah and His Messenger in order to judge between them, is to say, “We hear and we obey.” These are the successful. (Quran, 24:51)
Whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger, and fears Allah, and is conscious of Him—these are the winners. (Quran, 24:52)
And they swear by Allah with their solemn oaths, that if you commanded them, they would mobilize. Say, “Do not swear. Obedience will be recognized. Allah is experienced with what you do.” (Quran, 24:53)
Say, “Obey Allah and obey the Messenger.” But if they turn away, then he is responsible for his obligations, and you are responsible for your obligations. And if you obey him, you will be guided. It is only incumbent on the Messenger to deliver the Clarifying Message. (Quran, 24:54)
Allah has promised those of you who believe and do righteous deeds, that He will make them successors on earth, as He made those before them successors, and He will establish for them their religion—which He has approved for them—and He will substitute security in place of their fear. They worship Me, never associating anything with Me. But whoever disbelieves after that—these are the sinners. (Quran, 24:55)
Pray regularly, and give regular charity, and obey the Messenger, so that you may receive mercy. (Quran, 24:56)
Never think that those who disbelieve can escape on earth. Their place is the Fire; a miserable destination. (Quran, 24:57)
O you who believe! Permission must be requested by your servants and those of you who have not reached puberty. On three occasions: before the Dawn Prayer, and at noon when you change your clothes, and after the Evening Prayer. These are three occasions of privacy for you. At other times, it is not wrong for you or them to intermingle with one another. Allah thus clarifies the revelations for you. Allah is Knowledgeable and Wise. (Quran, 24:58)
When the children among you reach puberty, they must ask permission, as those before them asked permission. Allah thus clarifies His revelations for you. Allah is Knowledgeable and Wise. (Quran, 24:59)
Women past the age of childbearing, who have no desire for marriage, commit no wrong by taking off their outer clothing, provided they do not flaunt their finery. But to maintain modesty is better for them. Allah is Hearing and Knowing. (Quran, 24:60)
There is no blame on the blind, nor any blame on the lame, nor any blame on the sick, nor on yourselves for eating at your homes, or your fathers’ homes, or your mothers’ homes, or your brothers’ homes, or your sisters’ homes, or the homes of your paternal uncles, or the homes of your paternal aunts, or the homes of your maternal uncles, or the homes of your maternal aunts, or those whose keys you own, or the homes of your friends. You commit no wrong by eating together or separately. But when you enter any home, greet one another with a greeting from Allah, blessed and good. Allah thus explains the revelations for you, so that you may understand. (Quran, 24:61)
The believers are those who believe in Allah and His Messenger, and when they are with him for a matter of common interest, they do not leave until they have asked him for permission. Those who ask your permission are those who believe in Allah and His Messenger. So when they ask your permission to attend to some affair of theirs, give permission to any of them you wish, and ask Allah’s forgiveness for them. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 24:62)
Do not address the Messenger in the same manner you address one another. Allah knows those of you who slip away using flimsy excuses. So let those who oppose his orders beware, lest an ordeal strikes them, or a painful punishment befalls them. (Quran, 24:63)
Surely, to Allah belongs everything in the heavens and the earth. He knows what you are about. And on the Day they are returned to Him, He will inform them of what they did. Allah has full knowledge of all things. (Quran, 24:64)

Do you not see how your Lord extends the shadow? Had He willed, He could have made it still. And We made the sun a pointer to it. (Quran, 25:45)
Then We withdraw it towards Us gradually. (Quran, 25:46)
And it is He who made the night a covering for you, and sleep for rest; and He made the day a revival. (Quran, 25:47)

To revive dead lands thereby, and to provide drink for the multitude of animals and humans We created. (Quran, 25:49)
We have circulated it among them, that they may reflect, but most people persist in thanklessness. (Quran, 25:50)

So do not obey the disbelievers, but strive against them with it, a mighty struggle. (Quran, 25:52)

Your Lord called to Moses, “Go to the tyrannical people. (Quran, 26:10)

He said, “Bring it, if you are being truthful.” (Quran, 26:31)
So he cast his staff; and it was a serpent, plain to see. (Quran, 26:32)
And he pulled his hand; and it was white, for all to see. (Quran, 26:33)
He said to the dignitaries around him, “This is a skilled magician. (Quran, 26:34)
He intends to drive you out of your land with his magic, so what do you recommend?” (Quran, 26:35)
They said, “Delay him and his brother, and send recruiters to the cities. (Quran, 26:36)
To bring you every experienced magician.” (Quran, 26:37)
So the magicians were gathered for the appointment on a specified day. (Quran, 26:38)
And it was said to the people, “Are you all gathered? (Quran, 26:39)
That we may follow the magicians, if they are the winners.” (Quran, 26:40)
When the magicians arrived, they said to Pharaoh, “Is there a reward for us, if we are the winners?” (Quran, 26:41)
He said, “Yes, and you will be among those favored.” (Quran, 26:42)
Moses said to them, “Present what you intend to present.” (Quran, 26:43)

Then Moses threw his staff, and behold, it began swallowing their trickery. (Quran, 26:45)
And the magicians fell down prostrating. (Quran, 26:46)
They said, “We have believed in the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:47)
The Lord of Moses and Aaron.” (Quran, 26:48)

They said, “No problem. To our Lord we will return. (Quran, 26:50)
We are eager for our Lord to forgive us our sins, since we are the first of the believers.” (Quran, 26:51)
And We inspired Moses: “Travel with My servants by night. You will be followed.” (Quran, 26:52)
Pharaoh sent heralds to the cities. (Quran, 26:53)
“These are a small gang. (Quran, 26:54)
And they are enraging us. (Quran, 26:55)
But we are a vigilant multitude.” (Quran, 26:56)
So We drove them out of gardens and springs. (Quran, 26:57)
And treasures and noble dwellings. (Quran, 26:58)
So it was. And We made the Children of Israel inherit them. (Quran, 26:59)
And they pursued them at sunrise. (Quran, 26:60)
When the two groups sighted each other, the followers of Moses said, “We are being overtaken.” (Quran, 26:61)
He said, “No; my Lord is with me, He will guide me.” (Quran, 26:62)
We inspired Moses: “Strike the sea with your staff.” Whereupon it parted, and each part was like a huge hill. (Quran, 26:63)
And there We brought the others near. (Quran, 26:64)
And We saved Moses and those with him, all together. (Quran, 26:65)
Then We drowned the others. (Quran, 26:66)
In that there is a sign, but most of them are not believers. (Quran, 26:67)
Surely, your Lord is the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 26:68)
And relate to them the story of Abraham. (Quran, 26:69)
When he said to his father and his people, “What do you worship?” (Quran, 26:70)
They said, “We worship idols, and we remain devoted to them.” (Quran, 26:71)
He said, “Do they hear you when you pray? (Quran, 26:72)
Or do they benefit you, or harm you?” (Quran, 26:73)
They said, “But we found our ancestors doing so.” (Quran, 26:74)
He said, “Have you considered what you worship. (Quran, 26:75)
You and your ancient ancestors? (Quran, 26:76)
They are enemies to me, but not so the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:77)
He who created me, and guides me. (Quran, 26:78)
He who feeds me, and waters me. (Quran, 26:79)
And when I get sick, He heals me. (Quran, 26:80)
He who makes me die, and then revives me. (Quran, 26:81)
He who, I hope, will forgive my sins on the Day of the Reckoning.” (Quran, 26:82)
“My Lord! Grant me wisdom, and include me with the righteous. (Quran, 26:83)
And give me a reputation of truth among the others. (Quran, 26:84)
And make me of the inheritors of the Garden of Bliss. (Quran, 26:85)
And forgive my father—he was one of the misguided. (Quran, 26:86)
And do not disgrace me on the Day they are resurrected. (Quran, 26:87)
The Day when neither wealth nor children will help. (Quran, 26:88)
Except for him who comes to Allah with a sound heart.” (Quran, 26:89)
And Paradise will be brought near for the righteous. (Quran, 26:90)
And the Blaze will be displayed to the deviators. (Quran, 26:91)
And it will be said to them, “Where are those you used to worship?” (Quran, 26:92)
Besides Allah? Can they help you, or help themselves?” (Quran, 26:93)
Then they will be toppled into it, together with the seducers. (Quran, 26:94)
And the soldiers of Satan, all of them. (Quran, 26:95)
They will say, as they feud in it. (Quran, 26:96)
“By Allah, We were in evident error. (Quran, 26:97)
For equating you with the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:98)
No one misled us except the sinners. (Quran, 26:99)
Now we have no intercessors. (Quran, 26:100)
And no sincere friend. (Quran, 26:101)
If only we could have another chance, we would be among the faithful.” (Quran, 26:102)
Surely in this is a sign, but most of them are not believers. (Quran, 26:103)
Your Lord is the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 26:104)
The people of Noah disbelieved the messengers. (Quran, 26:105)
Their brother Noah said to them, “Do you not fear? (Quran, 26:106)
I am to you a faithful messenger. (Quran, 26:107)
So fear Allah, and obey me. (Quran, 26:108)
I ask of you no payment for this. My payment is only from the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:109)
So fear Allah, and obey me.” (Quran, 26:110)
They said, “Shall we believe in you, when it is the lowliest who follow you?” (Quran, 26:111)
He said, “What do I know about what they do? (Quran, 26:112)
Their account rests only with my Lord, if you have sense. (Quran, 26:113)
And I am not about to drive away the believers. (Quran, 26:114)
I am only a clear warner.” (Quran, 26:115)
They said, “If you do not refrain, O Noah, you will be stoned.” (Quran, 26:116)
He said, “My Lord, my people have denied me. (Quran, 26:117)
So judge between me and them decisively, and deliver me and the believers who are with me. (Quran, 26:118)
So We delivered him and those with him in the laden Ark. (Quran, 26:119)
Then We drowned the rest. (Quran, 26:120)
In that is a sign, but most of them are not believers. (Quran, 26:121)
Your Lord is the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 26:122)
Aad disbelieved the messengers. (Quran, 26:123)
When their brother Hud said to them, “Do you not fear? (Quran, 26:124)
I am to you a faithful messenger. (Quran, 26:125)
So fear Allah, and obey me. (Quran, 26:126)
I ask of you no payment for this. My payment is only from the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:127)
Do you build a monument on every height for vanity's sake? (Quran, 26:128)
And you set up fortresses, hoping to live forever? (Quran, 26:129)
And when you strike, you strike mercilessly? (Quran, 26:130)
So fear Allah, and obey me. (Quran, 26:131)
And reverence Him, who supplied you with everything you know. (Quran, 26:132)
He supplied you with livestock and children. (Quran, 26:133)
And gardens and springs. (Quran, 26:134)

This is nothing but morals of the ancients. (Quran, 26:137)

So they denied him, and We destroyed them. Surely in this is a sign, but most of them are not believers. (Quran, 26:139)

So fear Allah, and obey me. (Quran, 26:144)
I ask of you no payment for it. My payment is only from the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:145)

In gardens and springs? (Quran, 26:147)
And fields, and palm-trees whose fruits are delicious? (Quran, 26:148)
And you skillfully carve houses in the mountains? (Quran, 26:149)
So fear Allah, and obey me. (Quran, 26:150)
And do not obey the command of the extravagant. (Quran, 26:151)
Who spread turmoil on earth, and do not reform.” (Quran, 26:152)
They said, “You are surely one of the bewitched. (Quran, 26:153)
You are nothing but a man like us. So bring us a sign, if you are truthful. (Quran, 26:154)
He said, “This is a she-camel; she has her turn of drinking, and you have your turn of drinking—on a specified day. (Quran, 26:155)
And do not touch her with harm, lest the punishment of a great day seizes you.” (Quran, 26:156)
But they slaughtered her, and became full of remorse. (Quran, 26:157)
So the punishment overtook them. Surely in this is a sign, but most of them are not believers. (Quran, 26:158)
Your Lord is the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 26:159)

Do you approach the males of the world? (Quran, 26:165)
And forsake the wives your Lord created for you? Indeed, you are intrusive people.” (Quran, 26:166)
They said, “Unless you refrain, O Lot, you will be expelled.” (Quran, 26:167)
He said, “I certainly deplore your conduct.” (Quran, 26:168)
“My Lord, save me and my family from what they do.” (Quran, 26:169)
So We saved him and his family, altogether. (Quran, 26:170)
Except for an old woman among those who tarried. (Quran, 26:171)
Then We destroyed the others. (Quran, 26:172)
And We rained down on them a rain. Dreadful is the rain of those forewarned. (Quran, 26:173)
Surely in this is a sign, but most of them are not believers. (Quran, 26:174)
Your Lord is the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 26:175)
The People of the Woods disbelieved the messengers. (Quran, 26:176)
When Shuaib said to them, “Do you not fear? (Quran, 26:177)
I am to you a trustworthy messenger. (Quran, 26:178)
So fear Allah, and obey me. (Quran, 26:179)
I ask of you no payment for it. My payment is only from the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:180)
Give full measure, and do not cheat. (Quran, 26:181)
And weigh with accurate scales. (Quran, 26:182)
And do not defraud people of their belongings, and do not work corruption in the land. (Quran, 26:183)
And fear Him who created you and the masses of old.” (Quran, 26:184)
They said, “You are one of those bewitched. (Quran, 26:185)
And you are nothing but a man like us; and we think that you are a liar. (Quran, 26:186)
So bring down on us pieces from the sky, if you are truthful.” (Quran, 26:187)
He said, “My Lord is Well Aware of what you do.” (Quran, 26:188)
But they denied him. So the punishment of the day of gloom gripped them. It was the punishment of a great day. (Quran, 26:189)
Surely in this is a sign, but most of them are not believers. (Quran, 26:190)
Your Lord is the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 26:191)
It is a revelation from the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 26:192)
The Honest Spirit came down with it. (Quran, 26:193)
Upon your heart, that you may be one of the warners. (Quran, 26:194)
In a clear Arabic tongue. (Quran, 26:195)
And it is in the scriptures of the ancients. (Quran, 26:196)
Is it not a sign for them that the scholars of the Children of Israel recognized it? (Quran, 26:197)
Had We revealed it to one of the foreigners. (Quran, 26:198)
And he had recited it to them, they still would not have believed in it. (Quran, 26:199)
Thus We make it pass through the hearts of the guilty. (Quran, 26:200)
They will not believe in it until they witness the painful punishment. (Quran, 26:201)
It will come to them suddenly, while they are unaware. (Quran, 26:202)
Then they will say, “Are we given any respite?” (Quran, 26:203)
Do they seek to hasten Our punishment? (Quran, 26:204)
Have you considered: if We let them enjoy themselves for some years. (Quran, 26:205)
Then there comes to them what they were promised. (Quran, 26:206)
Of what avail to them will be their past enjoyments? (Quran, 26:207)
Never did We destroy a town, but it had warners. (Quran, 26:208)
As a reminder—We are never unjust. (Quran, 26:209)
It was not the devils that revealed it. (Quran, 26:210)
It is not in their interests, nor in their power. (Quran, 26:211)
They are barred from hearing. (Quran, 26:212)
So do not pray to another god with Allah, else you will be of those tormented. (Quran, 26:213)
And warn your close relatives. (Quran, 26:214)
And lower your wing to those of the believers who follow you. (Quran, 26:215)
And if they disobey you, say, “I am innocent of what you do.” (Quran, 26:216)
And put your trust in the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 26:217)
He Who sees you when you rise. (Quran, 26:218)
And your devotions amidst the worshipers. (Quran, 26:219)
He is indeed the Hearer, the Aware. (Quran, 26:220)
Shall I inform you upon whom the devils descend? (Quran, 26:221)
They descend upon every sinful liar. (Quran, 26:222)
They give ear, and most of them are liars. (Quran, 26:223)
And as for the poets—the deviators follow them. (Quran, 26:224)
Do you not see how they ramble in every style? (Quran, 26:225)
And how they say what they do not do? (Quran, 26:226)
Except for those who believe, and do good deeds, and remember Allah frequently, and defend themselves after they are wronged. As for those who do wrong, they will know by what overturning they will be overturned. (Quran, 26:227)
Ta, Seen. These are the Signs of the Quran—a book that makes things clear. (Quran, 27:1)
Guidance and good news for the believers. (Quran, 27:2)
Those who observe the prayers, and give charity regularly, and are certain of the Hereafter. (Quran, 27:3)
As for those who do not believe in the Hereafter: We made their deeds appear good to them, so they wander aimlessly. (Quran, 27:4)
It is they who will receive the grievous punishment—and in the Hereafter they will be the greatest losers. (Quran, 27:5)
You are receiving the Quran from an All-Wise, All-Knowing. (Quran, 27:6)
When Moses said to his family, “I have glimpsed a fire. I will bring you some news from it; or bring you a firebrand, that you may warm yourselves.” (Quran, 27:7)
Then, when he reached it, he was called: “Blessed is He who is within the fire, and He who is around it, and glorified be Allah, Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 27:8)
O Moses, it is I, Allah, the Almighty, the Wise. (Quran, 27:9)
Throw down your staff.” But when he saw it quivering, as though it were a demon, he turned around not looking back. “O Moses, do not fear; the messengers do not fear in My presence. (Quran, 27:10)
But whoever has done wrong, and then substituted goodness in place of evil. I am Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 27:11)
Put your hand inside your pocket, and it will come out white, without blemish—among nine miracles to Pharaoh and his people, for they are immoral people.” (Quran, 27:12)
Yet when Our enlightening signs came to them, they said, “This is obvious witchcraft.” (Quran, 27:13)
And they rejected them, although their souls were certain of them, out of wickedness and pride. So see how the outcome was for the mischief-makers. (Quran, 27:14)
And We gave David and Solomon knowledge. They said, “Praise Allah, who has favored us over many of His believing servants.” (Quran, 27:15)
And Solomon succeeded David. He said, “O people, we were taught the language of birds, and we were given from everything. This is indeed a real blessing.” (Quran, 27:16)
To the service of Solomon were mobilized his troops of sprites, and men, and birds—all held in strict order. (Quran, 27:17)
Until, when they came upon the Valley of Ants, an ant said, “O ants! Go into your nests, lest Solomon and his troops crush you without noticing.” (Quran, 27:18)
He smiled and laughed at her words, and said, “My Lord, direct me to be thankful for the blessings you have bestowed upon me and upon my parents, and to do good works that please You. And admit me, by Your grace, into the company of Your virtuous servants.” (Quran, 27:19)
Then he inspected the birds, and said, “Why do I not see the hoopoe? Or is he among the absentees? (Quran, 27:20)
I will punish him most severely, or slay him, unless he gives me a valid excuse.” (Quran, 27:21)
But he did not stay for long. He said, “I have learnt something you did not know. I have come to you from Sheba, with reliable information. (Quran, 27:22)
I found a woman ruling over them, and she was given of everything, and she has a magnificent throne. (Quran, 27:23)
I found her and her people worshiping the sun, instead of Allah. Satan made their conduct appear good to them, and diverted them from the path, so they are not guided. (Quran, 27:24)
If only they would worship Allah, who brings to light the mysteries of the heavens and the earth, and knows what you conceal and what you reveal. (Quran, 27:25)
Allah—There is no god but He, the Lord of the Sublime Throne.” (Quran, 27:26)
He said, “We will see, whether you have spoken the truth, or whether you are a liar. (Quran, 27:27)
Go with this letter of mine, and deliver it to them; then withdraw from them, and see how they respond.” (Quran, 27:28)
She said, “O Counselors, a gracious letter was delivered to me. (Quran, 27:29)
It is from Solomon, and it is, ‘In the Name of Allah, the Gracious, the Merciful. (Quran, 27:30)
Do not defy me, and come to me submissively.’” (Quran, 27:31)
She said, “O counselors, advise me in this matter of mine. I never make a decision unless you are present.” (Quran, 27:32)
They said, “We are a people of might and great courage, but the decision is yours, so consider what you wish to command.” (Quran, 27:33)
She said, “When kings enter a city, they devastate it, and subjugate its dignified people. Thus they always do. (Quran, 27:34)
I am sending them a gift, and will see what the envoys bring back.” (Quran, 27:35)
When he came to Solomon, he said, “Are you supplying me with money? What Allah has given me is better than what He has given you. It is you who delight in your gift. (Quran, 27:36)
Go back to them. We will come upon them with troops they cannot resist; and we will expel them from there, disgraced and humiliated.” (Quran, 27:37)
He said, “O notables, which one of you will bring me her throne before they come to me in submission?” (Quran, 27:38)
An imp of the sprites said, “I will bring it to you before you rise from your seat. I am strong and reliable enough to do it.” (Quran, 27:39)
He who had knowledge from the Book said, “I will bring it to you before your glance returns to you.” And when he saw it settled before him, he said, “This is from the grace of my Lord, to test me, whether I am grateful or ungrateful. He who is grateful, his gratitude is to his own credit; but he who is ungrateful—my Lord is Independent and Generous.” (Quran, 27:40)
He said, “Disguise her throne for her, and we shall see whether she will be guided, or remains one of the misguided.” (Quran, 27:41)
When she arrived, it was said, “Is your throne like this?” She said, “As if this is it.” “We were given knowledge before her, and we were submissive.” (Quran, 27:42)
But she was prevented by what she worshiped besides Allah; she belonged to a disbelieving people. (Quran, 27:43)
It was said to her, “Go inside the palace.” And when she saw it, she thought it was a deep pond, and she bared her legs. He said, “It is a palace paved with glass.” She said, “My Lord, I have done wrong to myself, and I have submitted with Solomon, to Allah, Lord of the Worlds.” (Quran, 27:44)
And We sent to Thamood their brother Saleh: “Worship Allah.” But they became two disputing factions. (Quran, 27:45)
He said, “O my people, why are you quick to do evil rather than good? If only you would seek Allah’s forgiveness, so that you may be shown mercy.” (Quran, 27:46)
They said, “We consider you an ill omen, and those with you.” He said, “Your omen is with Allah. In fact, you are a people being tested.” (Quran, 27:47)
In the city was a gang of nine who made mischief in the land and did no good. (Quran, 27:48)
They said, “Swear by Allah to one another that we will attack him and his family by night, and then tell his guardian, 'We did not witness the murder of his family, and we are being truthful.'“ (Quran, 27:49)
They planned a plan, and We planned a plan, but they did not notice. (Quran, 27:50)
So note the outcome of their planning; We destroyed them and their people, altogether. (Quran, 27:51)
Here are their homes, in ruins, on account of their iniquities. Surely in this is a sign for people who know. (Quran, 27:52)
And We saved those who believed and were pious. (Quran, 27:53)
And Lot, when he said to his people, “Do you commit lewdness with open eyes? (Quran, 27:54)
Do you lust after men instead of women? You are truly ignorant people.” (Quran, 27:55)
But the only response of his people was to say, “Expel the family of Lot from your town. They are purist people.” (Quran, 27:56)
So We saved him and his family, except for his wife, whom We destined to be among the laggards. (Quran, 27:57)
And We rained upon them a rain. Miserable was the rain of those forewarned. (Quran, 27:58)
Say, “Praise Allah, and peace be upon His servants whom He has selected. Is Allah better, or what they associate?” (Quran, 27:59)
Or, who created the heavens and the earth, and rains down water from the sky for you? With it We produce gardens full of beauty, whose trees you could not have produced. Is there another god with Allah? But they are a people who equate. (Quran, 27:60)
Or, who made the earth habitable, and made rivers flow through it, and set mountains on it, and placed a partition between the two seas? Is there another god with Allah? But most of them do not know. (Quran, 27:61)
Or, who answers the one in need when he prays to Him, and relieves adversity, and makes you successors on earth? Is there another god with Allah? How hardly you pay attention. (Quran, 27:62)
Or, who guides you through the darkness of land and sea, and who sends the winds as heralds of His mercy? Is there another god with Allah? Most exalted is Allah, above what they associate. (Quran, 27:63)
Or, who originates the creation and then repeats it, and who gives you livelihood from the sky and the earth? Is there another god with Allah? Say, “Produce your evidence, if you are truthful.” (Quran, 27:64)
Say, “No one in the heavens or on earth knows the future except Allah; and they do not perceive when they will be resurrected.” (Quran, 27:65)
In fact, their knowledge of the Hereafter is confused. In fact, they are in doubt about it. In fact, they are blind to it. (Quran, 27:66)
Those who disbelieve say, “When we have become dust, and our ancestors, shall we be brought out? (Quran, 27:67)
We were promised that before, we and our ancestors—these are nothing but legends of the ancients.” (Quran, 27:68)
Say, travel through the earth, and observe the fate of the guilty.” (Quran, 27:69)
But do not grieve over them, and do not be troubled by what they plot. (Quran, 27:70)
And they say, “When is this promise, if you are truthful?” (Quran, 27:71)
Say, “Perhaps some of what you are impatient for has drawn near.” (Quran, 27:72)
Your Lord is gracious towards humanity, but most of them are not thankful. (Quran, 27:73)
And your Lord knows what their hearts conceal, and what they reveal. (Quran, 27:74)
There is no mystery in the heaven and the earth, but it is in a Clear Book. (Quran, 27:75)
This Quran relates to the Children of Israel most of what they differ about. (Quran, 27:76)
And it is guidance and mercy for the believers. (Quran, 27:77)
Your Lord will judge between them by His wisdom. He is the Almighty, the All-Knowing. (Quran, 27:78)
So rely on Allah. You are upon the clear truth. (Quran, 27:79)
You cannot make the dead hear, nor can you make the deaf hear the call if they turn their backs and flee. (Quran, 27:80)
Nor can you guide the blind out of their straying. You can make no one listen, except those who believe in Our verses; for they are Muslims. (Quran, 27:81)
And when the Word has fallen on them, We will bring out for them from the earth a creature which will say to them that the people are uncertain of Our revelations. (Quran, 27:82)
On the Day when We gather from every community a group of those who rejected Our revelations; and they will be restrained. (Quran, 27:83)
Until, when they arrive, He will say, “Did you reject My revelations without comprehending them? Or what is it you were doing?” (Quran, 27:84)
The Word will come down upon them for their wrongdoing, and they will not speak. (Quran, 27:85)
Do they not see that We made the night for them to rest therein, and the day for visibility? Surely in that are signs for people who believe. (Quran, 27:86)
On the Day when the Trumpet is blown, everyone in the heavens and the earth will be horrified, except whomever Allah wills; and everyone will come before Him in humility. (Quran, 27:87)
And you see the mountains, and imagine them fixed, yet they pass, as the passing of the clouds—the making of Allah, who has perfected everything. He is fully Informed of what you do. (Quran, 27:88)
Whoever brings a virtue will receive better than it—and they will be safe from the horrors of that Day. (Quran, 27:89)
But whoever brings evil—their faces will be tumbled into the Fire. Will you be rewarded except for what you used to do? (Quran, 27:90)
“I was commanded to worship the Lord of this town, who has sanctified it, and to Whom everything belongs; and I was commanded to be of those who submit. (Quran, 27:91)
And to recite the Quran.” Whoever is guided—is guided to his own advantage. And whoever goes astray, then say, “I am one of the warners.” (Quran, 27:92)
And say, “Praise belongs to Allah; He will show you His signs, and you will recognize them. Your Lord is not heedless of what you do.” (Quran, 27:93)
Ta, Seen, Meem. (Quran, 28:1)
These are the Verses of the Clear Book. (Quran, 28:2)
We narrate to you from the history of Moses and Pharaoh—in truth—for people who believe. (Quran, 28:3)
Pharaoh exalted himself in the land, and divided its people into factions. He persecuted a group of them, slaughtering their sons, while sparing their daughters. He was truly a corrupter. (Quran, 28:4)
But We desired to favor those who were oppressed in the land, and to make them leaders, and to make them the inheritors. (Quran, 28:5)
And to establish them in the land; and to show Pharaoh, Hamaan, and their troops, the very thing they feared. (Quran, 28:6)
We inspired the mother of Moses: “Nurse him; then, when you fear for him, cast him into the river, and do not fear, nor grieve; We will return him to you, and make him one of the messengers.” (Quran, 28:7)
Pharaoh’s household picked him up, to be an opponent and a sorrow for them. Pharaoh, Hamaan, and their troops were sinners. (Quran, 28:8)
Pharaoh’s wife said, “An eye's delight for me and for you. Do not kill him; perhaps he will be useful to us, or we may adopt him as a son.” But they did not foresee. (Quran, 28:9)
The heart of Moses’ mother became vacant. She was about to disclose him, had We not steadied her heart, that she may remain a believer. (Quran, 28:10)
She said to his sister, “Trail him.” So she watched him from afar, and they were unaware. (Quran, 28:11)
We forbade him breastfeeding at first. So she said, “Shall I tell you about a family that can raise him for you, and will look after him?” (Quran, 28:12)
Thus We returned him to his mother, that she may be comforted, and not grieve, and know that Allah’s promise is true. But most of them do not know. (Quran, 28:13)
And when he reached his maturity, and became established, We gave him wisdom and knowledge. Thus do We reward the virtuous. (Quran, 28:14)
Once he entered the city, unnoticed by its people. He found in it two men fighting—one of his own sect, and one from his enemies. The one of his sect solicited his assistance against the one from his enemies; so Moses punched him, and put an end to him. He said, “This is of Satan's doing; he is an enemy that openly misleads.” (Quran, 28:15)
He said, “My Lord, I have wronged myself, so forgive me.” So He forgave him. He is the Forgiver, the Merciful. (Quran, 28:16)
He said, “My Lord, in as much as you have favored me, I will never be a supporter of the criminals.” (Quran, 28:17)
The next morning, he went about in the city, fearful and vigilant, when the man who had sought his assistance the day before was shouting out to him. Moses said to him, “You are clearly a troublemaker.” (Quran, 28:18)
As he was about to strike the one who was their enemy, he said, “O Moses, do you intend to kill me, as you killed someone yesterday? You only want to be a bully in the land, and do not want to be a peacemaker.” (Quran, 28:19)
And a man came from the farthest part of the city running. He said, “O Moses, the authorities are considering killing you, so leave; I am giving you good advice.” (Quran, 28:20)
So he left, fearful and vigilant. He said, “My Lord, deliver me from the wrongdoing people.” (Quran, 28:21)
As he headed towards Median, he said, “Perhaps my Lord will guide me to the right way.” (Quran, 28:22)
And when he arrived at the waters of Median, he found there a crowd of people drawing water, and he noticed two women waiting on the side. He said, “What is the matter with you?” They said, “We cannot draw water until the shepherds depart, and our father is a very old man.” (Quran, 28:23)
So he drew water for them, and then withdrew to the shade, and said, “My Lord, I am in dire need of whatever good you might send down to me.” (Quran, 28:24)
Then, one of the two women approached him, walking bashfully. She said, “My father is calling you, to reward you for drawing water for us.” And when he came to him, and told him the story, he said, “Do not fear, you have escaped from the wrongdoing people.” (Quran, 28:25)
One of the two women said, “Father, hire him; the best employee for you is the strong and trustworthy.” (Quran, 28:26)
He said, “I want to marry you to one of these two daughters of mine, provided you work for me for eight years. But if you complete ten, that is up to you. I do not intend to impose any hardship on you. You will find me, Allah willing, one of the righteous.” (Quran, 28:27)
He said, “Let this be an agreement between you and me. Whichever of the two terms I fulfill, there shall be no reprisal against me; and Allah is witness over what we say.” (Quran, 28:28)
When Moses had completed the term, and departed with his family, he noticed a fire by the side of the Mount. He said to his family, “Stay here, I have glimpsed a fire. Perhaps I can bring you some information from there, or an ember from the fire, that you may warm yourselves.” (Quran, 28:29)
When he reached it, he was called from the right side of the valley, at the Blessed Spot, from the bush: “O Moses, it is I, Allah, the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 28:30)
Throw down your staff.” And when he saw it wiggling, as if it were possessed, he turned his back to flee, and did not look back. “O Moses, come forward, and do not fear, you are perfectly safe. (Quran, 28:31)
Put your hand inside your pocket, and it will come out white, without blemish. And press your arm to your side, against fear. These are two proofs from your Lord, to Pharaoh and his dignitaries. They are truly sinful people.” (Quran, 28:32)
He said, “My Lord, I have killed one of them, and I fear they will kill me. (Quran, 28:33)
And my brother Aaron, he is more eloquent than me, so send him with me, to help me, and to confirm my words, for I fear they will reject me.” (Quran, 28:34)
He said, “We will strengthen your arm with your brother, and We will give you authority, so they will not touch you. By virtue of Our signs, you and those who follow you will be the triumphant.” (Quran, 28:35)
But when Moses came to them with Our signs, clear and manifest, they said, “This is nothing but fabricated magic, and We never heard of this from our ancestors of old.” (Quran, 28:36)
Moses said, “My Lord is well aware of him who brings guidance from Him, and him who will have the sequel of the abode. The wrongdoers will not succeed.” (Quran, 28:37)
Pharaoh said, “O nobles, I know of no god for you other than me. So fire-up the bricks for me O Hamaan, and build me a tower, that I may ascend to the Allah of Moses, though I think he is a liar.” (Quran, 28:38)
He and his troops acted arrogantly in the land, with no justification. They thought they would not be returned to Us. (Quran, 28:39)
So We seized him, and his troops, and We threw them into the sea. Observe, therefore, what was the end of the oppressors. (Quran, 28:40)
And We made them leaders calling to the Fire. And on Resurrection Day, they will not be saved. (Quran, 28:41)
And We pursued them in this world with a curse. And on Resurrection Day, they will be among the despised. (Quran, 28:42)
We gave Moses the Scripture after We had annihilated the previous generations; as an illumination for mankind, and guidance, and mercy, so that they may remember. (Quran, 28:43)
You were not on the Western Side when We decreed the command to Moses, nor were you among the witnesses. (Quran, 28:44)
But We established many generations, and time took its toll on them. Nor were you among the people of Median, reciting Our revelations to them. But We kept sending messengers. (Quran, 28:45)
Nor were you by the side of the Mount when We proclaimed. Rather, it was a mercy from your Lord, that you may warn people who received no warner before you, so that they may take heed. (Quran, 28:46)
Otherwise, if a calamity befell them as a result of what their hands have perpetrated, they would say, “Our Lord, if only You had sent us a messenger, we would have followed Your revelations, and been among the believers.” (Quran, 28:47)
But when the truth came to them from Us, they said, “If only he was given the like of what was given to Moses.” Did they not disbelieve in what was given to Moses in the past? They said, “Two works of magic backing one another.” And they said, “We are disbelieving in both.” (Quran, 28:48)
Say, “Then bring a scripture from Allah, more conductive to guidance than both, and I will follow it, if you are truthful.” (Quran, 28:49)
But if they fail to respond to you, know that they follow their fancies. And who is more lost than him who follows his fancy without guidance from Allah? Allah does not guide the unjust people. (Quran, 28:50)
We have delivered the Word to them, that they may remember. (Quran, 28:51)
Those to whom We gave the Scripture before it believe in it. (Quran, 28:52)
When it is recited to them, they say, “We have believed in it; it is the truth from our Lord; we were Muslims prior to it.” (Quran, 28:53)
These will be given their reward twice, because they persevered; and they counter evil with good; and from Our provisions to them, they give. (Quran, 28:54)
And when they hear vain talk, they avoid it, and say, “We have our deeds, and you have your deeds; peace be upon you; we do not desire the ignorant.” (Quran, 28:55)
You cannot guide whom you love, but Allah guides whom He wills, and He knows best those who are guided. (Quran, 28:56)
And they say, “If we follow the guidance with you, we will be snatched from our land.” Did We not establish for them a Safe Sanctuary, to which are brought all kinds of fruits, as provision from Ourselves? But most of them do not know. (Quran, 28:57)
And how many a city did We destroy for turning unappreciative of its livelihood? Here are their homes, uninhabited after them, except for a few. And We became the Inheritors. (Quran, 28:58)
Your Lord never destroys cities without first sending a messenger in their midst, reciting to them Our revelations. And We never destroy the cities, unless their people are wrongdoers. (Quran, 28:59)
Whatever thing you are given is but the material of this world, and its glitter. But what is with Allah is better, and longer lasting. Do you not comprehend? (Quran, 28:60)
Can someone to whom We have made a fine promise—which he will attain—be equal to someone to whom We have given enjoyments in this world, but who will be, on Resurrection Day, among the arraigned? (Quran, 28:61)
On the Day when He will call to them, and say, “Where are My associates whom you used to claim?” (Quran, 28:62)
Those against whom the sentence is justified will say, “Our Lord, these are they whom we misled. We misled them, as we were misled. We beg Your forgiveness; it was not us they used to worship.” (Quran, 28:63)
And it will be said, “Call on your partners.” And they will call on them, but they will not respond to them. And they will see the suffering. If only they were guided. (Quran, 28:64)
On the Day when He will call to them, and say, “What did you answer the Messengers?” (Quran, 28:65)
They will be blinded by the facts on that Day, and they will not question each other. (Quran, 28:66)
But he who repents, and believes, and does righteous deeds, may well be among the winners. (Quran, 28:67)
Your Lord creates whatever He wills, and He chooses. The choice is not theirs. Glory be to Allah, and exalted be He above the associations they make. (Quran, 28:68)
And your Lord knows what their hearts conceal, and what they reveal. (Quran, 28:69)
And He is Allah. There is no god but He. To Him belongs all praise in this life, and in the next. And His is the decision, and to Him you will be returned. (Quran, 28:70)
Say, “Have you considered? Had Allah made the night perpetual over you until the Day of Resurrection, which god other than Allah will bring you illumination? Do you not hear?” (Quran, 28:71)
Say, “Have you considered? Had Allah made the day perpetual over you until the Day of Resurrection, which god other than Allah will bring you night to rest in? Do you not see?” (Quran, 28:72)
It is out of His mercy that He made for you the night and the day, that you may rest in it, and seek some of His bounty; and that you may give thanks. (Quran, 28:73)
On the Day when He will call to them, and say, “Where are My associates whom you used to claim?” (Quran, 28:74)
And We will draw out from every community a witness, and say, “Produce your evidence.” Then they will realize that the truth is Allah’s, and those they used to invent have forsaken them. (Quran, 28:75)
Quaroon belonged to the clan of Moses, but he oppressed them. We had given him treasures, the keys of which would weigh down a group of strong men. His people said to him, “Do not exult; Allah does not love the exultant. (Quran, 28:76)
But seek, with what Allah has given you, the Home of the Hereafter, and do not neglect your share of this world. And be charitable, as Allah has been charitable to you. And do not seek corruption in the land. Allah does not like the seekers of corruption.” (Quran, 28:77)
He said, “I was given all this on account of knowledge I possess.” Did he not know that Allah destroyed many generations before him, who were stronger than he, and possessed greater riches? But the guilty will not be asked about their sins. (Quran, 28:78)
And he went out before his people in his splendor. Those who desired the worldly life said, “If only we possessed the likes of what Quaroon was given. He is indeed very fortunate.” (Quran, 28:79)
But those who were given knowledge said, “Woe to you! The reward of Allah is better for those who believe and do righteous deeds.” Yet none attains it except the steadfast. (Quran, 28:80)
So We caused the earth to cave in on him and his mansion. He had no company to save him from Allah, and he could not defend himself. (Quran, 28:81)
Those who had wished they were in his position the day before were saying, “Indeed, it is Allah who spreads the bounty to whomever He wills of His servants, and restricts it. Had Allah not been gracious to us, He would have caved in on us. No wonder the ungrateful never prosper.” (Quran, 28:82)
That Home of the Hereafter—We assign it for those who seek no superiority on earth, nor corruption. And the outcome is for the cautious. (Quran, 28:83)
Whoever brings a virtue will receive better than it. But whoever brings evil—the evildoers will be rewarded only according to what they used to do. (Quran, 28:84)
He Who ordained the Quran for you will return you Home. Say, “My Lord knows best who comes with guidance, and who is in manifest error.” (Quran, 28:85)
You did not expect the Scripture to be transmitted to you, except as mercy from your Lord. Therefore, do not be a supporter of the disbelievers. (Quran, 28:86)
And do not let them divert you from Allah’s revelations after they have been revealed to you. And pray to your Lord, and never be of the polytheists. (Quran, 28:87)
And do not invoke with Allah any other god. There is no god but He. All things perish, except His presence. His is the judgment, and to Him you will be returned. (Quran, 28:88)
Alif, Lam, Meem. (Quran, 29:1)
Have the people supposed that they will be left alone to say, “We believe,” without being put to the test? (Quran, 29:2)
We have tested those before them. Allah will surely know the truthful, and He will surely know the liars. (Quran, 29:3)
Or do those who commit sins think they can fool Us? Terrible is their opinion! (Quran, 29:4)
Whoever looks forward to the meeting with Allah—the appointed time of Allah is coming. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing. (Quran, 29:5)
Whoever strives, strives only for himself. Allah is Independent of the beings. (Quran, 29:6)
Those who believe and do righteous deeds—We will remit their sins, and We will reward them according to the best of what they used to do. (Quran, 29:7)
We have advised the human being to be good to his parents. But if they urge you to associate with Me something you have no knowledge of, do not obey them. To Me is your return; and I will inform you of what you used to do. (Quran, 29:8)
Those who believe and do good works—We will admit them into the company of the righteous. (Quran, 29:9)
Among the people is he who says, “We have believed in Allah.” Yet when he is harmed on Allah’s account, he equates the people's persecution with Allah’s retribution. And if help comes from your Lord, he says, “We were actually with you.” Is not Allah aware of what is inside the hearts of the people? (Quran, 29:10)
Allah certainly knows those who believe, and He certainly knows the hypocrites. (Quran, 29:11)
Those who disbelieve say to those who believe, “Follow our way, and we will carry your sins.” In no way can they carry any of their sins. They are liars. (Quran, 29:12)
They will carry their own loads, and other loads with their own. And they will be questioned on the Day of Resurrection concerning what they used to fabricate. (Quran, 29:13)
We sent Noah to his people, and He stayed among them for a thousand years minus fifty years. Then the Deluge swept them; for they were wrongdoers. (Quran, 29:14)
But We saved him, together with the company of the Ark, and We made it a sign for all peoples. (Quran, 29:15)
And Abraham, when he said to his people, “Worship Allah, and fear Him. That is better for you, if you only knew. (Quran, 29:16)
You worship idols besides Allah, and you fabricate falsehoods. Those you worship, instead of Allah, cannot provide you with livelihood. So seek your livelihood from Allah, and worship Him, and thank Him. To Him you will be returned.” (Quran, 29:17)
If you disbelieve, communities before you have also disbelieved. The Messenger is only responsible for clear transmission. (Quran, 29:18)
Have they not seen how Allah originates the creation, and then reproduces it? This is easy for Allah. (Quran, 29:19)
Say, “Roam the earth, and observe how He originated the creation.” Then Allah will bring about the next existence. Allah has power over all things.” (Quran, 29:20)
He punishes whom He wills, and He grants mercy to whom He wills, and to Him you will be restored. (Quran, 29:21)
You cannot escape, on earth or in the heaven; and you have no protector and no savior besides Allah. (Quran, 29:22)
Those who disbelieved in Allah’s signs and His encounter—these have despaired of My mercy. For them is a painful torment. (Quran, 29:23)
But the only response from his people was their saying, “Kill him, or burn him.” But Allah saved him from the fire. Surely in that are signs for people who believe. (Quran, 29:24)
And he said, “You have chosen idols instead of Allah, out of affection for one another in the worldly life. But then, on the Day of Resurrection, you will disown one another, and curse one another. Your destiny is Hell, and you will have no saviors.” (Quran, 29:25)
Then Lot believed in him, and said, “I am emigrating to my Lord. He is the Noble, the Wise.” (Quran, 29:26)
And We granted him Isaac and Jacob, and conferred on his descendants the Prophethood and the Book, and gave him his reward in this life; and in the Hereafter he will be among the upright. (Quran, 29:27)
And Lot, when he said to his people, “You are committing an obscenity not perpetrated before you by anyone in the whole world. (Quran, 29:28)
You approach men, and cut off the way, and commit lewdness in your gatherings.” But the only response from his people was to say, “Bring upon us Allah’s punishment, if you are truthful.” (Quran, 29:29)
He said, “My Lord, help me against the people of corruption.” (Quran, 29:30)
And when Our envoys brought Abraham the good news, they said, “We are going to destroy the people of this town; its people are wrongdoers.” (Quran, 29:31)
He said, “Yet Lot is in it.” They said, “We are well aware of who is in it. We will save him, and his family, except for his wife, who will remain behind.” (Quran, 29:32)
Then, when Our envoys came to Lot, they were mistreated, and he was troubled and distressed on their account. They said, “Do not fear, nor grieve. We will save you and your family, except for your wife, who will remain behind.” (Quran, 29:33)
“We will bring down upon the people of this town a scourge from heaven, because of their wickedness.” (Quran, 29:34)
And We left behind a clear trace of it, for people who understand. (Quran, 29:35)
And to Median, their brother Shuaib. He said, “O my people, worship Allah and anticipate the Last Day, and do not spread corruption in the land.” (Quran, 29:36)
But they rejected him, so the tremor overtook them, and they were left motionless in their homes. (Quran, 29:37)
And Aad and Thamood. It has become clear to you from their dwellings. Satan embellished for them their deeds, barring them from the path, even though they could see. (Quran, 29:38)
And Quaroon, and Pharaoh, and Hamaan—Moses went to them with clear arguments, but they acted arrogantly in the land. And they could not get ahead. (Quran, 29:39)
Each We seized by his sin. Against some We sent a sandstorm. Some were struck by the Blast. Some We caused the ground to cave in beneath them. And some We drowned. It was not Allah who wronged them, but it was they who wronged their own selves. (Quran, 29:40)
The likeness of those who take to themselves protectors other than Allah is that of the spider. It builds a house. But the most fragile of houses is the spider’s house. If they only knew. (Quran, 29:41)
Allah knows what they invoke besides Him. He is the Almighty, the Wise. (Quran, 29:42)
These examples—We put them forward to the people; but none grasps them except the learned. (Quran, 29:43)
Allah created the heavens and the earth with truth. Surely in that is a sign for the believers. (Quran, 29:44)
Recite what is revealed to you of the Scripture, and perform the prayer. The prayer prevents indecencies and evils. And the remembrance of Allah is greater. And Allah knows what you do. (Quran, 29:45)
And do not argue with the People of the Scripture except in the best manner possible, except those who do wrong among them. And say, “We believe in what was revealed to us, and in what was revealed to you; and our Allah and your Allah is One; and to Him we are submissive.” (Quran, 29:46)
Likewise, We revealed to you the Scripture. Those to whom We gave the Scripture believe in it, and some of these believe in it. None renounce Our communications except the disbelievers. (Quran, 29:47)
You did not read any scripture before this, nor did you write it down with your right hand; otherwise the falsifiers would have doubted. (Quran, 29:48)
In fact, it is clear signs in the hearts of those given knowledge. No one renounce Our signs except the unjust. (Quran, 29:49)
And they said, “If only a miracle from his Lord was sent down to him.” Say, “Miracles are only with Allah, and I am only a clear warner.” (Quran, 29:50)
Does it not suffice them that We revealed to you the Scripture, which is recited to them? In that is mercy and a reminder for people who believe. (Quran, 29:51)
Say, “Allah suffices as witness between you and me. He knows everything in the heavens and the Earth. Those who believe in vanity and reject Allah—it is they who are the losers.” (Quran, 29:52)
And they urge you to hasten the punishment. Were it not for a specified time, the punishment would have come to them. But it will come upon them suddenly, while they are unaware. (Quran, 29:53)
They urge you to hasten the punishment. But Hell will engulf the disbelievers. (Quran, 29:54)
On the Day when the punishment will envelop them, from above them, and from beneath their feet, He will say, “Taste what you used to do!” (Quran, 29:55)
O My servants who have believed: My earth is vast, so worship Me alone. (Quran, 29:56)
Every soul will taste death. Then to Us you will be returned. (Quran, 29:57)
Those who believe and work righteousness—We will settle them in Paradise, in mansions under which rivers flow, dwelling therein forever. Excellent is the compensation for the workers. (Quran, 29:58)
Those who endure patiently, and in their Lord they trust. (Quran, 29:59)
How many a creature there is that does not carry its provision? Allah provides for them, and for you. He is the Hearer, the Knowledgeable. (Quran, 29:60)
And if you asked them, “Who created the heavens and the earth and regulated the sun and the moon?” They would say, “Allah.” Why then do they deviate? (Quran, 29:61)
Allah expands the provision for whomever He wills of His servants, and restricts it. Allah is Cognizant of all things. (Quran, 29:62)
And if you asked them, “Who sends water down from the sky, with which He revives the earth after it had died?” They would say, “Allah.” Say, “Praise be to Allah.” But most of them do not understand. (Quran, 29:63)
The life of this world is nothing but diversion and play, and the Home of the Hereafter is the Life, if they only knew. (Quran, 29:64)
When they embark on a vessel, they pray to Allah, devoting their faith to Him; but once He has delivered them safely to land, they attribute partners to Him. (Quran, 29:65)
To be ungrateful for what We have given them, and to enjoy themselves. They will surely come to know. (Quran, 29:66)
Do they not see that We established a Secure Sanctuary, while all around them the people are being carried away? Do they believe in falsehood, and reject the blessings of Allah? (Quran, 29:67)
And who does greater wrong than he who fabricates lies and attributes them to Allah, or calls the truth a lie when it has come to him? Is there not in Hell a dwelling for the blasphemers? (Quran, 29:68)
As for those who strive for Us—We will guide them in Our ways. Allah is with the doers of good. (Quran, 29:69)
Alif, Lam, Meem. (Quran, 30:1)
The Romans have been defeated. (Quran, 30:2)
In a nearby territory. But following their defeat, they will be victorious. (Quran, 30:3)
In a few years. The matter is up to Allah, in the past, and in the future. On that day, the believers will rejoice. (Quran, 30:4)
In Allah’s support. He supports whomever He wills. He is the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 30:5)
The promise of Allah—Allah never breaks His promise, but most people do not know. (Quran, 30:6)
They know an outer aspect of the worldly life, but they are heedless of the Hereafter. (Quran, 30:7)
Do they not reflect within themselves? Allah did not create the heavens and the earth, and what is between them, except with reason, and for a specific duration. But most people, regarding meeting their Lord, are disbelievers. (Quran, 30:8)
Have they not travelled the earth and seen how those before them ended up? They were more powerful than them, and they cultivated the land and developed it more than they developed it, and their messengers came to them with clear signs. Allah would never wrong them, but they used to wrong themselves. (Quran, 30:9)
Then, evil was the end of those who committed evil. That is because they rejected Allah’s revelations, and used to ridicule them. (Quran, 30:10)
Allah originates creation, and then repeats it. Then to Him you will be returned. (Quran, 30:11)
On the Day when the Hour takes place, the guilty will despair. (Quran, 30:12)
They will have no intercessors from among their idols, and they will disown their partners. (Quran, 30:13)
On the Day when the Hour takes place—on that Day they will separate. (Quran, 30:14)
As for those who believed and did good deeds—they will be delighted in meadows. (Quran, 30:15)
But as for those who disbelieved, and rejected Our signs and the encounter of the Hereafter—those will be hauled into the torment. (Quran, 30:16)
So glorify Allah when you retire at night, and when you rise in the morning. (Quran, 30:17)
His is the praise in the heavens and on earth, and in the evening, and when you reach midday. (Quran, 30:18)
He brings the living out of the dead, and He brings the dead out of the living, and He revives the land after it had died. Likewise you will be resurrected. (Quran, 30:19)
And of His signs is that He created you from dust; and behold, you become humans spreading out. (Quran, 30:20)
And of His signs is that He created for you mates from among yourselves, so that you may find tranquility in them; and He planted love and compassion between you. In this are signs for people who reflect. (Quran, 30:21)
And of His signs is the creation of the heavens and the earth, and the diversity of your languages and colors. In this are signs for those who know. (Quran, 30:22)
And of His signs are your sleep by night and day, and your pursuit of His bounty. In this are signs for people who listen. (Quran, 30:23)
And of His signs is that He shows you the lightning, causing fear and hope. And He brings down water from the sky, and with it He revives the earth after it was dead. In this are signs for people who understand. (Quran, 30:24)
And of His signs is that the heaven and the earth stand at His disposal. And then, when He calls you out of the earth, you will emerge at once. (Quran, 30:25)
To Him belongs everyone in the heavens and the earth. All are submissive to Him. (Quran, 30:26)
It is He who initiates creation, and then repeats it, something easy for Him. His is the highest attribute, in the heavens and the earth. He is the Almighty, the Wise. (Quran, 30:27)
He illustrates an example for you, from your own selves: do you make your servants full partners in the wealth We have given you? Do you revere them as you revere one another? We thus explain the revelations for a people who understand. (Quran, 30:28)
Yet the wrongdoers follow their desires without knowledge. But who can guide whom Allah leaves astray? They will have no helpers. (Quran, 30:29)
So devote yourself to the religion of monotheism—the natural instinct Allah has instilled in mankind. There is no altering Allah’s creation. This is the true religion, but most people do not know. (Quran, 30:30)
Turning towards Him—and be conscious of Him, and perform the prayer, and do not be of the idolaters. (Quran, 30:31)
Of those who divided their religion, and became sects; each faction pleased with what they have. (Quran, 30:32)
When affliction touches the people, they call on their Lord, turning to Him in repentance. But then, when He gives them a taste of His mercy, some of them attribute partners to their Lord. (Quran, 30:33)
To show ingratitude for what We have given them. Indulge yourselves—you will surely know. (Quran, 30:34)
Have We sent down to them any authority, which speaks in support of their idols? (Quran, 30:35)
When We give people a taste of mercy, they rejoice in it. But when adversity befalls them, because of what their hands have perpetrated, they begin to despair. (Quran, 30:36)
Do they not see that Allah expands the provision for whomever He wills, or restricts it? Surely in this are signs for people who believe. (Quran, 30:37)
So give the relative his rights, and the destitute, and the wayfarer. That is best for those who seek Allah’s presence. Those are the prosperous. (Quran, 30:38)
The usury you practice, seeking thereby to multiply people’s wealth, will not multiply with Allah. But what you give in charity, desiring Allah’s approval—these are the multipliers. (Quran, 30:39)
Allah is He who created you, then provides for you, then makes you die, then brings you back to life. Can any of your idols do any of that? Glorified is He, and Exalted above what they associate. (Quran, 30:40)
Corruption has appeared on land and sea, because of what people’s hands have earned, in order to make them taste some of what they have done, so that they might return. (Quran, 30:41)
Say, “Roam the earth, and observe the fate of those who came before. Most of them were idolaters.” (Quran, 30:42)
So devote yourself to the upright religion, before there comes from Allah a Day that cannot be averted. On that Day, they will be shocked. (Quran, 30:43)
Whoever disbelieves, upon him falls his disbelief. And whoever acts righteously—they are preparing for themselves. (Quran, 30:44)
So that He may reward those who have believed and done the righteous deeds out of His bounty. Indeed, He does not love the ungrateful. (Quran, 30:45)
And of His signs is that He sends the winds bearing good news, to give you a taste of His mercy, and so that the ships may sail by His command, and so that you may seek of His bounty, and so that you may give thanks. (Quran, 30:46)
Before you, We sent messengers to their people. They came to them with clear proofs. Then We took revenge on those who sinned. It is incumbent on Us to help the believers. (Quran, 30:47)
Allah is He who sends the winds. They stir up clouds. Then He spreads them in the sky as He wills. And He breaks them apart. Then you see rain drops issuing from their midst. Then, when He makes it fall upon whom He wills of His servants, behold, they rejoice. (Quran, 30:48)
Although they were before this—before it was sent down upon them—in despair. (Quran, 30:49)
So observe the effects of Allah’s mercy—how He revives the earth after it was dead. Indeed, He is the Reviver of the dead. He is Capable of everything. (Quran, 30:50)
But if We send a wind, and they see it turning things yellow, they would continue thereafter to disbelieve. (Quran, 30:51)
You cannot make the dead hear, nor can you make the deaf hear the call when they turn away. (Quran, 30:52)
Nor can you guide the blind out of their error. You can make hear only those who believe in Our signs, and so have submitted. (Quran, 30:53)
Allah is He Who created you weak, then after weakness gave you strength, then after strength gave you weakness and gray hair. He creates whatever He wills. He is the Omniscient, the Omnipotent. (Quran, 30:54)
On the Day when the Hour takes place, the sinners will swear they had stayed but an hour. Thus they were deluded. (Quran, 30:55)
But those endowed with knowledge and faith will say, “You remained in Allah’s Book until the Day of Resurrection. This is the Day of Resurrection, but you did not know.” (Quran, 30:56)
On that Day, the sinners’ excuses will not benefit them, nor will they be excused. (Quran, 30:57)
We have cited in this Quran for the people every sort of parable. But even if you bring them a miracle, those who disbelieve will say, “You are nothing but fakers.” (Quran, 30:58)
Allah thus seals the hearts of those who do not know. (Quran, 30:59)
So be patient. The promise of Allah is true. And do not let those who lack certainty belittle you. (Quran, 30:60)
Alif, Lam, Meem. (Quran, 31:1)
These are the Verses of the Wise Book. (Quran, 31:2)
A guide and a mercy for the righteous. (Quran, 31:3)
Those who observe the prayer, and pay the obligatory charity, and are certain of the Hereafter. (Quran, 31:4)
These are upon guidance from their Lord. These are the successful. (Quran, 31:5)
Among the people is he who trades in distracting tales; intending, without knowledge, to lead away from Allah’s way, and to make a mockery of it. These will have a humiliating punishment. (Quran, 31:6)
And when Our Verses are recited to him, he turns away in pride, as though he did not hear them, as though there is deafness in his ears. So inform him of a painful punishment. (Quran, 31:7)
As for those who believe and do good deeds—for them are the Gardens of Bliss. (Quran, 31:8)
Dwelling therein forever. The promise of Allah is true. He is the Mighty, the Wise. (Quran, 31:9)
He created the heavens without pillars that you can see, and placed stabilizers on earth lest it shifts with you, and scattered throughout it all kinds of creatures. And from the sky We sent down water, and caused to grow therein of every noble pair. (Quran, 31:10)
Such is Allah’s creation. Now show me what those besides Him have created. In fact, the wicked are in obvious error. (Quran, 31:11)
We endowed Luqman with wisdom: “Give thanks to Allah.” Whoever is appreciative—is appreciative for the benefit of his own soul. And whoever is unappreciative—Allah is Sufficient and Praiseworthy. (Quran, 31:12)
When Luqman said to his son, as he advised him, “O my son, do not associate anything with Allah, for idolatry is a terrible wrong.” (Quran, 31:13)
We have entrusted the human being with the care of his parents. His mother carried him through hardship upon hardship, weaning him in two years. So give thanks to Me, and to your parents. To Me is the destination. (Quran, 31:14)
But if they strive to have you associate with Me something of which you have no knowledge, do not obey them. But keep them company in this life, in kindness, and follow the path of him who turns to Me. Then to Me is your return; and I will inform you of what you used to do. (Quran, 31:15)
“O my son, even if it were the weight of a mustard-seed, in a rock, or in the heavens, or on earth, Allah will bring it to light. Allah is Kind and Expert. (Quran, 31:16)
O my son, observe the prayer, advocate righteousness, forbid evil, and be patient over what has befallen you. These are of the most honorable traits. (Quran, 31:17)
And do not treat people with arrogance, nor walk proudly on earth. Allah does not love the arrogant showoffs. (Quran, 31:18)
And moderate your stride, and lower your voice. The most repulsive of voices is the donkey’s voice.” (Quran, 31:19)
Do you not see how Allah placed at your service everything in the heavens and the earth? How He showered you with His blessings, both outward and inward? Yet among the people is he who argues about Allah without knowledge, without guidance, and without an enlightening Scripture. (Quran, 31:20)
And when it is said to them, “Follow what Allah has revealed,” they say, “Rather, we follow what we found our parents devoted to.” Even if Satan is calling them to the suffering of the Blaze? (Quran, 31:21)
Whoever submits himself wholly to Allah, and is a doer of good, has grasped the most trustworthy handle. With Allah rests the outcome of all events. (Quran, 31:22)
Whoever disbelieves—let not his disbelief sadden you. To Us is their return. Then We will inform them of what they did. Allah knows what lies within the hearts. (Quran, 31:23)
We give them a little comfort; then We compel them to a harsh torment. (Quran, 31:24)
And if you ask them, “Who created the heavens and the earth?” They will say, “Allah.” Say, “Praise be to Allah.” But most of them do not know. (Quran, 31:25)
To Allah belongs everything in the heavens and the earth. Allah is the Rich, the Praised. (Quran, 31:26)
If all the trees on earth were pens, filled by the ocean, with seven more oceans besides, the Words of Allah would not run out. Allah is Majestic and Wise. (Quran, 31:27)
Your creation and your resurrection are only as a single soul. Allah is Hearing and Seeing. (Quran, 31:28)
Have you not seen how Allah merges the night into the day, and merges the day into the night? That He subjected the sun and the moon, each running for a stated term? And that Allah is Cognizant of everything you do? (Quran, 31:29)
That is because Allah is the Reality, and what they worship besides Him is falsehood, and because Allah is the Exalted, the Supreme. (Quran, 31:30)
Have you not seen how the ships sail through the sea, by the grace of Allah, to show you of His wonders? In that are signs for every persevering, thankful person. (Quran, 31:31)
When waves, like canopies, cover them, they call upon Allah, devoting their religion to Him. But when He has delivered them to dry land, some of them waver. No one renounces Our revelations except the treacherous blasphemer. (Quran, 31:32)
O people! Be conscious of your Lord, and dread a Day when no parent can avail his child, nor can a child avail his parent, in anything. The promise of Allah is true. Therefore, do not let this life deceive you, nor let illusions deceive you regarding Allah. (Quran, 31:33)
With Allah rests the knowledge of the Hour. He sends down the rain, and He knows what the wombs contain. No soul knows what it will reap tomorrow, and no soul knows in what land it will die. Allah is All-Knowing, Well-Informed. (Quran, 31:34)
Alif, Lam, Meem. (Quran, 32:1)
The revelation of the Book, without a doubt, is from the Lord of the Universe. (Quran, 32:2)
Yet they say, “He made it up.” In fact, it is the Truth from your Lord, to warn a people who received no warner before you, that they may be guided. (Quran, 32:3)
Allah is He who created the heavens and the earth and everything between them in six days, and then established Himself on the Throne. Apart from Him, you have no master and no intercessor. Will you not reflect? (Quran, 32:4)
He regulates all affairs, from the heavens, to the earth. Then it ascends to Him on a Day the length of which is a thousand years by your count. (Quran, 32:5)
That is the Knower of the Invisible and the Visible, the Powerful, the Merciful. (Quran, 32:6)
He who perfected everything He created, and originated the creation of man from clay. (Quran, 32:7)
Then made his reproduction from an extract of an insignificant fluid. (Quran, 32:8)
Then He proportioned him, and breathed into him of His Spirit. Then He gave you the hearing, and the eyesight, and the brains—but rarely do you give thanks. (Quran, 32:9)
And they say, “When we are lost into the earth, shall we be in a new creation?” In fact, they deny the meeting with their Lord. (Quran, 32:10)
Say, “The angel of death put in charge of you will reclaim you. Then to your Lord you will be returned.” (Quran, 32:11)
If only you could see the guilty, bowing their heads before their Lord: “Our Lord, we have seen and we have heard, so send us back, and we will act righteously; we are now convinced.” (Quran, 32:12)
Had We willed, We could have given every soul its guidance, but the declaration from Me will come true: “I will fill Hell with jinn and humans, altogether.” (Quran, 32:13)
So taste, because you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours; We have forgotten you; so taste the eternal torment for what you used to do. (Quran, 32:14)
They believe in Our communications, those who, when reminded of them, fall down prostrate, and glorify their Lord with praise, and are not proud. (Quran, 32:15)
Their sides shun their beds, as they pray to their Lord, out of reverence and hope; and from Our provisions to them, they give. (Quran, 32:16)
No soul knows what eye’s delight awaits them—a reward for what they used to do. (Quran, 32:17)
