Is someone who is faithful like someone who is a sinner? They are not equal. (Quran, 32:18)
As for those who believe and do righteous deeds, for them are the Gardens of Shelter—hospitality for what they used to do. (Quran, 32:19)
But as for those who transgressed, their shelter is the Fire. Every time they try to get out of it, they will be brought back into it, and it will be said to them, “Taste the suffering of the Fire which you used to deny.” (Quran, 32:20)
We will make them taste the lesser torment, prior to the greater torment, so that they may return. (Quran, 32:21)
Who is more wrong than he, who, when reminded of his Lord’s revelations, turns away from them? We will certainly wreak vengeance upon the criminals. (Quran, 32:22)
We gave Moses the Book; so do not be in doubt regarding His encounter; and We made it a guidance for the Children of Israel. (Quran, 32:23)
And We appointed leaders from among them, guiding by Our command, as long as they persevered and were certain of Our communications. (Quran, 32:24)
Your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection regarding everything they had disputed. (Quran, 32:25)
Is it not a lesson for them, how many generations We have destroyed before them, in whose habitations they walk? Surely in that are signs. Do they not hear? (Quran, 32:26)
Do they not see how We conduct the water to a dry land, and with it We produce vegetation, from which their livestock eat, and themselves? Do they not see? (Quran, 32:27)
And they say, “When is this victory, if you are truthful?” (Quran, 32:28)
Say, “On the day of victory, the faith of those who disbelieved will be of no avail to them, and they will not be granted respite.” (Quran, 32:29)
So turn away from them, and wait. They too are waiting. (Quran, 32:30)
O Prophet! Fear Allah, and do not obey the unbelievers and the hypocrites. Allah is Knowledgeable and Wise. (Quran, 33:1)
And follow what is revealed to you from your Lord. Allah is fully aware of what you do. (Quran, 33:2)
And put your trust in Allah. Allah is enough as a trustee. (Quran, 33:3)
Allah did not place two hearts inside any man's body. Nor did He make your wives whom you equate with your mothers, your actual mothers. Nor did He make your adopted sons, your actual sons. These are your words coming out of your mouths. Allah speaks the truth, and guides to the path. (Quran, 33:4)
Call them after their fathers; that is more equitable with Allah. But if you do not know their fathers, then your brethren in faith and your friends. There is no blame on you if you err therein, barring what your hearts premeditates. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 33:5)
The Prophet is more caring of the believers than they are of themselves, and his wives are mothers to them. And blood-relatives are closer to one another in Allah’s Book than the believers or the emigrants, though you should do good to your friends. That is inscribed in the Book. (Quran, 33:6)
Recall that We received a pledge from the prophets, and from you, and from Noah, and Abraham, and Moses, and Jesus son of Mary. We received from them a solemn pledge. (Quran, 33:7)
That He may ask the sincere about their sincerity. He has prepared for the disbelievers a painful punishment. (Quran, 33:8)
O you who believe! Remember Allah’s blessings upon you, when forces came against you, and We sent against them a wind, and forces you did not see. Allah is Observant of what you do. (Quran, 33:9)
When they came upon you, from above you, and from beneath you; and the eyes became dazed, and the hearts reached the throats, and you harbored doubts about Allah. (Quran, 33:10)
There and then the believers were tested, and were shaken most severely. (Quran, 33:11)
When the hypocrites and those in whose hearts is sickness said, “Allah and His Messenger promised us nothing but illusion.” (Quran, 33:12)
And when a group of them said, “O people of Yathrib, you cannot make a stand, so retreat.” And a faction of them asked the Prophet to excuse them, saying, “Our homes are exposed,” although they were not exposed. They only wanted to flee. (Quran, 33:13)
Had it been invaded from its sides, and they were asked to dissent, they would have done so with little hesitation. (Quran, 33:14)
Although they had made a pledge to Allah, in the past, that they will not turn their backs. A pledge to Allah is a responsibility. (Quran, 33:15)
Say, “Flight will not benefit you, if you flee from death or killing, even then you will be given only brief enjoyment.” (Quran, 33:16)
Say, “Who is it who will shield you from Allah, if He intends adversity for you, or intends mercy for you?” Besides Allah, they will find for themselves neither friend nor helper. (Quran, 33:17)
Allah already knows the hinderers among you, and those who say to their brethren, “Come and join us.” Rarely do they mobilize for battle. (Quran, 33:18)
Being stingy towards you. And when fear approaches, you see them staring at you—their eyes rolling—like someone fainting at death. Then, when panic is over, they whip you with sharp tongues. They resent you any good. These have never believed, so Allah has nullified their works; a matter easy for Allah. (Quran, 33:19)
They assumed that the confederates had not withdrawn. But were the confederates to advance, they would wish they were in the desert with the Bedouins, inquiring about your news. And if they were among you, they would have done little fighting. (Quran, 33:20)
You have an excellent example in the Messenger of Allah; for anyone who seeks Allah and the Last Day, and remembers Allah frequently. (Quran, 33:21)
And when the believers saw the confederates, they said, “This is what Allah and His messenger have promised us; and Allah and His messenger have told the truth.” And it only increased them in faith and submission. (Quran, 33:22)
Of the believers are men who are true to what they pledged to Allah. Some of them have fulfilled their vows; and some are still waiting, and never wavering. (Quran, 33:23)
That Allah may reward the truthful for their truthfulness; and punish the hypocrites, if He wills, or pardon them. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 33:24)
Allah repelled the disbelievers in their rage; they gained no advantage. Allah thus spared the believers combat. Allah is Strong and Mighty. (Quran, 33:25)
And He brought down from their strongholds those of the People of the Book who backed them, and He threw terror into their hearts. Some of them you killed, and others you took captive. (Quran, 33:26)
And He made you inherit their land, and their homes, and their possessions, and a region you have never stepped on. Allah has power over all things. (Quran, 33:27)
O Prophet! Say to your wives, “If you desire the life of this world and its finery, then let me compensate you, and release you kindly. (Quran, 33:28)
But if you desire Allah, His Messenger, and the Home of the Hereafter, then Allah has prepared for the righteous among you a magnificent compensation.” (Quran, 33:29)
O wives of the Prophet! Whoever of you commits a proven indecency, the punishment for her will be doubled. And that would be easy for Allah. (Quran, 33:30)
But whoever of you remains obedient to Allah and His Messenger, and acts righteously, We will give her a double reward; and We have prepared for her a generous provision. (Quran, 33:31)
O wives of the Prophet! You are not like any other women, if you observe piety. So do not speak too softly, lest the sick at heart lusts after you, but speak in an appropriate manner. (Quran, 33:32)
And settle in your homes; and do not display yourselves, as in the former days of ignorance. And perform the prayer, and give regular charity, and obey Allah and His Messenger. Allah desires to remove all impurity from you, O People of the Household, and to purify you thoroughly. (Quran, 33:33)
And remember what is recited in your homes of Allah's revelations and wisdom. Allah is Kind and Informed. (Quran, 33:34)
Muslim men and Muslim women, believing men and believing women, obedient men and obedient women, truthful men and truthful women, patient men and patient women, humble men and humble women, charitable men and charitable women, fasting men and fasting women, men who guard their chastity and women who guard, men who remember Allah frequently and women who remember—Allah has prepared for them a pardon, and an immense reward. (Quran, 33:35)
It is not for any believer, man or woman, when Allah and His Messenger have decided a matter, to have liberty of choice in their decision. Whoever disobeys Allah and His Messenger has gone far astray. (Quran, 33:36)
When you said to him whom Allah had blessed, and you had favored, “Keep your wife to yourself, and fear Allah.” But you hid within yourself what Allah was to reveal. And you feared the people, but it was Allah you were supposed to fear. Then, when Zaid ended his relationship with her, We gave her to you in marriage, that there may be no restriction for believers regarding the wives of their adopted sons, when their relationship has ended. The command of Allah was fulfilled. (Quran, 33:37)
There is no blame on the Prophet regarding what Allah has ordained for him. Such is the pattern of Allah among those who passed before. The command of Allah is an absolute decree. (Quran, 33:38)
Those who deliver the messages of Allah, and fear Him, and never fear anyone except Allah. Allah is sufficient as a reckoner. (Quran, 33:39)
Muhammad is not the father of any of your men; but he is the Messenger of Allah, and the seal of the prophets. Allah is Cognizant of everything. (Quran, 33:40)
O you who believe, remember Allah with frequent remembrance. (Quran, 33:41)
And glorify Him morning and evening. (Quran, 33:42)
It is He who reaches out to you, and His angels, to bring you out of darkness into the light. And He is Ever-Merciful towards the believers. (Quran, 33:43)
Their greeting on the Day they meet Him is, “Peace,” and He has prepared for them a generous reward. (Quran, 33:44)
O prophet! We have sent you as a witness, and a bearer of good news, and a warner. (Quran, 33:45)
And a caller towards Allah by His leave, and an illuminating beacon. (Quran, 33:46)
And give the believers the good news that for them is a great reward. (Quran, 33:47)
And do not obey the blasphemers and the hypocrites, and ignore their insults, and rely on Allah. Allah is a sufficient protector. (Quran, 33:48)
O you who believe! When you marry believing women, but then divorce them before you have touched them, there is no waiting period for you to observe in respect to them; but compensate them, and release them in a graceful manner. (Quran, 33:49)
O Prophet! We have permitted to you your wives to whom you have given their dowries, and those you already have, as granted to you by Allah, and the daughters of your paternal uncle, and the daughters of your paternal aunts, and the daughters of your maternal uncle, and the daughters of your maternal aunts who emigrated with you, and a believing woman who has offered herself to the Prophet, if the Prophet desires to marry her, exclusively for you, and not for the believers. We know what We have ordained for them regarding their wives and those their right-hands possess. This is to spare you any difficulty. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 33:50)
You may defer any of them you wish, and receive any of them you wish. Should you desire any of those you had deferred, there is no blame on you. This is more proper, so that they will be comforted, and not be grieved, and be content with what you have given each one of them. Allah knows what is within your hearts. Allah is Omniscient and Clement. (Quran, 33:51)
Beyond that, no other women are permissible for you, nor can you exchange them for other wives, even if you admire their beauty, except those you already have. Allah is Watchful over all things. (Quran, 33:52)
O you who believe! Do not enter the homes of the Prophet, unless you are given permission to come for a meal; and do not wait for its preparation. And when you are invited, go in. And when you have eaten, disperse, without lingering for conversation. This irritates the Prophet, and he shies away from you, but Allah does not shy away from the truth. And when you ask his wives for something, ask them from behind a screen; that is purer for your hearts and their hearts. You must never offend the Messenger of Allah, nor must you ever marry his wives after him, for that would be an enormity with Allah. (Quran, 33:53)
Whether you declare a thing, or hide it, Allah is Aware of all things. (Quran, 33:54)
There is no blame on them concerning their fathers, or their sons, or their brothers, or their brothers’ sons, or their sisters’ sons, or their women, or their female servants. But they should remain conscious of Allah. Allah is Witness over all things. (Quran, 33:55)
Allah and His angels give blessings to the Prophet. O you who believe, call for blessings on him, and greet him with a prayer of peace. (Quran, 33:56)
Those who insult Allah and His Messenger, Allah has cursed them in this life and in the Hereafter, and has prepared for them a demeaning punishment. (Quran, 33:57)
Those who harm believing men and believing women, for acts they did not commit, bear the burden of perjury and a flagrant sin. (Quran, 33:58)
O Prophet! Tell your wives, and your daughters, and the women of the believers, to lengthen their garments. That is more proper, so they will be recognized and not harassed. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 33:59)
If the hypocrites, and those with sickness in their hearts, and the rumormongers in the City, do not desist, We will incite you against them; then they will not be your neighbors there except for a short while. (Quran, 33:60)
They are cursed; wherever they are found, they should be captured and killed outright. (Quran, 33:61)
Such has been Allah’s precedent with those who passed away before. You will find no change in Allah’s system. (Quran, 33:62)
The people ask you about the Hour. Say, “The knowledge thereof rests with Allah. But what do you know? Perhaps the hour is near.” (Quran, 33:63)
Allah has cursed the disbelievers, and has prepared for them a Blaze. (Quran, 33:64)
Dwelling therein forever, not finding a protector or a savior. (Quran, 33:65)
The Day when their faces are flipped into the Fire, they will say, “If only we had obeyed Allah and obeyed the Messenger.” (Quran, 33:66)
And they will say, “Lord, we have obeyed our superiors and our dignitaries, but they led us away from the way. (Quran, 33:67)
Lord, give them double the punishment, and curse them with a great curse.” (Quran, 33:68)
O you who believe! Do not be like those who abused Moses; but Allah cleared him of what they said. He was distinguished with Allah. (Quran, 33:69)
O you who believe! Be conscious of Allah, and speak in a straightforward manner. (Quran, 33:70)
He will rectify your conduct for you, and will forgive you your sins. Whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger has won a great victory. (Quran, 33:71)
We offered the Trust to the heavens, and the earth, and the mountains; but they refused to bear it, and were apprehensive of it; but the human being accepted it. He was unfair and ignorant. (Quran, 33:72)
Allah will punish the hypocrites, men and women, and the idolaters, men and women. And Allah will redeem the believers, men and women. Allah is Ever-Forgiving, Most Merciful. (Quran, 33:73)
Praise be to Allah, to Whom belongs everything in the heavens and the earth; and praise be to Him in the Hereafter. He is the Wise, the Expert. (Quran, 34:1)
He knows what penetrates into the earth, and what comes out of it, and what descends from the sky, and what ascends to it. He is the Merciful, the Forgiving. (Quran, 34:2)
Those who disbelieve say, “The Hour will not come upon us.” Say, “Yes indeed, by my Lord, it will come upon you. He is the Knower of the unseen.” Not an atom's weight in the heavens and the earth, or anything smaller or larger, escapes His knowledge. All are in a Clear Record. (Quran, 34:3)
That He may recompense those who believe and do good works. Those will have forgiveness, and a generous provision. (Quran, 34:4)
As for those who strive against Our revelations, seeking to undermine them—for them is a punishment of a painful plague. (Quran, 34:5)
Those who received knowledge know that what is revealed to you from your Lord is the truth; and it guides to the path of the Majestic, the Praiseworthy. (Quran, 34:6)
Those who disbelieved said, “Shall we point out to you a man, who will tell you that, once torn into shreds, you will be in a new creation? (Quran, 34:7)
Did he invent a lie about Allah, or is there madness in him?” Indeed, those who do not believe in the Hereafter are in torment, and far astray. (Quran, 34:8)
Do they not reflect upon what lies before them and behind them, of the heaven and the earth? If We will, We can make the earth cave in beneath them, or make pieces of the sky fall down on them. In that is a sign for every devout servant. (Quran, 34:9)
We bestowed upon David favor from Us: “O mountains, and birds: echo with him.” And We softened iron for him. (Quran, 34:10)
“Make coats of armor, and measure the links well; and work righteousness. I am Observant of everything you do.” (Quran, 34:11)
And for Solomon the wind—its outward journey was one month, and its return journey was one month. And We made a spring of tar flow for him. And there were sprites that worked under him, by the leave of his Lord. But whoever of them swerved from Our command, We make him taste of the punishment of the Inferno. (Quran, 34:12)
They made for him whatever he wished: sanctuaries, statues, bowls like pools, and heavy cauldrons. “O House of David, work with appreciation,” but a few of My servants are appreciative. (Quran, 34:13)
Then, when We decreed death for him, nothing indicated his death to them except an earthworm eating at his staff. Then, when he fell down, it became clear to the sprites that, had they known the unseen, they would not have remained in the demeaning torment. (Quran, 34:14)
In Sheba’s homeland there used to be a wonder: two gardens, on the right, and on the left. “Eat of your Lord’s provision, and give thanks to Him.” A good land, and a forgiving Lord. (Quran, 34:15)
But they turned away, so We unleashed against them the flood of the dam; and We substituted their two gardens with two gardens of bitter fruits, thorny shrubs, and meager harvest. (Quran, 34:16)
We thus penalized them for their ingratitude. Would We penalize any but the ungrateful? (Quran, 34:17)
Between them and the towns We had blessed, We placed prominent towns, and We made the travel between them easy. “Travel between them by night and day, in safety.” (Quran, 34:18)
But they said, “Our Lord, lengthen the distances of our journeys.” They wronged themselves; so We made them history, and We scattered them in every direction. In this are lessons for every steadfast and appreciative person. (Quran, 34:19)
Satan was correct in his assessment of them. They followed him, except for a group of believers. (Quran, 34:20)
He had no authority over them; except that We willed to distinguish him who believes in the Hereafter, from him who is doubtful about it. Your Lord is Guardian over all things. (Quran, 34:21)
Say, “Call upon those whom you claim besides Allah. They possess not an atom's weight in the heavens or the earth, and they possess no share of either, and He has no backers from among them.” (Quran, 34:22)
Intercession with Him is of no value, except for someone He has permitted. Until, when fear has subsided from their hearts, they will say, “What did your Lord say?” They will say, “The truth, and He is the High, the Great.” (Quran, 34:23)
Say, “Who provides for you from the heavens and the earth?” Say, “Allah. And Either you, or we, are rightly guided, or in evident error.” (Quran, 34:24)
Say, “You will not be asked about our misdeeds, nor will we be asked about what you do.” (Quran, 34:25)
Say, “Our Lord will bring us together; then He will judge between us equitably. He is the All-Knowing Judge.” (Quran, 34:26)
Say, “Show me those you have attached to Him as associates. No indeed! But He is Allah, the Powerful, the Wise.” (Quran, 34:27)
We sent you only universally to all people, a herald and warner, but most people do not know. (Quran, 34:28)
And they say, “When is this promise due, if you are truthful?” (Quran, 34:29)
Say, “You are promised a Day, which you cannot postpone by one hour, nor bring forward.” (Quran, 34:30)
Those who disbelieve say, “We will never believe in this Quran, nor in what came before it.” If you could only see the wrongdoers, captive before their Lord, throwing back allegations at one another. Those who were oppressed will say to those who were arrogant, “Were it not for you, we would have been believers.” (Quran, 34:31)
Those who were arrogant will say to those who were oppressed, “Was it us who turned you away from guidance when it came to you? No indeed, you yourselves were sinful.” (Quran, 34:32)
And those who were oppressed will say to those who were arrogant, “It was your scheming by night and day; as you instructed us to reject Allah, and to set up rivals to Him.” They will hide their remorse when they see the retribution. We will put yokes around the necks of those who disbelieved. Will they be repaid for anything other than what they used to do? (Quran, 34:33)
We sent no warner to any town, without its affluent saying, “We reject what you are sent with.” (Quran, 34:34)
And they say, “We have more wealth and more children, and we will not be punished.” (Quran, 34:35)
Say, “My Lord spreads out His bounty to whomever He wills, or restricts it; but most people do not know.” (Quran, 34:36)
It is neither your wealth nor your children that bring you closer to Us, but it is he who believes and does good deeds. These will have a double reward for what they did; and they will reside in the Chambers, in peace and security. (Quran, 34:37)
But those who work against Our revelations, seeking to undermine them—those will be summoned to the punishment. (Quran, 34:38)
Say, “My Lord extends the provision to whomever He wills of His servants, or withholds it. Anything you spend, He will replace it. He is the Best of providers.” (Quran, 34:39)
On the Day when He gathers them all together, then say to the angels, “Was it you these used to worship?” (Quran, 34:40)
They will say, “Be You glorified; You are our Master, not them. In fact, they used to worship the jinn, and most of them had faith in them.” (Quran, 34:41)
“Today, none of you has the power to profit or harm the other.” And We will say to those who did wrong, “Taste the agony of the Fire which you used to deny.” (Quran, 34:42)
And when Our enlightening Verses are recited to them, they say, “This is nothing but a man who wants to divert you from what your ancestors used to worship.” And they say, “This is nothing but a fabricated lie.” And when the Truth comes to them, the blasphemers say of the Truth, “This is nothing but plain magic.” (Quran, 34:43)
But We gave them no book to study, and We did not send them any warner before you. (Quran, 34:44)
Those before them also denied the Truth, yet they have not attained one-tenth of what We had given them. They rejected My messengers, so how was My disapproval? (Quran, 34:45)
Say, “I offer you a single advice: devote yourselves to Allah, in pairs, or individually; and reflect. There is no madness in your friend. He is just a warner to you, before the advent of a severe punishment.” (Quran, 34:46)
Say, “Whatever compensation I have asked of you, is yours. My compensation comes only from Allah, and He is Witness over all things.” (Quran, 34:47)
Say, “My Lord projects the truth. He is the Knower of the Unseen.” (Quran, 34:48)
Say, “The Truth has come; while falsehood can neither originate, nor regenerate.” (Quran, 34:49)
Say, “If I err, I err only to my own loss; but if I am guided, it is by what my Lord inspires me. He is Hearing and Near.” (Quran, 34:50)
If you could only see when they are terrified, and there is no escape, and they are seized from a nearby place. (Quran, 34:51)
And they say, “We have believed in it.” But how can they attain it from a distant place? (Quran, 34:52)
They have rejected it in the past, and made allegations from a far-off place. (Quran, 34:53)
A barrier will be placed between them and what they desire, as was done formerly with their counterparts. They were in disturbing doubt. (Quran, 34:54)
Praise be to Allah, Originator of the heavens and the earth, Maker of the angels messengers with wings—double, triple, and quadruple. He adds to creation as He wills. Allah is Able to do all things. (Quran, 35:1)
Whatever mercy Allah unfolds for the people, none can withhold it. And if He withholds it, none can release it thereafter. He is the Exalted in Power, Full of Wisdom. (Quran, 35:2)
O people! Remember Allah’s blessings upon you. Is there a creator other than Allah who provides for you from the heaven and the earth? There is no god but He. So how are you misled? (Quran, 35:3)
If they reject you, messengers before you were also rejected. To Allah all matters are returned. (Quran, 35:4)
O people! The promise of Allah is true; so let not the lowly life seduce you, and let not the Tempter tempt you away from Allah. (Quran, 35:5)
Satan is an enemy to you, so treat him as an enemy. He only invites his gang to be among the inmates of the Inferno. (Quran, 35:6)
Those who disbelieve will suffer a harsh punishment, but those who believe and do righteous deeds will have forgiveness and a great reward. (Quran, 35:7)
What of him whose evil deed was made attractive to him, and so he regards it as good? Allah leads astray whomever He wills, and He guides whomever He wills. Therefore, do not waste yourself sorrowing over them. Allah knows exactly what they do. (Quran, 35:8)
Allah is He who sends the winds, which agitate clouds, which We drive to a dead land, and thereby revive the ground after it had died. Likewise is the Resurrection. (Quran, 35:9)
Whoever desires honor—all honor belongs to Allah. To Him ascends speech that is pure, and He elevates righteous conduct. As for those who plot evil, a terrible punishment awaits them, and the planning of these will fail. (Quran, 35:10)
Allah created you from dust, then from a small drop; then He made you pairs. No female conceives, or delivers, except with His knowledge. No living thing advances in years, or its life is shortened, except it be in a Record. That is surely easy for Allah. (Quran, 35:11)
The two seas are not the same. One is fresh, sweet, good to drink, while the other is salty and bitter. Yet from each you eat tender meat, and extract jewelry which you wear. And you see the ships plowing through them, so that you may seek of His bounty, so that you may give thanks. (Quran, 35:12)
He merges the night into the day, and He merges the day into the night; and He regulates the sun and the moon, each running for a stated term. Such is Allah, your Lord; His is the sovereignty. As for those you call upon besides Him, they do not possess a speck. (Quran, 35:13)
If you pray to them, they cannot hear your prayer. And even if they heard, they would not answer you. And on the Day of Resurrection, they will reject your partnership. None informs you like an Expert. (Quran, 35:14)
O people! It is you who are the poor, in need of Allah; while Allah is the Rich, the Praiseworthy. (Quran, 35:15)
If He wills, He can do away with you, and produce a new creation. (Quran, 35:16)
And that would not be difficult for Allah. (Quran, 35:17)
No burdened soul can carry the burden of another. Even if one weighted down calls for help with its burden, nothing can be lifted from it, even if they were related. You are to warn those who fear their Lord inwardly, and perform the prayer. He who purifies himself purifies himself for his own good. To Allah is the ultimate return. (Quran, 35:18)
Not equal are the blind and the seeing. (Quran, 35:19)
Nor are the darkness and the light. (Quran, 35:20)
Nor are the shade and the torrid heat. (Quran, 35:21)
Nor are equal the living and the dead. Allah causes whomever He wills to hear, but you cannot make those in the graves hear. (Quran, 35:22)
You are only a warner. (Quran, 35:23)
We sent you with the truth; a bearer of good news, and a warner. There is no community but a warner has passed through it. (Quran, 35:24)
If they disbelieve you, those before them also disbelieved. Their messengers came to them with the clear proofs, with the Psalms, and with the Enlightening Scripture. (Quran, 35:25)
Then I seized those who disbelieved—so how was My rejection? (Quran, 35:26)
Have you not seen that Allah sends down water from the sky? With it We produce fruits of various colors. And in the mountains are streaks of white and red—varying in their hue—and pitch-black. (Quran, 35:27)
Likewise, human beings, animals, and livestock come in various colors. From among His servants, the learned fear Allah. Allah is Almighty, Oft-Forgiving. (Quran, 35:28)
Those who recite the Book of Allah, and perform the prayer, and spend of what We have provided for them, secretly and publicly, expect a trade that will not fail. (Quran, 35:29)
He will pay them their dues in full, and will increase them from His bounty. He is Forgiving and Appreciative. (Quran, 35:30)
What We inspired in you, of the Book, is the truth, confirming what preceded it. Allah is Well-Informed of His servants, All-Seeing. (Quran, 35:31)
Then We passed the Book to those of Our servants whom We chose. Some of them wrong their souls, and some follow a middle course, and some are in the foremost in good deeds by Allah’s leave; that is the greatest blessing. (Quran, 35:32)
The Gardens of Eden, which they will enter. They will be adorned therein with gold bracelets and pearls, and their garments therein will be of silk. (Quran, 35:33)
And they will say, “Praise Allah, who has lifted all sorrow from us. Our Lord is Most Forgiving, Most Appreciative. (Quran, 35:34)
He Who settled us in the Home of Permanence, by His grace, where boredom will not touch us, and fatigue will not afflict us.” (Quran, 35:35)
As for those who disbelieve, for them is the Fire of Hell, wherein they will never be finished off and die, nor will its punishment be lightened for them. Thus We will repay every ingrate. (Quran, 35:36)
And they will scream therein, “Our Lord, let us out, and we will act righteously, differently from the way we used to act.” Did We not give you a life long enough, in which anyone who wanted to understand would have understood? And the warner did come to you. So taste. The evildoers will have no helper. (Quran, 35:37)
Allah is the Knower of the future of the heavens and the earth. He knows what the hearts contain. (Quran, 35:38)
It is He who made you successors on earth. Whoever disbelieves, his disbelief will recoil upon him. The disbelief of the disbelievers adds only to their Lord's disfavor of them. The disbelief of the disbelievers adds only to their perdition. (Quran, 35:39)
Say, “Have you considered those partners of yours that you worship instead of Allah? Show me what they have created on earth. Or do they have any share in the heavens?” Or have We given them a book whose clear teachings they follow? In fact, the wrongdoers promise one another nothing but delusions. (Quran, 35:40)
Allah holds the heavens and the earth, lest they fall apart. And were they to fall apart, there is none to hold them together except He. He is Most Clement, Most Forgiving. (Quran, 35:41)
And they swore by Allah with their solemn oaths, that if a warner came to them, they would be more guided than any other people. Yet when a warner came to them, it only increased them in aversion. (Quran, 35:42)
Priding themselves on earth, and scheming evil. But evil scheming overwhelms none but its authors. Do they expect anything but the precedent of the ancients? You will not find any change in Allah’s practice, and you will not find any substitute to Allah’s practice. (Quran, 35:43)
Have they not journeyed in the land and observed the fate of those who preceded them? They were superior to them in strength. But nothing can defeat Allah in the heavens or on Earth. He is indeed Omniscient and Omnipotent. (Quran, 35:44)
If Allah were to punish the people for what they have earned, He would not leave a single living creature on its surface. But He defers them until a stated time. Then, when their time has arrived—Allah is Observant of His creatures. (Quran, 35:45)
Ya, Seen. (Quran, 36:1)
By the Wise Quran. (Quran, 36:2)
You are one of the messengers. (Quran, 36:3)
On a straight path. (Quran, 36:4)
The revelation of the Almighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 36:5)
To warn a people whose ancestors were not warned, and so they are unaware. (Quran, 36:6)
The Word was realized against most of them, for they do not believe. (Quran, 36:7)
We placed shackles around their necks, up to their chins, so they are stiff-necked. (Quran, 36:8)
And We placed a barrier in front of them, and a barrier behind them, and We have enshrouded them, so they cannot see. (Quran, 36:9)
It is the same for them, whether you warn them, or do not warn them—they will not believe. (Quran, 36:10)
You warn only him who follows the Message, and fears the Most Gracious inwardly. So give him good news of forgiveness, and a generous reward. (Quran, 36:11)
It is We who revive the dead; and We write down what they have forwarded, and their traces. We have tallied all things in a Clear Record. (Quran, 36:12)
And cite for them the parable of the landlords of the town—when the messengers came to it. (Quran, 36:13)
We sent them two messengers, but they denied them both, so We reinforced them with a third. They said, “We are messengers to you.” (Quran, 36:14)
They said, “You are nothing but humans like us, and the Gracious did not send down anything; you are only lying.” (Quran, 36:15)
They said, “Our Lord knows that we are messengers to you. (Quran, 36:16)
And our only duty is clear communication.” (Quran, 36:17)
They said, “We see an evil omen in you; if you do not give up, we will stone you, and a painful punishment from us will befall you.” (Quran, 36:18)
They said, “Your evil omen is upon you. Is it because you were reminded? But you are an extravagant people.” (Quran, 36:19)
Then a man came running from the remotest part of the city. He said, “O my people, follow the messengers. (Quran, 36:20)
Follow those who ask you of no wage, and are themselves guided. (Quran, 36:21)
“And why should I not worship Him Who created me, and to Whom you will be returned? (Quran, 36:22)
Shall I take other gods instead of Him? If the Merciful desires harm for me, their intercession will not avail me at all, nor will they save me. (Quran, 36:23)
In that case, I would be completely lost. (Quran, 36:24)
I have believed in your Lord, so listen to me.” (Quran, 36:25)
It was said, “Enter Paradise.” He said, “If only my people knew. (Quran, 36:26)
How my Lord has forgiven me, and made me one of the honored.” (Quran, 36:27)
After him, We sent down no hosts from heaven to his people; nor would We ever send any down. (Quran, 36:28)
It was just one Cry, and they were stilled. (Quran, 36:29)
Alas for the servants. No messenger ever came to them, but they ridiculed him. (Quran, 36:30)
Have they not considered how many generations We destroyed before them; and that unto them they will not return? (Quran, 36:31)
All of them, every single one of them, will be arraigned before Us. (Quran, 36:32)
And there is a sign for them in the dead land: We give it life, and produce from it grains from which they eat. (Quran, 36:33)
And We place in it gardens of palm-trees and vines, and cause springs to gush out of it. (Quran, 36:34)
That they may eat from its fruits, although their hands did not make it. Will they not be appreciative? (Quran, 36:35)
Glory be to Him who created all the pairs; of what the earth produces, and of their own selves, and of what they do not know. (Quran, 36:36)
Another sign for them is the night: We strip the day out of it—and they are in darkness. (Quran, 36:37)
And the sun runs towards its destination. Such is the design of the Almighty, the All-Knowing. (Quran, 36:38)
And the moon: We have disposed it in phases, until it returns like the old twig. (Quran, 36:39)
The sun is not to overtake the moon, nor is the night to outpace the day. Each floats in an orbit. (Quran, 36:40)
Another sign for them is that We carried their offspring in the laden Ark. (Quran, 36:41)
And We created for them the like of it, in which they ride. (Quran, 36:42)
If We will, We can drown them—with no screaming to be heard from them, nor will they be saved. (Quran, 36:43)
Except by a mercy from Us, and enjoyment for a while. (Quran, 36:44)
Yet when it is said to them, “Beware of what lies before you, and what lies behind you, that you may receive mercy.” (Quran, 36:45)
Yet never came to them a sign of their Lord’s signs, but they turned away from it. (Quran, 36:46)
And when it is said to them, “Spend of what Allah has provided for you,” those who disbelieve say to those who believe, “Shall we feed someone whom Allah could feed, if He so willed? You must be deeply misguided.” (Quran, 36:47)
And they say, “When will this promise be, if you are truthful?” (Quran, 36:48)
All they can expect is a single blast, which will seize them while they feud. (Quran, 36:49)
They will not be able to make a will, nor will they return to their families. (Quran, 36:50)
The Trumpet will be blown, then behold, they will rush from the tombs to their Lord. (Quran, 36:51)
They will say, “Woe to us! Who resurrected us from our resting-place?” This is what the Most Gracious had promised, and the messengers have spoken the truth.” (Quran, 36:52)
It will be but a single scream; and behold, they will all be brought before Us. (Quran, 36:53)
On that Day, no soul will be wronged in the least, and you will be recompensed only for what you used to do. (Quran, 36:54)
The inhabitants of Paradise, on that Day, will be happily busy. (Quran, 36:55)
They and their spouses, in shades, reclining on couches. (Quran, 36:56)
They will have therein fruits. They will have whatever they call for. (Quran, 36:57)
Peace—a saying from a Most Merciful Lord. (Quran, 36:58)
But step aside today, you criminals. (Quran, 36:59)
Did I not covenant with you, O Children of Adam, that you shall not serve the devil? That he is your sworn enemy? (Quran, 36:60)
And that you shall serve Me? This is a straight path. (Quran, 36:61)
He has misled a great multitude of you. Did you not understand? (Quran, 36:62)
This is Hellfire, which you were promised. (Quran, 36:63)
Roast in it today, because you persistently disbelieved. (Quran, 36:64)
On this Day, We will seal their mouths, and their hands will speak to Us, and their feet will testify to everything they had done. (Quran, 36:65)
If We will, We can blind their eyes as they rush towards the path—but how will they see? (Quran, 36:66)
And if We will, We can cripple them in their place; so they can neither move forward, nor go back. (Quran, 36:67)
Whomever We grant old age, We reverse his development. Do they not understand? (Quran, 36:68)
We did not teach him poetry, nor is it proper for him. It is only a reminder, and a Clear Quran. (Quran, 36:69)
That he may warn whoever is alive, and prove the Word against the faithless. (Quran, 36:70)
Have they not seen that We created for them, of Our Handiwork, livestock that they own? (Quran, 36:71)
And We subdued them for them. Some they ride, and some they eat. (Quran, 36:72)
And they have in them other benefits, and drinks. Will they not give thanks? (Quran, 36:73)
Yet they have taken to themselves gods other than Allah, that perhaps they may be helped. (Quran, 36:74)
They cannot help them, although they are arrayed as troops for them. (Quran, 36:75)
So let their words not sadden you. We know what they conceal, and what they reveal. (Quran, 36:76)
Does the human being not consider that We created him from a seed? Yet he becomes a fierce adversary. (Quran, 36:77)
And he produces arguments against Us, and he forgets his own creation. He says, “Who will revive the bones when they have decayed?” (Quran, 36:78)
Say, “He who initiated them in the first instance will revive them. He has knowledge of every creation.” (Quran, 36:79)
He who produced fuel for you from the green trees, with which you kindle a fire. (Quran, 36:80)
Is not He who created the heavens and the earth able to create the like of them? Certainly. He is the Supreme All-Knowing Creator. (Quran, 36:81)
His command, when He wills a thing, is to say to it, “Be,” and it comes to be. (Quran, 36:82)
So glory be to Him in whose hand is the dominion of everything, and to Him you will be returned. (Quran, 36:83)
By the aligners aligning. (Quran, 37:1)
And the drivers driving. (Quran, 37:2)
And the reciters of the Reminder. (Quran, 37:3)
Your Allah is indeed One. (Quran, 37:4)
Lord of the heavens and the earth, and everything between them; and Lord of the Easts. (Quran, 37:5)
We have adorned the lower heaven with the beauty of the planets. (Quran, 37:6)
And guarded it against every defiant devil. (Quran, 37:7)
They cannot eavesdrop on the Supernal Elite, for they get bombarded from every side. (Quran, 37:8)
Repelled—they will have a lingering torment. (Quran, 37:9)
Except for him who snatches a fragment—he gets pursued by a piercing projectile. (Quran, 37:10)
Inquire of them, “Are they more difficult to create, or the others We created?” We created them from sticky clay. (Quran, 37:11)
But you wonder, and they ridicule. (Quran, 37:12)
And when reminded, they pay no attention. (Quran, 37:13)

Say, “Yes indeed, and you will be totally subdued.” (Quran, 37:18)
It will be a single nudge, and they will be staring. (Quran, 37:19)
They will say, “Woe to us. This is the Day of Judgment.” (Quran, 37:20)
“This is the Day of Separation which you used to deny. (Quran, 37:21)
Gather those who did wrong, and their mates, and what they used to worship. (Quran, 37:22)
Besides Allah, and lead them to the way to Hell. (Quran, 37:23)
And stop them. They are to be questioned.” (Quran, 37:24)
What is the matter with you? Why do you not help one another? (Quran, 37:25)
In fact, on that Day, they will be submissive. (Quran, 37:26)
They will come to one another, questioning one another. (Quran, 37:27)
They will say, “You used to come at us from the right.” (Quran, 37:28)
They will say, “You yourselves were not believers. (Quran, 37:29)
We had no authority over you. You yourselves were rebellious people. (Quran, 37:30)
The Word of our Lord has been realized against us. We are tasting it. (Quran, 37:31)
We seduced you. We were seducers.” (Quran, 37:32)
On that Day, they will share in the punishment. (Quran, 37:33)
Thus We deal with the sinners. (Quran, 37:34)
When it was said to them, “There is no god except Allah,” they grew arrogant. (Quran, 37:35)
And said, “Are we to abandon our gods for a mad poet?” (Quran, 37:36)
In fact, he came with the truth, and he confirmed the messengers. (Quran, 37:37)
Most assuredly, you will taste the painful punishment. (Quran, 37:38)
And you will be repaid only for what you used to do. (Quran, 37:39)
Except for Allah’s sincere servants. (Quran, 37:40)
For them is a known provision. (Quran, 37:41)
Fruits; and they will be honored. (Quran, 37:42)
In the Gardens of Bliss. (Quran, 37:43)
On furnishings, facing one another. (Quran, 37:44)
They will be offered a cup of pure drink. (Quran, 37:45)
White; a delight to those who drink. (Quran, 37:46)
Never polluted, and never intoxicating. (Quran, 37:47)
With them will be bashful women with lovely eyes. (Quran, 37:48)
As if they were closely guarded pearls. (Quran, 37:49)
Then they will approach one another, questioning. (Quran, 37:50)
One of them will say, “I used to have a friend. (Quran, 37:51)
Who used to say, “Are you of those who believe? (Quran, 37:52)
That after we die and become dust and bones, we will be called to account?” (Quran, 37:53)
He will say, “Will you have a look?” (Quran, 37:54)
He will look, and will see him in the pit of Hell. (Quran, 37:55)
He will say, “By Allah, you almost ruined me. (Quran, 37:56)
Were it not for the grace of my Lord, I would have been among the arraigned.” (Quran, 37:57)
“We will not die. (Quran, 37:58)
Except for our first death, and we will not be punished.” (Quran, 37:59)
This is the supreme triumph. (Quran, 37:60)
For the like of this let the workers work. (Quran, 37:61)
Is this a better hospitality, or the Tree of Bitterness? (Quran, 37:62)
We made it an ordeal for the unjust. (Quran, 37:63)
It is a tree that grows from the bottom of Hell. (Quran, 37:64)
Its fruits are like the devils’ heads. (Quran, 37:65)
They will eat from it, and fill their bellies with it. (Quran, 37:66)
Then, on top of it, they will have a brew of boiling liquid. (Quran, 37:67)
Then their return will be to the Blaze. (Quran, 37:68)
They had found their parents astray. (Quran, 37:69)
And rushed along in their footsteps. (Quran, 37:70)
And most of the ancients before them went astray. (Quran, 37:71)
Even though We sent messengers to warn them. (Quran, 37:72)
So observe the end of those who were warned. (Quran, 37:73)
Except for the sincere servants of Allah. (Quran, 37:74)
And Noah called out to Us, and We are the Best of responders. (Quran, 37:75)
And We saved him and his family from the great calamity. (Quran, 37:76)
And We made his descendants the survivors. (Quran, 37:77)
And We left mention of him among those who succeeded. (Quran, 37:78)
Peace be upon Noah among all people. (Quran, 37:79)
We thus reward the righteous. (Quran, 37:80)
He was one of Our believing servants. (Quran, 37:81)
Then We drowned the others. (Quran, 37:82)
Of his kind was Abraham. (Quran, 37:83)
When he came to his Lord with a sound heart. (Quran, 37:84)
He said to his father and his people, “What are you worshiping? (Quran, 37:85)
Is it falsified gods, instead of Allah, that you want? (Quran, 37:86)

And said, “I am sick.” (Quran, 37:89)
But they turned their backs on him, and went away. (Quran, 37:90)

And they came running towards him. (Quran, 37:94)

Then, when they had submitted, and he put his forehead down. (Quran, 37:103)

This was certainly an evident test. (Quran, 37:106)

Saad. By the renowned Quran. (Quran, 38:1)
Those who disbelieve are steeped in arrogance and defiance. (Quran, 38:2)
How many generations have We destroyed before them? They cried out when it was too late to escape. (Quran, 38:3)
And they marveled that a warner has come to them from among them. The disbelievers said, “This is a lying magician.” (Quran, 38:4)
“Did he turn all the gods into one Allah? This is something strange.” (Quran, 38:5)
The notables among them announced: “Go on, and hold fast to your gods. This is something planned. (Quran, 38:6)
We never heard of this in the former faith. This is nothing but a fabrication. (Quran, 38:7)
Was the message sent down to him, out of all of us?” In fact, they are doubtful of My warning. In fact, they have not yet tasted My punishment. (Quran, 38:8)
Or do they possess the treasuries of the mercy of your Lord—the Majestic, the Giver? (Quran, 38:9)
Or do they possess the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth and what is between them? Then let them ascend the ropes. (Quran, 38:10)
An army of confederates will be defeated there. (Quran, 38:11)
Before them the people of Noah denied the truth; as did Aad, and Pharaoh of the Stakes. (Quran, 38:12)
And Thamood, and the people of Lot, and the dwellers of the Woods—these were the confederates. (Quran, 38:13)
None of them but denied the messengers, so My retribution was deserved. (Quran, 38:14)
These can expect only a single scream, from which there is no recovery. (Quran, 38:15)
And they say, “Our Lord, hasten Your writ upon us, before the Day of Account.” (Quran, 38:16)
Be patient in the face of what they say, and mention Our servant David, the resourceful. He was obedient. (Quran, 38:17)
We committed the mountains to glorify with him, in the evening and at daybreak. (Quran, 38:18)
And the birds, gathered together. All obedient to him. (Quran, 38:19)
And We strengthened his kingdom, and gave him wisdom and decisive speech. (Quran, 38:20)
Has the story of the two disputants reached you? When they scaled the sanctuary? (Quran, 38:21)
When they entered upon David, and he was startled by them. They said, “Do not fear. Two disputants; one of us has wronged the other; so judge between us fairly, and do not be biased, and guide us to the straight way.” (Quran, 38:22)
“This brother of mine has ninety-nine ewes, and I have one ewe, and he said, ‘Entrust it to me,’ and he pressured me with words.” (Quran, 38:23)
He said, “He has done you wrong by asking your ewe in addition to his ewes. Many partners take advantage of one another, except those who believe and do good deeds, but these are so few.” David realized that We were testing him, so he sought forgiveness from his Lord, and fell down to his knees, and repented. (Quran, 38:24)
So We forgave him that. And for him is nearness to Us, and a good place of return. (Quran, 38:25)
“O David, We made you a ruler in the land, so judge between the people with justice, and do not follow desire, lest it diverts you from Allah’s path. Those who stray from Allah’s path will have a painful punishment, for having ignored the Day of Account.” (Quran, 38:26)
We did not create the heaven and the earth and everything between them in vain. That is the assumption of those who disbelieve—so woe to those who disbelieve because of the Fire. (Quran, 38:27)
Or are We to treat those who believe and do righteous deeds like those who make trouble on earth? Or are We to treat the pious like the shameless? (Quran, 38:28)
A blessed Book that We sent down to you, that they may ponder its Verses, and for those with intelligence to take heed. (Quran, 38:29)
And We granted David, Solomon, an excellent servant. He was penitent. (Quran, 38:30)
When the beautiful horses were paraded before him in the evening. (Quran, 38:31)
He said, “I have preferred the love of niceties to the remembrance of my Lord—until it disappeared behind the veil. (Quran, 38:32)
Bring them back to me.” And he began caressing their legs and necks. (Quran, 38:33)
We tested Solomon, and placed a body on his throne; then he repented. (Quran, 38:34)
He said, “My Lord, forgive me, and grant me a kingdom never to be attained by anyone after me. You are the Giver.” (Quran, 38:35)
So We placed the wind at his service, blowing gently by his command, wherever he directed. (Quran, 38:36)
And the demons—every builder and diver. (Quran, 38:37)
And others fettered in chains. (Quran, 38:38)
“This is Our gift; so give generously, or withhold; without account.” (Quran, 38:39)
For him is nearness to Us, and a beautiful resort. (Quran, 38:40)
And mention Our servant Job, when he called out to his Lord, “Satan has afflicted me with hardship and pain.” (Quran, 38:41)
“Stamp with your foot—here is cool water to wash with, and to drink.” (Quran, 38:42)
And We restored his family for him, and their like with them; as a mercy from Us, and a lesson for those who possess insight. (Quran, 38:43)
“Take with your hand a bundle, and strike with it, and do not break your oath.” We found him patient. What an excellent servant! He was obedient. (Quran, 38:44)
And mention Our servants Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob—endowed with ability and vision. (Quran, 38:45)
We distinguished them with a distinct quality: the remembrance of the Home. (Quran, 38:46)
To Us they are among the chosen, the outstanding. (Quran, 38:47)
And mention Ishmael, Elisha, and Ezekiel; all are among the outstanding. (Quran, 38:48)
This is a reminder. The devout will have a good place of return. (Quran, 38:49)
The Gardens of Eden, with their doors wide-open for them. (Quran, 38:50)
Relaxing therein, and calling for abundant fruit and beverage. (Quran, 38:51)
With them will be attendants with modest gaze, of same age. (Quran, 38:52)
This is what you are promised for the Day of Account. (Quran, 38:53)
Such is Our bounty, inexhaustible. (Quran, 38:54)
All This. But the transgressors will have a miserable return. (Quran, 38:55)
Hell; in which they will roast; what a miserable abode! (Quran, 38:56)
All this. Let them taste it—boiling and bitter cold. (Quran, 38:57)
And similar torments of diverse kinds. (Quran, 38:58)
“This is a crowd rushing headlong with you.” There is no welcome for them. They will be scorched by the Fire. (Quran, 38:59)
They will say, “But it is you! There is no welcome for you! It is you who brought it upon us! What a miserable end!” (Quran, 38:60)
They will say, “Our Lord, whoever brought this upon us, give him double torment in the Fire.” (Quran, 38:61)
And they will say, “What is it with us that we do not see men we used to count among the wicked? (Quran, 38:62)
Did we take them for mockery, or have our eyes swerved from them? (Quran, 38:63)
This is certainly true—the feuding of the people of the Fire. (Quran, 38:64)
Say, “I am only a warner, and there is no god except Allah—the One, the Conqueror. (Quran, 38:65)
The Lord of the heavens and the earth, and everything between them; the Mighty, the Forgiver.” (Quran, 38:66)
Say, “It is a message of great importance. (Quran, 38:67)
From which you are turning away. (Quran, 38:68)
I have no knowledge of the Highest Assembly as they dispute. (Quran, 38:69)
It is only revealed to me that I am a clear warner.” (Quran, 38:70)
Your Lord said to the angels, “I am creating a human being from clay. (Quran, 38:71)
When I have formed him, and breathed into him of My spirit, fall prostrate before him. (Quran, 38:72)
So the angels fell prostrate, all of them. (Quran, 38:73)
Except for Satan. He was too proud, and one of the faithless. (Quran, 38:74)

And My curse will be upon you until the Day of Judgment.” (Quran, 38:78)

Except for your loyal servants among them.” (Quran, 38:83)

I will fill Hell with you, and with every one of them who follows you.” (Quran, 38:85)

It is but a reminder to mankind. (Quran, 38:87)
And you will know its message after a while.” (Quran, 38:88)
The revelation of the Book is from Allah, the Mighty and Wise. (Quran, 39:1)
We sent down to you the Book with the truth, so serve Allah, devoting your religion to Him. (Quran, 39:2)
Is not to Allah that sincere faith is due? As for those who take guardians besides Him, “We only worship them that they may bring us nearer to Allah.” Allah will judge between them regarding their differences. Allah does not guide the lying blasphemer. (Quran, 39:3)
If Allah wanted to have a son, He could have selected from His creation at will. Glory be to Him. He is Allah, the One, the Prevailing. (Quran, 39:4)
He created the heavens and the earth with reason. He wraps the night around the day, and He wraps the day around the night. And He regulates the sun and the moon, each running along a specific course. He is indeed the Almighty, the Forgiver. (Quran, 39:5)
He created you from one person, then made from it its mate, and brought down livestock for you—eight kinds in pairs. He creates you in the wombs of your mothers, in successive formations, in a triple darkness. Such is Allah, your Lord. His is the kingdom. There is no god but He. So what made you deviate? (Quran, 39:6)
If you disbelieve, Allah is Independent of you, yet He does not approve ingratitude on the part of His servants. And if you are thankful, He will approve that in you. No bearer of burden can bear the burden of another. Then to your Lord is your return; and He will inform you of what you used to do. He is aware of what the hearts contain. (Quran, 39:7)
When some adversity touches the human being, he prays to his Lord, repenting to Him. But then, when He confers on him a grace of His, he forgets what he was praying for before, and he attributes rivals to Allah, in order to lead astray from His way. Say, “Enjoy your disbelief for a little while; you will be among the inmates of the Fire.” (Quran, 39:8)
Is he who worships devoutly during the watches of the night, prostrating himself and standing up, mindful of the Hereafter, and placing his hope in the mercy of his Lord? Say, “Are those who know and those who do not know equal?” Only those possessed of reason will remember. (Quran, 39:9)
Say, “O My devotees who have believed, keep your duty to your Lord. For those who do good in this world, is goodness. And Allah’s earth is vast. The steadfast will be paid their wages in full, without reckoning.” (Quran, 39:10)
Say, “I was commanded to serve Allah, devoting my religion exclusively to Him. (Quran, 39:11)
And I was commanded to be the first of those who submit.” (Quran, 39:12)
Say, “I fear, if I disobeyed my Lord, the punishment of a horrendous Day.” (Quran, 39:13)
Say, “It is Allah I worship, sincere in my faith in Him.” (Quran, 39:14)
“But you can worship whatever you wish besides Him.” Say, “The losers are those who lose their souls and their people on the Day of Resurrection.” That is indeed the obvious loss. (Quran, 39:15)
They will have layers of Fire above them, and layers beneath them. That is how Allah strikes fear into His servants—“O My servants! Beware of Me!” (Quran, 39:16)
As for those who avoid the worship of idols, and devote themselves to Allah—theirs is the good news. So give good news to My servants. (Quran, 39:17)
Those who listen to the Word, and follow the best of it. These are they whom Allah has guided. These are they who possess intellect. (Quran, 39:18)
What about someone who has deserved the sentence of punishment? Is it you who can save those in the Fire? (Quran, 39:19)
But those who fear their Lord will have mansions upon mansions, built high, with streams flowing beneath them. The promise of Allah; and Allah never breaks a promise. (Quran, 39:20)
Have you not considered how Allah sends down water from the sky, then He makes it flow into underground wells, then He produces with it plants of various colors, then they wither and you see them yellowing, then He turns them into debris? Surely in this is a reminder for those with understanding. (Quran, 39:21)
What about someone whose heart Allah has opened to Islam, so that he follows a light from His Lord? Woe to those whose hearts are hardened against the mention of Allah. Those are in manifest error. (Quran, 39:22)
Allah has sent down the best of narrations: A Scripture consistent and paired. The skins of those who reverence their Lord shiver from it, then their skins and their hearts soften up to the remembrance of Allah. Such is Allah’s guidance; He guides with it whomever He wills. But whomever Allah leaves astray, for him there is no guide. (Quran, 39:23)
What about someone who covers his face against the terrible misery of the Day of Resurrection? To the evildoers it will be said, “Taste what you used to earn.” (Quran, 39:24)
Those before them also denied the truth, so the penalty came upon them from where they did not perceive. (Quran, 39:25)
Allah made them taste disgrace in the present life, but the punishment of the Hereafter is worse, if they only knew. (Quran, 39:26)
We have cited in this Quran for mankind every ideal, that they may take heed. (Quran, 39:27)
An Arabic Quran, without any defect, so they may become righteous. (Quran, 39:28)
Allah cites the example of a man shared by partners at odds, and a man belonging exclusively to one man. Are they equal in status? Praise be to Allah, but most of them do not know. (Quran, 39:29)
You will die, and they will die. (Quran, 39:30)
Then, on the Day of Resurrection, you will be quarrelling before your Lord. (Quran, 39:31)
Who is more evil than he who lies about Allah, and denies the truth when it has come to him? Is there not in Hell room for the ungrateful? (Quran, 39:32)
But he who promotes the truth, and testifies to it—these are the righteous. (Quran, 39:33)
They will have whatever they please with their Lord. Such is the reward for the virtuous. (Quran, 39:34)
Allah will acquit them of the worst of their deeds, and will reward them according to the best of what they used to do. (Quran, 39:35)
Is Allah not enough for His servant? And they frighten you with those besides Him. Whomever Allah sends astray, for him there is no guide. (Quran, 39:36)
And whomever Allah guides, for him there is no misleader. Is Allah not Powerful and Vengeful? (Quran, 39:37)
And if you asked them, “Who created the heavens and the earth?” they would say, “Allah.” Say, “Have you seen those you pray to instead of Allah? If Allah willed any harm for me, can they lift His harm? And if He willed a blessing for me, can they hold back His mercy?” Say, “Allah suffices for me. On Him the reliant rely.” (Quran, 39:38)
Say: “O my people, work according to your ability; and so will I. Then you will know. (Quran, 39:39)
Who will receive a humiliating punishment, and on whom will fall a lasting torment.” (Quran, 39:40)
We sent down upon you the Book for mankind in truth. He who follows guidance does so for the good of his soul. And he who strays in error does so to its detriment. You are not their overseer. (Quran, 39:41)
Allah takes the souls at the time of their death, and those that have not died during their sleep. He retains those for which He has decreed death, and He releases the others until a predetermined time. In that are signs for people who reflect. (Quran, 39:42)
Or have they chosen intercessors other than Allah? Say, “Even though they have no power over anything, and are devoid of reason?” (Quran, 39:43)
Say, “All intercession is up to Allah. To Him belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth. Then to Him you will be returned.” (Quran, 39:44)
When Allah alone is mentioned, the hearts of those who do not believe in the Hereafter shrink with resentment. But when those other than Him are mentioned, they become filled with joy. (Quran, 39:45)
Say, “Our Allah, Initiator of the heavens and the earth, Knower of all secrets and declarations. You will judge between your servants regarding what they had differed about.” (Quran, 39:46)
If those who did wrong owned everything on earth, and the like of it with it, they would redeem themselves with it from the terrible suffering on the Day of Resurrection. But there will appear to them from Allah what they never anticipated. (Quran, 39:47)
There will appear to them the evils of their deeds, and they will be surrounded by what they used to ridicule. (Quran, 39:48)
When adversity touches the human being, he calls on Us. But then, when We favor him with a blessing from Us, he says, “I have attained this by virtue of my knowledge.” However, it is a test, but most of them do not know. (Quran, 39:49)
Those before them said it, but what they had earned did not avail them. (Quran, 39:50)
The evils of their deeds caught up with them. And the wrongdoers among these will also be afflicted by the evils of what they earned, and they cannot prevent it. (Quran, 39:51)
Do they not know that Allah extends the provision to whomever He wills, and constricts it? In that are signs for people who believe. (Quran, 39:52)
Say, “O My servants who have transgressed against themselves: do not despair of Allah’s mercy, for Allah forgives all sins. He is indeed the Forgiver, the Clement.” (Quran, 39:53)
And turn to your Lord, and submit to Him, before the retribution comes upon you. Then you will not be helped. (Quran, 39:54)
And follow the best of what was revealed to you from your Lord, before the punishment comes upon you suddenly, while you are unaware. (Quran, 39:55)
So that a soul may not say, “How sorry I am, for having neglected my duty to Allah, and for having been of the scoffers.” (Quran, 39:56)
Or say, “Had Allah guided me; I would have been of the pious.” (Quran, 39:57)
Or say, when it sees the penalty, “If only I had another chance, I would be of the virtuous.” (Quran, 39:58)
Yes indeed! My Verses did come to you, but you called them lies, turned arrogant, and were of the faithless. (Quran, 39:59)
On the Day of Resurrection, you will see those who told lies about Allah with their faces blackened. Is there not a place in Hell for the arrogant? (Quran, 39:60)
And Allah will save those who maintained righteousness to their place of salvation. No harm will touch them, nor will they grieve. (Quran, 39:61)
Allah is the Creator of all things, and He is in Charge of all things. (Quran, 39:62)
To Him belong the reins of the heavens and the earth. But those who blaspheme against the revelations of Allah—it is they who are the losers. (Quran, 39:63)
Say, “Is it other than Allah you instruct me to worship, you ignorant ones?” (Quran, 39:64)
It was revealed to you, and to those before you, that if you idolize, your works will be in vain, and you will be of the losers. (Quran, 39:65)
Rather, worship Allah, and be of the appreciative. (Quran, 39:66)
They have not esteemed Allah as He ought to be esteemed. The entire earth will be in His grip on the Day of Resurrection, and the heavens will be folded in His right. Immaculate is He, and Transcendent He is beyond the associations they make. (Quran, 39:67)
And the Trumpet will be sounded, whereupon everyone in the heavens and the earth will be stunned, except whomever Allah wills. Then it will be sounded another time, whereupon they will rise up, looking on. (Quran, 39:68)
And the earth will shine with the Light of its Lord; and the Book will be put in place; and the prophets and the witnesses will be brought in; and Judgment will be passed among them equitably, and they will not be wronged. (Quran, 39:69)
And every soul will be fully compensated for what it had done. He is well aware of what they do. (Quran, 39:70)
Those who disbelieved will be driven to Hell in throngs. Until, when they have reached it, and its gates are opened, its keepers will say to them, “Did not messengers from among you come to you, reciting to you the revelations of your Lord, and warning you of the meeting of this Day of yours?” They will say, “Yes, but the verdict of punishment is justified against the disbelievers.” (Quran, 39:71)
It will be said, “Enter the gates of Hell, to abide therein eternally.” How wretched is the destination of the arrogant. (Quran, 39:72)
And those who feared their Lord will be led to Paradise in throngs. Until, when they have reached it, and its gates are opened, its keepers will say to them, “Peace be upon you, you have been good, so enter it, to abide therein eternally.” (Quran, 39:73)
And they will say, “Praise be to Allah, who has fulfilled His promise to us, and made us inherit the land, enjoying Paradise as we please.” How excellent is the reward of the workers. (Quran, 39:74)
And you will see the angels hovering around the Throne, glorifying their Lord with praise. And it will be judged between them equitably, and it will be said, “Praise be to Allah, Lord of the Worlds.” (Quran, 39:75)
Ha, Meem. (Quran, 40:1)
The sending down of the Scripture is from Allah the Almighty, the Omniscient. (Quran, 40:2)
Forgiver of sins, Accepter of repentance, Severe in punishment, Bountiful in bounty. There is no god but He. To Him is the ultimate return. (Quran, 40:3)
None argues against Allah’s revelations except those who disbelieve. So do not be impressed by their activities in the land. (Quran, 40:4)
Before them the people of Noah rejected the truth, as did the confederates after them. Every community plotted against their messenger, to capture him. And they argued with falsehood, to defeat with it the truth. But I seized them. What a punishment it was! (Quran, 40:5)
Thus the sentence of your Lord became realized against those who disbelieve, that they are to be inmates of the Fire. (Quran, 40:6)
Those who carry the Throne, and those around it, glorify their Lord with praise, and believe in Him, and ask for forgiveness for those who believe: “Our Lord, You have encompassed everything in mercy and knowledge; so forgive those who repent and follow Your path, and protect them from the agony of the Blaze. (Quran, 40:7)
And admit them, Our Lord, into the Gardens of Eternity, which You have promised them, and the righteous among their parents, and their spouses, and their offspring. You are indeed the Almighty, the Most Wise. (Quran, 40:8)
And shield them from the evil deeds. Whomever You shield from the evil deeds, on that Day, You have had mercy on him. That is the supreme achievement.” (Quran, 40:9)
Those who disbelieved will be addressed, “The loathing of Allah is greater than your loathing of yourselves—for you were invited to the faith, but you refused.” (Quran, 40:10)
They will say, “Our Lord, you made us die twice, and twice you gave us life. Now we acknowledge our sins. Is there any way out?” (Quran, 40:11)
That is because when Allah alone was called upon, you disbelieved; but when others were associated with Him, you believed. Judgment rests with Allah the Sublime, the Majestic. (Quran, 40:12)
It is He who shows you His wonders, and sends down sustenance from the sky for you. But none pays heed except the repentant. (Quran, 40:13)
So call upon Allah, with sincere devotion to Him, even though the disbelievers resent it. (Quran, 40:14)
Exalted in rank, Owner of the Throne. He conveys the Spirit, by His command, upon whomever He wills of His servants, to warn of the Day of Encounter. (Quran, 40:15)
The Day when they will emerge, nothing about them will be concealed from Allah. “To whom does the sovereignty belong today?” “To Allah, the One, the Irresistible.” (Quran, 40:16)
On that Day, every soul will be recompensed for what it had earned. There will be no injustice on that Day. Allah is quick to settle accounts. (Quran, 40:17)
And warn them of the Day of Imminence, when the hearts are at the throats, choking them. The evildoers will have no intimate friend, and no intercessor to be obeyed. (Quran, 40:18)
He knows the deceptions of the eyes, and what the hearts conceal. (Quran, 40:19)
Allah judges with justice, while those whom they invoke besides Him cannot judge with anything. It is Allah who is the Hearing, the Seeing. (Quran, 40:20)
Have they not travelled through the earth, and seen the consequences for those before them? They were stronger than them, and they left more impact on earth. But Allah seized them for their sins, and they had no defender against Allah. (Quran, 40:21)
That is because their messengers used to come to them with clear proofs, but they disbelieved, so Allah seized them. He is Strong, Severe in retribution. (Quran, 40:22)
We sent Moses with Our signs, and a clear authority. (Quran, 40:23)
To Pharaoh, Hamaan, and Quaroon. But they said, “A lying sorcerer.” (Quran, 40:24)
Then, when he came to them with the truth from Us, they said, “Kill the sons of those who have believed with him, and spare their daughters.” But the scheming of the unbelievers can only go astray. (Quran, 40:25)
Pharaoh said, “Leave me to kill Moses, and let him appeal to his Lord. I fear he may change your religion, or spread disorder in the land.” (Quran, 40:26)
Moses said, “I have sought the protection of my Lord and your Lord, from every tyrant who does not believe in the Day of Account.” (Quran, 40:27)
A believing man from Pharaoh's family, who had concealed his faith, said, “Are you going to kill a man for saying, `My Lord is Allah,’ and he has brought you clear proofs from your Lord? If he is a liar, his lying will rebound upon him; but if he is truthful, then some of what he promises you will befall you. Allah does not guide the extravagant imposter. (Quran, 40:28)
O my people! Yours is the dominion today, supreme in the land; but who will help us against Allah’s might, should it fall upon us?” Pharaoh said, “I do not show you except what I see, and I do not guide you except to the path of prudence.” (Quran, 40:29)
The one who had believed said, “O my people, I fear for you the like of the day of the confederates. (Quran, 40:30)
Like the fate of the people of Noah, and Aad, and Thamood, and those after them. Allah wants no injustice for the servants. (Quran, 40:31)
O my people, I fear for you the Day of Calling Out. (Quran, 40:32)
The Day when you will turn and flee, having no defender against Allah. Whomever Allah misguides has no guide.” (Quran, 40:33)
Joseph had come to you with clear revelations, but you continued to doubt what he came to you with. Until, when he perished, you said, “Allah will never send a messenger after him.” Thus Allah leads astray the outrageous skeptic. (Quran, 40:34)
Those who argue against Allah’s revelations, without any proof having come to them—a heinous sin in the sight of Allah, and of those who believe. Thus Allah seals the heart of every proud bully. (Quran, 40:35)
And Pharaoh said, “O Hamaan, build me a tower, that I may reach the pathways. (Quran, 40:36)
The pathways of the heavens, so that I may glance at the Allah of Moses; though I think he is lying.” Thus Pharaoh’s evil deeds were made to appear good to him, and he was averted from the path. Pharaoh's guile was only in defeat. (Quran, 40:37)
The one who had believed said, “O my people, follow me, and I will guide you to the path of rectitude.” (Quran, 40:38)
“O my people, the life of this world is nothing but fleeting enjoyment, but the Hereafter is the Home of Permanence. (Quran, 40:39)
Whoever commits a sin will be repaid only with its like. But whoever works righteousness, whether male or female, and is a believer—these will enter Paradise, where they will be provided for without account. (Quran, 40:40)
O my people, how is it that I call you to salvation, and you call me to the Fire? (Quran, 40:41)
You call me to reject Allah, and to associate with Him what I have no knowledge of, while I call you to the Mighty Forgiver. (Quran, 40:42)
Without a doubt, what you call me to has no say in this world, or in the Hereafter; and our turning back is to Allah; and the transgressors are the inmates of the Fire. (Quran, 40:43)
You will remember what I am telling you, so I commit my case to Allah. Allah is Observant of the servants.” (Quran, 40:44)
So Allah protected him from the evils of their scheming, while a terrible torment besieged Pharaoh’s clan. (Quran, 40:45)
The Fire. They will be exposed to it morning and evening. And on the Day the Hour takes place: “Admit the clan of Pharaoh to the most intense agony.” (Quran, 40:46)
As they quarrel in the Fire, the weak will say to those who were arrogant, “We were followers of yours; will you then spare us a portion of the Fire?” (Quran, 40:47)
Those who were arrogant will say, “We are all in it; Allah has judged between the servants.” (Quran, 40:48)
And those in the Fire will say to the keepers of Hell, “Call to your Lord to lessen our suffering for one day.” (Quran, 40:49)
They will say, “Did not your messengers come to you with clear signs?” They will say, “Yes.” They will say, “Then pray, but the prayers of the disbelievers will always be in vain.” (Quran, 40:50)
Most surely We will support Our messengers and those who believe, in this life, and on the Day the witnesses arise. (Quran, 40:51)
The Day when their excuses will not profit the wrongdoers, and the curse will be upon them, and they will have the Home of Misery. (Quran, 40:52)
We gave Moses guidance, and made the Children of Israel inherit the Scripture. (Quran, 40:53)
A guide and a reminder for those endowed with reason. (Quran, 40:54)
So be patient. The promise of Allah is true. And ask forgiveness for your sin, and proclaim the praise of your Lord evening and morning. (Quran, 40:55)
Those who dispute regarding Allah’s revelations without any authority having come to them—there is nothing in their hearts but the feeling of greatness, which they will never attain. So seek refuge in Allah; for He is the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing. (Quran, 40:56)
Certainly the creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of humanity, but most people do not know. (Quran, 40:57)
Not equal are the blind and the seeing. Nor are those who believe and work righteousness equal to the sinners. How little you reflect. (Quran, 40:58)
Indeed, the Hour is coming; there is no doubt about it; but most people do not believe. (Quran, 40:59)
Your Lord has said, “Pray to Me, and I will respond to you. But those who are too proud to worship Me will enter Hell forcibly.” (Quran, 40:60)
It is Allah Who made the night for you, that you may rest therein; and the day allowing sight. Allah is gracious towards the people, but most people do not give thanks. (Quran, 40:61)
Such is Allah, your Lord, Creator of all things. There is no god except Him; so how could you turn away? (Quran, 40:62)
Thus are turned away those who dispute the signs of Allah. (Quran, 40:63)
It is Allah who made the earth a habitat for you, and the sky a structure. And He designed you, and designed you well; and He provided you with the good things. Such is Allah, your Lord; so Blessed is Allah, Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 40:64)
He is the Living One. There is no god except He. So pray to Him, devoting your religion to Him. Praise be to Allah, the Lord of the Worlds. (Quran, 40:65)
Say, “I was prohibited from worshiping those you invoke besides Allah, now that clear revelations have come to me from my Lord; and I was commanded to submit to the Lord of the Worlds.” (Quran, 40:66)
It is He who created you from dust, then from a seed, then from an embryo, then He brings you out as an infant, then He lets you reach your maturity, then you become elderly—although some of you die sooner—so that you may reach a predetermined age, so that you may understand. (Quran, 40:67)
It is He who gives life and death; and when He decides on a thing, He just says to it, “Be,” and it comes to be. (Quran, 40:68)
Have you not observed those who dispute regarding Allah's revelations, how they have deviated? (Quran, 40:69)
Those who call the Book a lie, and what We sent Our messengers with—they will surely know. (Quran, 40:70)
When the yokes are around their necks, and they will be dragged by the chains. (Quran, 40:71)
Into the boiling water, then in the Fire they will be consumed. (Quran, 40:72)
Then it will be said to them, “Where are those you used to deify? (Quran, 40:73)
Instead of Allah?” They will say, “They have abandoned us. In fact, we were praying to nothing before.” Thus Allah sends the disbelievers astray. (Quran, 40:74)
That is because you used to rejoice on earth in other than the truth, and because you used to behave with vanity. (Quran, 40:75)
Enter the gates of Hell, to remain therein forever. What a terrible dwelling for the arrogant. (Quran, 40:76)
So be patient. The promise of Allah is true. Whether We show you some of what We have promised them, or take you to Us, to Us they will be returned. (Quran, 40:77)
We sent messengers before you. Some of them We told you about, and some We did not tell you about. No messenger can bring a miracle except by leave of Allah. Then, when the command of Allah is issued, fair judgment will be passed, and there and then the seekers of vanity will lose. (Quran, 40:78)
Allah is He who created the domestic animals for you—some for you to ride, and some you eat. (Quran, 40:79)
And in them you have other benefits as well, and through them you satisfy your needs. And on them, and on the ships, you are transported. (Quran, 40:80)
And He shows you His signs. So which of Allah’s signs will you deny? (Quran, 40:81)
Have they not journeyed through the land, and seen the outcome for those before them? They were more numerous than they, and had greater power and influence in the land. But what they had achieved availed them nothing. (Quran, 40:82)
