When their messengers came to them with clear proofs, they rejoiced in the knowledge they had, and the very things they used to ridicule besieged them. (Quran, 40:83)
Then, when they witnessed Our might, they said, “We believe in Allah alone, and we reject what we used to associate with Him.” (Quran, 40:84)
But their faith could not help them once they witnessed Our might. This has been Allah’s way of dealing with His servants. And there and then the disbelievers lost. (Quran, 40:85)
Ha, Meem. (Quran, 41:1)
A revelation from the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful. (Quran, 41:2)
A Scripture whose Verses are detailed, a Quran in Arabic for people who know. (Quran, 41:3)
Bringing good news, and giving warnings. But most of them turn away, so they do not listen. (Quran, 41:4)
And they say, “Our hearts are screened from what you call us to, and in our ears is deafness, and between us and you is a barrier. So do what you want, and so will we.” (Quran, 41:5)
Say, “I am only a human like you; it is inspired in me that your Allah is One Allah. So be upright towards Him, and seek forgiveness from Him.” And woe to the idolaters. (Quran, 41:6)
Those who do not pay the alms; and regarding the Hereafter, they are disbelievers. (Quran, 41:7)
As for those who believe and do righteous deeds—for them is a reward uninterrupted. (Quran, 41:8)
Say, “Do you reject the One who created the earth in two days? And you attribute equals to Him? That is the Lord of the Universe.” (Quran, 41:9)
He placed stabilizers over it; and blessed it; and planned its provisions in four days, equally to the seekers. (Quran, 41:10)
Then He turned to the sky, and it was smoke, and said to it and to the earth, “Come, willingly or unwillingly.” They said, “We come willingly.” (Quran, 41:11)
So He completed them as seven universes in two days, and He assigned to each universe its laws. And We decorated the lower universe with lamps, and for protection. That is the design of the Almighty, the All-Knowing. (Quran, 41:12)
But if they turn away, say, “I have warned you of a thunderbolt, like the thunderbolt of Aad and Thamood.” (Quran, 41:13)
Their messengers came to them, from before them and from behind them, saying, “Do not worship anyone but Allah.” They said, “Had our Lord willed, He would have sent down angels; Therefore, we reject what you are sent with.” (Quran, 41:14)
As for Aad, they turned arrogant on earth, and opposed justice, and said, “Who is more powerful than us?” Have they not considered that Allah, who created them, is more powerful than they? And they went on denying Our revelations. (Quran, 41:15)
So We unleashed upon them a screaming wind, for a few miserable days, to make them taste the punishment of shame in this life; but the punishment of the Hereafter is more shameful; and they will not be saved. (Quran, 41:16)
And as for Thamood, We guided them, but they preferred blindness over guidance. So the thunderbolt of the humiliating punishment seized them, because of what they used to earn. (Quran, 41:17)
And We saved those who believed and were righteous. (Quran, 41:18)
The Day when Allah’s enemies are herded into the Fire, forcibly. (Quran, 41:19)
Until, when they have reached it, their hearing, and their sight, and their skins will testify against them regarding what they used to do. (Quran, 41:20)
And they will say to their skins, “Why did you testify against us?” They will say, “Allah, Who made all things speak, made us speak. It is He who created you the first time, and to Him you are returned.” (Quran, 41:21)
You were unable to hide yourselves from your hearing, and your sight, and your skins, to prevent them from testifying against you, and you imagined that Allah was unaware of much of what you do. (Quran, 41:22)
It is that thought of yours about your Lord that led you to ruin—so you became of the losers. (Quran, 41:23)
If they endure patiently, the Fire will be their residence; and if they make up excuses, they will not be pardoned. (Quran, 41:24)
We had assigned companions for them, who glamorized to them what was in front of them, and what was behind them. And the Word proved true against them in communities of jinn and humans that have passed away before them. They were losers. (Quran, 41:25)
Those who disbelieve say, “Do not listen to this Quran, and talk over it, so that you may prevail.” (Quran, 41:26)
We will make those who disbelieve taste an intense agony, and We will recompense them according to the worst of what they used to do. (Quran, 41:27)
Such is the recompense of Allah’s enemies—the Fire—where they will have their permanent home, in recompense for having disregarded Our revelations. (Quran, 41:28)
Those who disbelieved will say, “Our Lord, show us those who led us astray—among jinn and humans—and we will trample them under our feet, so they become of the lowest.” (Quran, 41:29)
Surely, those who say: “Our Lord is Allah,” and then go straight, the angels will descend upon them: “Do not fear, and do not grieve, but rejoice in the news of the Garden which you were promised. (Quran, 41:30)
We are your allies in this life and in the Hereafter, wherein you will have whatever your souls desire, and you will have therein whatever you call for. (Quran, 41:31)
As Hospitality from an All-Forgiving, Merciful One.” (Quran, 41:32)
And who is better in speech than someone who calls to Allah, and acts with integrity, and says, “I am of those who submit”? (Quran, 41:33)
Good and evil are not equal. Repel evil with good, and the person who was your enemy becomes like an intimate friend. (Quran, 41:34)
But none will attain it except those who persevere, and none will attain it except the very fortunate. (Quran, 41:35)
When a temptation from the Devil provokes you, seek refuge in Allah; He is the Hearer, the Knower. (Quran, 41:36)
And of His signs are the night and the day, and the sun and the moon. Do not bow down to the sun, nor to the moon, but bow down to Allah, Who created them both, if it is Him that you serve. (Quran, 41:37)
But if they are too proud—those in the presence of your Lord praise Him night and day, and without ever tiring. (Quran, 41:38)
And of His signs is that you see the land still. But when We send down water upon it, it stirs and grows. Surely, He Who revived it will revive the dead. He is Able to do all things. (Quran, 41:39)
Those who despise Our revelations are not hidden from Us. Is he who is hurled into the Fire better? Or he who arrives safely on the Day of Resurrection? Do as you please; He is Seeing of everything you do. (Quran, 41:40)
Those who reject the Reminder when it has come to them—it is an invincible Book. (Quran, 41:41)
Falsehood cannot approach it, from before it or behind it. It is a revelation from One Wise and Praiseworthy. (Quran, 41:42)
Nothing is said to you but was said to the Messengers before you: your Lord is Possessor of Forgiveness, and Possessor of Painful Repayment. (Quran, 41:43)
Had We made it a Quran in a foreign language, they would have said, “If only its verses were made clear.” Non-Arabic and an Arab? Say, “For those who believe, it is guidance and healing. But as for those who do not believe: there is heaviness in their ears, and it is blindness for them. These are being called from a distant place.” (Quran, 41:44)
We gave Moses the Book, but disputes arose concerning it. Were it not for a prior decree from your Lord, judgment would have been pronounced between them. But they are in perplexing doubt concerning it. (Quran, 41:45)
Whoever acts righteously does so for himself; and whoever works evil does so against himself. Your Lord is not unjust to the servants. (Quran, 41:46)
To Him is referred the knowledge of the Hour. No fruit emerges from its sheath, and no female conceives or delivers, except with His knowledge. And on the Day when He calls out to them, “Where are My associates?” They will say, “We admit to you, none of us is a witness.” (Quran, 41:47)
What they used to pray to before will forsake them, and they will realize that they have no escape. (Quran, 41:48)
The human being never tires of praying for good things; but when adversity afflicts him, he despairs and loses hope. (Quran, 41:49)
And when We let him taste a mercy from Us, after the adversity that had afflicted him, he will say, “This is mine, and I do not think that the Hour is coming; and even if I am returned to my Lord, I will have the very best with Him.” We will inform those who disbelieve of what they did, and We will make them taste an awful punishment. (Quran, 41:50)
When We provide comfort for the human being, he withdraws and distances himself; but when adversity befalls him, he starts lengthy prayers. (Quran, 41:51)
Say, “Have you considered? If it is from Allah and you reject it—who is further astray than he who is cutoff and alienated?” (Quran, 41:52)
We will show them Our proofs on the horizons, and in their very souls, until it becomes clear to them that it is the truth. Is it not sufficient that your Lord is witness over everything? (Quran, 41:53)
Surely they are in doubt about the encounter with their Lord. Surely He comprehends everything. (Quran, 41:54)
Ha, Meem. (Quran, 42:1)
Ayn, Seen, Qaf. (Quran, 42:2)
Thus He inspires you, and those before you—Allah the Almighty, the Wise. (Quran, 42:3)
To Him belongs everything in the heavens and everything on earth. He is the Sublime, the Magnificent. (Quran, 42:4)
The heavens above them almost burst apart, while the angels glorify the praises of their Lord, and ask forgiveness for those on earth. Allah is indeed the Forgiver, the Merciful. (Quran, 42:5)
As for those who take masters other than Him: Allah is in charge of them, and you are not responsible for them. (Quran, 42:6)
Thus We inspired you with an Arabic Quran, that you may warn the Central City and whoever is around it, and to warn of the Day of Assembly, of which there is no doubt; a group in the Garden, and a group in the Furnace. (Quran, 42:7)
Had Allah willed, He could have made them one community, but He admits into His mercy whomever He wills. As for the wrongdoers, they will have no protector and no savior. (Quran, 42:8)
Or have they adopted protectors besides him? But Allah is the Protector, and He gives life to the dead, and He has power over all things. (Quran, 42:9)
Whatever matter you differ about, its judgment rests with Allah. “Such is Allah, my Lord, in Whom I trust, and unto Him I repent.” (Quran, 42:10)
Originator of the heavens and the earth. He made for you mates from among yourselves, and pairs of animals, by means of which He multiplies you. There is nothing like Him. He is the Hearing, the Seeing. (Quran, 42:11)
To Him belongs absolute control of the heavens and the earth. He spreads the bounties to whomever He wills, or reduces it. He is aware of all things. (Quran, 42:12)
He prescribed for you the same religion He enjoined upon Noah, and what We inspired to you, and what We enjoined upon Abraham, and Moses, and Jesus: “You shall uphold the religion, and be not divided therein.” As for the idolaters, what you call them to is outrageous to them. Allah chooses to Himself whom He wills, and He guides to Himself whoever repents. (Quran, 42:13)
They became divided only after knowledge came to them, out of resentment among themselves. Were it not for a predetermined decision from your Lord, judgment would have been pronounced between them. Indeed, those who were made to inherit the Book after them are in grave doubt about it. (Quran, 42:14)
To this go on inviting, and be upright as you were commanded, and do not follow their inclinations, and say, “I believe in whatever Book Allah has sent down, and I was commanded to judge between you equitably. Allah is our Lord and your Lord. We have our deeds, and you have your deeds. Let there be no quarrel between us and you. Allah will bring us together, and to Him is the ultimate return.” (Quran, 42:15)
As for those who dispute about Allah after having answered His call, their argument is invalid with their Lord; and upon them falls wrath; and a grievous torment awaits them. (Quran, 42:16)
It is Allah who revealed the Book with the truth, and the Balance. And what will make you realize that perhaps the Hour is near? (Quran, 42:17)
Those who do not believe in it seek to hasten it; but those who believe are apprehensive of it, and they know it to be the truth. Absolutely, those who question the Hour are in distant error. (Quran, 42:18)
Allah is kind towards His worshipers. He provides for whomever He wills. He is the Powerful, the Honorable. (Quran, 42:19)
Whoever desires the harvest of the Hereafter, We increase for him his harvest; and whoever desires the harvest of this world, We give him thereof, and he has no share of the Hereafter. (Quran, 42:20)
Or is it that they have partners who litigate for them religious laws never authorized by Allah? Were it not for the conclusive decision, it would have been settled between them. The wicked will have a painful punishment. (Quran, 42:21)
You will see the unjust terrified of what they have earned, and it will befall them. As for those who believe and do good deeds, they will be in the Meadows of the Gardens; they will have whatever they please in the presence of their Lord; that is the supreme blessing. (Quran, 42:22)
That is the good news Allah gives to His servants who believe and do good deeds. Say, “I ask of you no wage for it, except affection among the near of kin.” Whoever does a good deed, We will increase its goodness for him. Allah is Forgiving and Appreciative. (Quran, 42:23)
Or do they say, “He forged a lie about Allah.” If Allah so willed, He could have sealed your heart. But Allah obliterates the false, and confirm the true by His Words. He knows what is in the hearts. (Quran, 42:24)
It is He who accepts the repentance of His worshipers, and remits the sins, and knows what you do. (Quran, 42:25)
And He answers those who believe and do good deeds, and He increases them of His grace. But the disbelievers will suffer a terrible punishment. (Quran, 42:26)
If Allah were to increase the provision to His servants, they would transgress on earth; but He sends down in precise measure whatever He wills. Surely, regarding His servants, He is Expert and Observant. (Quran, 42:27)
It is He who brings down the rain after they have despaired, and unfolds His mercy. He is the Guardian, the Praised. (Quran, 42:28)
And of His signs are the creation of the heavens and the earth, and the creatures He has spread throughout them; and He is Able to gather them at will. (Quran, 42:29)
Whatever misfortune befalls you, it is because of what your hands have earned; and yet He pardons much. (Quran, 42:30)
You are not the ones to interfere on earth; and besides Allah, you have no ally, and no helper. (Quran, 42:31)
And of His signs are the ships sailing the sea like flags. (Quran, 42:32)
If He willed, He could have stilled the winds, leaving them motionless on its surface. Surely in that are signs for every disciplined, grateful person. (Quran, 42:33)
Or He could wreck them, because of what they have earned. And yet He pardons much. (Quran, 42:34)
Those who dispute Our signs know that there is no asylum for them. (Quran, 42:35)
Whatever thing you are given is only the provision of this life. But what Allah possesses is better and more lasting for those who believe and rely on their Lord. (Quran, 42:36)
And those who avoid major sins and indecencies; and if they become angry, they forgive. (Quran, 42:37)
And those who respond to their Lord, and pray regularly, and conduct their affairs by mutual consultation, and give of what We have provided them. (Quran, 42:38)
And those who, when wronged, defend themselves. (Quran, 42:39)
The repayment of a bad action is one equivalent to it. But whoever pardons and makes reconciliation, his reward lies with Allah. He does not love the unjust. (Quran, 42:40)
As for those who retaliate after being wronged, there is no blame on them. (Quran, 42:41)
Blame lies on those who wrong people, and commit aggression in the land without right. These will have a painful punishment. (Quran, 42:42)
But whoever endures patiently and forgives—that is a sign of real resolve. (Quran, 42:43)
Whoever Allah leaves astray has no protector apart from Him. And you will see the transgressors, when they see the torment, saying, “Is there a way of going back?” (Quran, 42:44)
And you will see them exposed to it, cowering from disgrace, looking with concealed eyes. Those who believed will say, “The losers are those who lost themselves and their families on the Day of Resurrection.” Indeed, the evildoers are in a lasting torment. (Quran, 42:45)
They will have no allies to support them against Allah. Whomever Allah leaves astray has no way out. (Quran, 42:46)
Respond to your Lord before there comes from Allah a Day that cannot be turned back. You will have no refuge on that Day, and no possibility of denial. (Quran, 42:47)
But if they turn away—We did not send you as a guardian over them. Your only duty is communication. Whenever We let man taste mercy from Us, he rejoices in it; but when misfortune befalls them, as a consequence of what their hands have perpetrated, man turns blasphemous. (Quran, 42:48)
To Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. He creates whatever He wills. He grants daughters to whomever He wills, and He grants sons to whomever He wills. (Quran, 42:49)
Or He combines them together, males and females; and He renders whomever He wills sterile. He is Knowledgeable and Capable. (Quran, 42:50)
It is not for any human that Allah should speak to him, except by inspiration, or from behind a veil, or by sending a messenger to reveal by His permission whatever He wills. He is All-High, All-Wise. (Quran, 42:51)
We thus inspired you spiritually, by Our command. You did not know what the Scripture is, nor what faith is, but We made it a light, with which We guide whomever We will of Our servants. You surely guide to a straight path. (Quran, 42:52)
The path of Allah, to whom belongs everything in the heavens and everything on earth. Indeed, to Allah all matters revert. (Quran, 42:53)
Ha, Meem. (Quran, 43:1)
By the Book that makes things clear. (Quran, 43:2)
We made it an Arabic Quran, so that you may understand. (Quran, 43:3)
And it is with Us, in the Source Book, sublime and wise. (Quran, 43:4)
Shall We hold back the Reminder from you, since you are a transgressing people? (Quran, 43:5)
How many a prophet did We send to the ancients? (Quran, 43:6)
No messenger came to them, but they ridiculed him. (Quran, 43:7)
We destroyed people more powerful than they, and so the example of the ancients has passed away. (Quran, 43:8)
And if you asked them, “Who created the heavens and the earth?” They would say, “The Mighty, the Knower created them.” (Quran, 43:9)
He who made the earth a habitat for you, and traced pathways for you on it, that you may be guided. (Quran, 43:10)
He who sends down water from the sky in due proportion; and so We revive thereby a dead land. Thus you will be brought out. (Quran, 43:11)
He Who created all the pairs; and provided you with ships, and animals on which you ride. (Quran, 43:12)
That you may mount their backs, and remember the favor of your Lord as you sit firmly upon them, and say, “Glory be to Him Who placed these at our service; surely we could not have done it by ourselves. (Quran, 43:13)
And surely, to our Lord we will return.” (Quran, 43:14)
Yet they turn one of His servants into a part of Him. Man is clearly ungrateful. (Quran, 43:15)
Or has He chosen for Himself daughters from what He creates, and favored you with sons? (Quran, 43:16)
Yet when one of them is given news of what he attributes to the Most Gracious, his face darkens, and he suppresses grief. (Quran, 43:17)
“Someone brought up to be beautiful, and unable to help in a fight?” (Quran, 43:18)
And they appoint the angels, who are servants to the Most Gracious, as females. Have they witnessed their creation? Their claim will be recorded, and they will be questioned. (Quran, 43:19)
And they say, “Had the Most Gracious willed, we would not have worshiped them.” But they have no knowledge of that; they are merely guessing. (Quran, 43:20)
Or have We given them a book prior to this one, to which they adhere? (Quran, 43:21)
But they say, “We found our parents on a course, and we are guided in their footsteps.” (Quran, 43:22)
Likewise, We sent no warner before you to any town, but the wealthy among them said, “We found our parents on a course, and we are following in their footsteps.” (Quran, 43:23)
He would say, “Even if I bring you better guidance than what you found your parents following?” They would say, “We reject what you are sent with.” (Quran, 43:24)
So We wreaked vengeance upon them. Behold, then, what was the fate of those who deny. (Quran, 43:25)
When Abraham said to his father and his people, “I am innocent of what you worship. (Quran, 43:26)
Except for He who created me, for He will guide me.” (Quran, 43:27)
And he made it an enduring word in his progeny, so that they may return. (Quran, 43:28)
I gave these and their forefathers some enjoyment, until the truth and a manifest messenger came to them. (Quran, 43:29)
But when the truth came to them, they said, “This is sorcery, and we refuse to believe in it.” (Quran, 43:30)
They also said, “If only this Quran was sent down to a man of importance from the two cities.” (Quran, 43:31)
Is it they who allocate the mercy of your Lord? It is We who have allocated their livelihood in this life, and We elevated some of them in rank above others, that some of them would take others in service. But your Lord’s mercy is better than what they amass. (Quran, 43:32)
Were it not that humanity would become a single community, We would have provided those who disbelieve in the Most Gracious with roofs of silver to their houses, and stairways by which they ascend. (Quran, 43:33)
And doors to their houses, and furnishings on which they recline. (Quran, 43:34)
And decorations. Yet all that is nothing but the stuff of this life. Yet the Hereafter, with your Lord, is for the righteous. (Quran, 43:35)
Whoever shuns the remembrance of the Most Gracious, We assign for him a devil, to be his companion. (Quran, 43:36)
They hinder them from the path, though they think they are guided. (Quran, 43:37)
Until, when he comes to Us, he will say, “If only there were between me and you the distance of the two Easts.” What an evil companion! (Quran, 43:38)
It will not benefit you on that Day, since you did wrong. You are partners in the suffering. (Quran, 43:39)
Can you make the deaf hear, or guide the blind, and him who is in evident error? (Quran, 43:40)
Even if We take you away, We will wreak vengeance upon them. (Quran, 43:41)
Or show you what We have promised them; for We have absolute power over them. (Quran, 43:42)
So adhere to what is revealed to you. You are upon a straight path. (Quran, 43:43)
It is a message for you, and for your people; and you will be questioned. (Quran, 43:44)
Ask those of Our messengers We sent before you: “Did We appoint gods besides the Most Gracious to be worshiped?” (Quran, 43:45)
We sent Moses with Our revelations to Pharaoh and his dignitaries. He said, “I am the Messenger of the Lord of the Worlds.” (Quran, 43:46)
But when he showed them Our signs, they started laughing at them. (Quran, 43:47)
Each sign We showed them was more marvelous than its counterpart. And We afflicted them with the plagues, so that they may repent. (Quran, 43:48)
They said, “O sorcerer, pray to your Lord for us, according to His pledge to you, and then we will be guided.” (Quran, 43:49)
But when We lifted the torment from them, they immediately broke their promise. (Quran, 43:50)
Pharaoh proclaimed among his people, saying, “O my people, do I not own the Kingdom of Egypt, and these rivers flow beneath me? Do you not see? (Quran, 43:51)
Am I not better than this miserable wretch, who can barely express himself? (Quran, 43:52)
Why are bracelets of gold not dropped on him, or they angels came with him in procession?” (Quran, 43:53)
Thus he fooled his people, and they obeyed him. They were wicked people. (Quran, 43:54)
And when they provoked Our wrath, We took retribution from them, and We drowned them all. (Quran, 43:55)
Thus We made them a precedent and an example for the others. (Quran, 43:56)
And when the son of Mary was cited as an example, your people opposed. (Quran, 43:57)
They said, “Are our gods better, or he?” They cited him only for argument. In fact, they are a quarrelsome people. (Quran, 43:58)
He was just a servant whom We blessed, and We made him an example for the Children of Israel. (Quran, 43:59)
Had We willed, We would have made of you angels to be successors on earth. (Quran, 43:60)
He is a portent of the Hour, so have no doubt about it, and follow Me. This is a straight way. (Quran, 43:61)
And let not Satan divert you. He is an open enemy to you. (Quran, 43:62)
When Jesus came with the clarifications, he said, “I have come to you with wisdom, and to clarify for you some of what you differ about. So fear Allah, and obey me. (Quran, 43:63)
Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so worship Him—this is a straight path.” (Quran, 43:64)
But the factions differed among themselves. So woe to the wrongdoers from the suffering of a painful Day. (Quran, 43:65)
Are they only waiting for the Hour to come upon them suddenly, while they are unaware? (Quran, 43:66)
On that Day, friends will be enemies of one another, except for the righteous. (Quran, 43:67)
O My servants, you have nothing to fear on that Day, nor will you grieve. (Quran, 43:68)
Those who believed in Our revelations, and were submissive. (Quran, 43:69)
Enter the Garden, you and your spouses, Joyfully. (Quran, 43:70)
They will be served around with trays of gold, and cups. Therein is whatever the souls desire and delights the eyes. Therein you will stay forever. (Quran, 43:71)
Such is the Garden you are made to inherit, because of what you used to do. (Quran, 43:72)
Therein you will have abundant fruit, from which you eat. (Quran, 43:73)
As for the sinners, they will be in the torment of Hell forever. (Quran, 43:74)
It will never be eased for them. In it, they will be devastated. (Quran, 43:75)
We did them no injustice, but it was they who were the unjust. (Quran, 43:76)
And they will cry, “O Malek, let your Lord finish us off.” He will say, “You are staying.” (Quran, 43:77)
We have given you the truth, but most of you hate the truth. (Quran, 43:78)
Have they contrived some scheme? We too are contriving. (Quran, 43:79)
Or do they think that We cannot hear their secrets and their conspiracies? Yes indeed, Our messengers are by them, writing down. (Quran, 43:80)
Say, “If the Most Gracious had a son, I would be the first to worship.” (Quran, 43:81)
Glorified be the Lord of the heavens and the earth, the Lord of the Throne, beyond what they describe. (Quran, 43:82)
So leave them to blunder and play, until they encounter their Day which they are promised. (Quran, 43:83)
It is He who is Allah in heaven, and Allah on earth. He is the Wise, the Knower. (Quran, 43:84)
And blessed is He Who has sovereignty over the heavens and the earth and what is between them. He alone has knowledge of the Hour, and to Him you will be returned. (Quran, 43:85)
Those they invoke besides Him are incapable of intercession; only those who testify to the truth and have knowledge. (Quran, 43:86)
And if you asked them, “Who created them?”, they would say, “Allah.” Why then do they deviate? (Quran, 43:87)
As for his statement: “My Lord, these are a people who do not believe.” (Quran, 43:88)
Pardon them, and say, “Peace.” They will come to know. (Quran, 43:89)
Ha, Meem. (Quran, 44:1)
By the Enlightening Scripture. (Quran, 44:2)
We have revealed it on a Blessed Night—We have warned. (Quran, 44:3)
In it is distinguished every wise command. (Quran, 44:4)
A decree from Us. We have been sending messages. (Quran, 44:5)
As mercy from your Lord. He is the Hearer, the Knower. (Quran, 44:6)
Lord of the heavens and the earth and what is between them, if you know for sure. (Quran, 44:7)
There is no god but He. He gives life and causes death—your Lord and Lord of your ancestors of old. (Quran, 44:8)
Yet they play around in doubt. (Quran, 44:9)
So watch out for the Day when the sky produces a visible smoke. (Quran, 44:10)
Enveloping mankind; this is a painful punishment. (Quran, 44:11)
“Our Lord, lift the torment from us, we are believers.” (Quran, 44:12)
But how can they be reminded? An enlightening messenger has already come to them. (Quran, 44:13)
But they turned away from him, and said, “Educated, but crazy!” (Quran, 44:14)
We will ease the punishment a little, but you will revert. (Quran, 44:15)
The Day when We launch the Great Assault—We will avenge. (Quran, 44:16)
Before them We tested the people of Pharaoh; a noble messenger came to them. (Quran, 44:17)
Saying, “Hand over Allah’s servants to me. I am an honest messenger to you.” (Quran, 44:18)
And, “Do not exalt yourselves above Allah. I come to you with clear authority. (Quran, 44:19)
I have taken refuge in my Lord and your Lord, lest you stone me. (Quran, 44:20)
But if you do not believe in me, keep away from me.” (Quran, 44:21)
He appealed to his Lord: “These are a sinful people.” (Quran, 44:22)
“Set out with My servants by night—you will be followed. (Quran, 44:23)
And cross the sea quickly; they are an army to be drowned.” (Quran, 44:24)
How many gardens and fountains did they leave behind? (Quran, 44:25)
And plantations, and splendid buildings. (Quran, 44:26)
And comforts they used to enjoy. (Quran, 44:27)
So it was; and We passed it on to another people. (Quran, 44:28)
Neither heaven nor earth wept over them, nor were they reprieved. (Quran, 44:29)
And We delivered the Children of Israel from the humiliating persecution. (Quran, 44:30)
From Pharaoh. He was a transgressing tyrant. (Quran, 44:31)
And We chose them knowingly over all other people. (Quran, 44:32)
And We gave them many signs, in which was an obvious test. (Quran, 44:33)
These people say. (Quran, 44:34)
“There is nothing but our first death, and we will not be resurrected. (Quran, 44:35)
Bring back our ancestors, if you are truthful.” (Quran, 44:36)
Are they better, or the people of Tubba and those before them? We annihilated them. They were evildoers. (Quran, 44:37)
We did not create the heavens and the earth and what is between them to play. (Quran, 44:38)
We created them only for a specific purpose, but most of them do not know. (Quran, 44:39)
The Day of Sorting Out is the appointed time for them all. (Quran, 44:40)
The Day when no friend will avail a friend in any way, and they will not be helped. (Quran, 44:41)
Except for him upon whom Allah has mercy. He is the Mighty, the Merciful. (Quran, 44:42)
The Tree of Bitterness. (Quran, 44:43)
The food of the sinner. (Quran, 44:44)
Like molten lead; boiling inside the bellies. (Quran, 44:45)
Like the boiling of seething water. (Quran, 44:46)
Seize him and drag him into the midst of Hell! (Quran, 44:47)
Then pour over his head the suffering of the Inferno! (Quran, 44:48)
Taste! You who were powerful and noble. (Quran, 44:49)
This is what you used to doubt. (Quran, 44:50)
As for the righteous, they will be in a secure place. (Quran, 44:51)
Amidst gardens and springs. (Quran, 44:52)
Dressed in silk and brocade, facing one another. (Quran, 44:53)
So it is, and We will wed them to lovely companions. (Quran, 44:54)
They will call therein for every kind of fruit, in peace and security. (Quran, 44:55)
Therein they will not taste death, beyond the first death; and He will protect them from the torment of Hell. (Quran, 44:56)
A favor from your Lord. That is the supreme salvation. (Quran, 44:57)
We made it easy in your language, so that they may remember. (Quran, 44:58)
So wait and watch. They too are waiting and watching. (Quran, 44:59)
Ha, Meem. (Quran, 45:1)
The revelation of the Book is from Allah, the Exalted in Might, the Wise. (Quran, 45:2)
In the heavens and the earth are proofs for the believers. (Quran, 45:3)
And in your own creation, and in the creatures He scattered, are signs for people of firm faith. (Quran, 45:4)
And in the alternation of night and day, and in the sustenance Allah sends down from the sky, with which He revives the earth after its death, and in the circulation of the winds, are marvels for people who reason. (Quran, 45:5)
These are Allah’s Verses which We recite to you in truth. In which message, after Allah and His revelations, will they believe? (Quran, 45:6)
Woe to every sinful liar. (Quran, 45:7)
Who hears Allah's revelations being recited to him, yet he persists arrogantly, as though he did not hear them. Announce to him a painful punishment. (Quran, 45:8)
And when he learns something of Our revelations, he takes them in mockery. For such there is a shameful punishment. (Quran, 45:9)
Beyond them lies Hell. What they have earned will not benefit them at all, nor will those they adopted as lords instead of Allah. They will have a terrible punishment. (Quran, 45:10)
This is guidance. Those who blaspheme their Lord’s revelations will have a punishment of agonizing pain. (Quran, 45:11)
It is Allah who placed the sea at your service, so that ships may run through it by His command, and that you may seek of His bounty, and that you may give thanks. (Quran, 45:12)
And He placed at your service whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on earth—all is from Him. In that are signs for a people who think. (Quran, 45:13)
Tell those who believe to forgive those who do not hope for the Days of Allah. He will fully recompense people for whatever they have earned. (Quran, 45:14)
Whoever does a good deed, it is for his soul; and whoever commits evil, it is against it; then to your Lord you will be returned. (Quran, 45:15)
We gave the Children of Israel the Book, and wisdom, and prophecy; and We provided them with the good things; and We gave them advantage over all other people. (Quran, 45:16)
And We gave them precise rulings. They fell into dispute only after knowledge came to them, out of mutual rivalry. Your Lord will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection regarding the things they differed about. (Quran, 45:17)
Then We set you upon a pathway of faith, so follow it, and do not follow the inclinations of those who do not know. (Quran, 45:18)
They will not help you against Allah in any way. The wrongdoers are allies of one another, while Allah is the Protector of the righteous. (Quran, 45:19)
This is an illumination for mankind, and guidance, and mercy for people who believe with certainty. (Quran, 45:20)
Do those who perpetrate the evil deeds assume that We will regard them as equal to those who believe and do righteous deeds, whether in their life or their death? Evil is their judgment! (Quran, 45:21)
Allah created the heavens and the earth with justice, so that every soul will be repaid for what it has earned. And they will not be wronged. (Quran, 45:22)
Have you considered him who has taken his desire for his god? Allah has knowingly led him astray, and has sealed his hearing and his heart, and has placed a veil over his vision. Who will guide him after Allah? Will you not reflect? (Quran, 45:23)
And they say, “There is nothing but this our present life; we die and we live, and nothing destroys us except time.” But they have no knowledge of that; they are only guessing. (Quran, 45:24)
When Our clarifying Verses are recited to them, their only argument is to say, “Bring back our ancestors, if you are truthful.” (Quran, 45:25)
Say, “Allah gives you life, then He makes you die; then He gathers you for the Day of Resurrection, about which there is no doubt. But most people do not know.” (Quran, 45:26)
To Allah belongs the kingship of the heavens and the earth. On the Day when the Hour takes place, on that Day the falsifiers will lose. (Quran, 45:27)
You will see every community on its knees; every community will be called to its Book: “Today you are being repaid for what you used to do. (Quran, 45:28)
This Book of Ours speaks about you in truth. We have been transcribing what you have been doing.” (Quran, 45:29)
As for those who believed and did righteous deeds, their Lord will admit them into His mercy. That is the clear triumph. (Quran, 45:30)
But as for those who disbelieved: “Were My revelations not recited to you? But you turned arrogant, and were guilty people.” (Quran, 45:31)
And when it was said, “The promise of Allah is true, and of the Hour there is no doubt,” you said, “We do not know what the Hour is; we think it is only speculation; we are not convinced.” (Quran, 45:32)
The evils of what they did will become evident to them, and the very thing they ridiculed will haunt them. (Quran, 45:33)
And it will be said, “Today We forget you, as you forgot the encounter of this Day of yours. Your abode is the Fire, and there are no saviors for you. (Quran, 45:34)
That is because you took Allah’s revelations for a joke, and the worldly life lured you.” So today they will not be brought out of it, and they will not be allowed to repent. (Quran, 45:35)
Praise belongs to Allah; Lord of the heavens, Lord of the earth, Lord of humanity. (Quran, 45:36)
To Him belongs all supremacy in the heavens and the earth. He is the Majestic, the Wise. (Quran, 45:37)
Ha, Meem. (Quran, 46:1)
The sending down of the Scripture is from Allah, the Honorable, the Wise. (Quran, 46:2)
We did not create the heavens and the earth and what lies between them except with reason, and for a finite period. But the blasphemers continue to ignore the warnings they receive. (Quran, 46:3)
Say, “Have you considered those you worship instead of Allah? Show me which portion of the earth they have created. Or do they own a share of the heavens? Bring me a scripture prior to this one, or some trace of knowledge, if you are truthful.” (Quran, 46:4)
Who is more wrong than him who invokes, besides Allah, those who will not answer him until the Day of Resurrection, and are heedless of their prayers? (Quran, 46:5)
And when humanity is gathered, they will be enemies to them, and will renounce their worship of them. (Quran, 46:6)
When Our revelations are recited to them, plain and clear, those who disbelieve say of the truth when it has come to them, “This is obviously magic.” (Quran, 46:7)
Or do they say, “He invented it himself”? Say, “If I invented it myself, there is nothing you can do to protect me from Allah. He knows well what you are engaged in. He is sufficient witness between me and you. He is the Forgiver, the Merciful.” (Quran, 46:8)
Say, “I am not different from the other messengers; and I do not know what will be done with me, or with you. I only follow what is inspired in me, and I am only a clear warner.” (Quran, 46:9)
Say, “Have you considered? What if it is from Allah and you disbelieve in it? A witness from the Children of Israel testified to its like, and has believed, while you turned arrogant. Allah does not guide the unjust people.” (Quran, 46:10)
Those who disbelieve say to those who believe, “If it were anything good, they would not have preceded us to it.” And since they were not guided by it, they will say, “This is an ancient lie.” (Quran, 46:11)
And before it was the Book of Moses, a model and a mercy. And this is a confirming Book, in the Arabic language, to warn those who do wrong—and good news for the doers of good. (Quran, 46:12)
Those who say, “Our Lord is Allah,” then lead a righteous life—they have nothing to fear, nor shall they grieve. (Quran, 46:13)
These are the inhabitants of Paradise, where they will dwell forever—a reward for what they used to do. (Quran, 46:14)
We have enjoined upon man kindness to his parents. His mother carried him with difficulty, and delivered him with difficulty. His bearing and weaning takes thirty months. Until, when he has attained his maturity, and has reached forty years, he says, “Lord, enable me to appreciate the blessings You have bestowed upon me and upon my parents, and to act with righteousness, pleasing You. And improve my children for me. I have sincerely repented to You, and I am of those who have surrendered.” (Quran, 46:15)
Those are they from whom We accept the best of their deeds, and We overlook their misdeeds, among the dwellers of Paradise—the promise of truth which they are promised. (Quran, 46:16)
As for him who says to his parents, “Enough of you! Are you promising me that I will be raised up, when generations have passed away before me?” While they cry for Allah’s help, “Woe to you! Believe! The promise of Allah is true!” But he says, “These are nothing but tales of the ancients.” (Quran, 46:17)
Those are they upon whom the sentence is justified, among the communities that have passed away before them, of jinn and humans. They are truly losers. (Quran, 46:18)
There are degrees for everyone, according to what they have done, and He will repay them for their works in full, and they will not be wronged. (Quran, 46:19)
On the Day when the faithless will be paraded before the Fire: “You have squandered your good in your worldly life, and you took pleasure in them. So today you are being repaid with the torment of shame, because of your unjust arrogance on earth, and because you used to sin.” (Quran, 46:20)
And mention the brother of Aad, as he warned his people at the dunes. Warnings have passed away before him, and after him: “Worship none but Allah; I fear for you the punishment of a tremendous Day.” (Quran, 46:21)
They said, “Did you come to us to divert us from our gods? Then bring us what you threaten us with, if you are being truthful.” (Quran, 46:22)
He said, “The knowledge is only with Allah, and I inform you of what I was sent with; but I see you are an ignorant people.” (Quran, 46:23)
Then, when they saw a cloud approaching their valley, they said, “This is a cloud that will bring us rain.” “In fact, it is what you were impatient for: a wind in which is grievous suffering.” (Quran, 46:24)
It will destroy everything by the command of its Lord. And when the morning came upon them, there was nothing to be seen except their dwellings. Thus We requite the guilty people. (Quran, 46:25)
We had empowered them in the same way as We empowered you; and We gave them the hearing, and the sight, and the minds. But neither their hearing, nor their sight, nor their minds availed them in any way. That is because they disregarded the revelations of Allah; and so they became surrounded by what they used to ridicule. (Quran, 46:26)
We have destroyed many townships around you, and diversified the signs, so that they may return. (Quran, 46:27)
Why then did the idols, whom they worshiped as means of nearness to Allah, not help them? In fact, they abandoned them. It was their lie, a fabrication of their own making. (Quran, 46:28)
Recall when We dispatched towards you a number of jinn, to listen to the Quran. When they came in its presence, they said, “Pay attention!” Then, when it was concluded, they rushed to their people, warning them. (Quran, 46:29)
They said, “O our people, we have heard a Scripture, sent down after Moses, confirming what came before it. It guides to the truth, and to a straight path. (Quran, 46:30)
O our people! Answer the caller to Allah, and believe in Him; and He will forgive you your sins, and will save you from a painful punishment.” (Quran, 46:31)
He who does not answer the caller to Allah will not escape on earth, and has no protectors besides Him. Those are in obvious error. (Quran, 46:32)
Do they not realize that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth, and was never tired by creating them, is Able to revive the dead? Yes indeed; He is Capable of everything. (Quran, 46:33)
On the Day when those who disbelieved are presented to the Fire: “Is this not real?” They will say, “Yes, indeed, by our Lord.” He will say, “Then taste the suffering for having disbelieved.” (Quran, 46:34)
So be patient, as the messengers with resolve were patient, and do not be hasty regarding them. On the Day when they witness what they are promised, it will seem as if they had lasted only for an hour of a day. A proclamation: Will any be destroyed except the sinful people? (Quran, 46:35)
Those who disbelieve and repel from the path of Allah—He nullifies their works. (Quran, 47:1)
While those who believe, and work righteousness, and believe in what was sent down to Muhammad—and it is the truth from their Lord—He remits their sins, and relieves their concerns. (Quran, 47:2)
That is because those who disbelieve follow falsehoods, while those who believe follow the truth from their Lord. Allah thus cites for the people their examples. (Quran, 47:3)
When you encounter those who disbelieve, strike at their necks. Then, when you have routed them, bind them firmly. Then, either release them by grace, or by ransom, until war lays down its burdens. Had Allah willed, He could have defeated them Himself, but He thus tests some of you by means of others. As for those who are killed in the way of Allah, He will not let their deeds go to waste. (Quran, 47:4)
He will guide them, and will improve their state of mind. (Quran, 47:5)
And will admit them into Paradise, which He has identified for them. (Quran, 47:6)
O you who believe! If you support Allah, He will support you, and will strengthen your foothold. (Quran, 47:7)
But as for those who disbelieve, for them is perdition, and He will waste their deeds. (Quran, 47:8)
That is because they hated what Allah revealed, so He nullified their deeds. (Quran, 47:9)
Have they not journeyed through the earth and seen the consequences for those before them? Allah poured destruction upon them, and for the unbelievers is something comparable. (Quran, 47:10)
That is because Allah is the Master of those who believe, while the disbelievers have no master. (Quran, 47:11)
Allah will admit those who believe and do good deeds into gardens beneath which rivers flow. As for those who disbelieve, they enjoy themselves, and eat as cattle eat, and the Fire will be their dwelling. (Quran, 47:12)
How many a town was more powerful than your town which evicted you? We destroyed them, and there was no helper for them. (Quran, 47:13)
Is he who stands upon evidence from his Lord, like someone whose evil deed is made to appear good to him? And they follow their own desires? (Quran, 47:14)
The likeness of the Garden promised to the righteous: in it are rivers of pure water, and rivers of milk forever fresh, and rivers of wine delightful to the drinkers, and rivers of strained honey. And therein they will have of every fruit, and forgiveness from their Lord. Like one abiding in the Fire forever, and are given to drink boiling water, that cuts-up their bowels? (Quran, 47:15)
Among them are those who listen to you, but when they leave your presence, they say to those given knowledge, “What did he say just now?” Those are they whose hearts Allah has sealed, and they follow their own desires. (Quran, 47:16)
As for those who are guided, He increases them in guidance, and He has granted them their righteousness. (Quran, 47:17)
Are they just waiting until the Hour comes to them suddenly? Its tokens have already come. But how will they be reminded when it has come to them? (Quran, 47:18)
Know that there is no god but Allah, and ask forgiveness for your sin, and for the believing men and believing women. Allah knows your movements, and your resting-place. (Quran, 47:19)
Those who believe say, “If only a chapter is sent down.” Yet when a decisive chapter is sent down, and fighting is mentioned in it, you see those in whose hearts is sickness looking at you with the look of someone fainting at death. So woe to them! (Quran, 47:20)
Obedience and upright speech. Then, when the matter is settled, being true to Allah would have been better for them. (Quran, 47:21)
If you turn away, you are likely to make mischief on earth, and sever your family ties. (Quran, 47:22)
Those are they whom Allah has cursed. He made them deaf, and blinded their sight. (Quran, 47:23)
Will they not ponder the Quran? Or are there locks upon their hearts? (Quran, 47:24)
Those who reverted after the guidance became clear to them—Satan has enticed them, and has given them latitude. (Quran, 47:25)
That is because they said to those who hated what Allah has revealed, “We will obey you in certain matters.” But Allah knows their secret thoughts. (Quran, 47:26)
How about when the angels take them at death, beating their faces and their backs? (Quran, 47:27)
That is because they pursued what displeases Allah, and they disliked His approval, so He nullified their works. (Quran, 47:28)
Do those in whose hearts is sickness think that Allah will not expose their malice? (Quran, 47:29)
Had We willed, We could have shown them to you, and you would have recognized them by their marks. Yet you will recognize them by their tone of speech. And Allah knows your actions. (Quran, 47:30)
We will certainly test you, until We know those among you who strive, and those who are steadfast, and We will test your reactions. (Quran, 47:31)
Those who disbelieve, and hinder from the path of Allah, and oppose the Messenger after guidance has become clear to them—they will not hurt Allah in the least, but He will nullify their deeds. (Quran, 47:32)
O you who believe! Obey Allah, and obey the Messenger, and do not let your deeds go to waste. (Quran, 47:33)
Those who disbelieve, and hinder from Allah’s path, and then die as disbelievers—Allah will not forgive them. (Quran, 47:34)
So do not waver and call for peace while you have the upper hand. Allah is with you, and He will not waste your efforts. (Quran, 47:35)
The life of this world is nothing but play and pastime. But if you have faith and lead a righteous life, He will grant you your rewards, and He will not ask you for your possessions. (Quran, 47:36)
Were He to ask you for it, and press you, you would become tightfisted, and He would expose your unwillingness. (Quran, 47:37)
Here you are, being called to spend in the cause of Allah. Among you are those who withhold; but whoever withholds is withholding against his own soul. Allah is the Rich, while you are the needy. And if you turn away, He will replace you with another people, and they will not be like you. (Quran, 47:38)
We have granted you a conspicuous victory. (Quran, 48:1)
That Allah may forgive you your sin, past and to come, and complete His favors upon you, and guide you in a straight path. (Quran, 48:2)
And help you with an unwavering support. (Quran, 48:3)
It is He who sent down tranquility into the hearts of the believers, to add faith to their faith. To Allah belong the forces of the heavens and the earth. Allah is Knowing and Wise. (Quran, 48:4)
He will admit the believers, male and female, into Gardens beneath which rivers flow, to abide therein forever, and He will remit their sins. That, with Allah, is a great triumph. (Quran, 48:5)
And He will punish the hypocrites, male and female, and the idolaters, male and female, those who harbor evil thoughts about Allah. They are surrounded by evil; and Allah is angry with them, and has cursed them, and has prepared for them Hell—a miserable destination. (Quran, 48:6)
To Allah belong the troops of the heavens and the earth. Allah is Mighty and Wise. (Quran, 48:7)
We sent you as a witness, and a bearer of good news, and a warner. (Quran, 48:8)
That you may believe in Allah and His Messenger, and support Him, and honor Him, and praise Him morning and evening. (Quran, 48:9)
Those who pledge allegiance to you are pledging allegiance to Allah. The hand of Allah is over their hands. Whoever breaks his pledge breaks it to his own loss. And whoever fulfills his covenant with Allah, He will grant him a great reward. (Quran, 48:10)
The Desert-Arabs who remained behind will say to you, “Our belongings and our families have preoccupied us, so ask forgiveness for us.” They say with their tongues what is not in their hearts. Say, “Who can avail you anything against Allah, if He desires loss for you, or desires gain for you?” In fact, Allah is Informed of what you do. (Quran, 48:11)
But you thought that the Messenger and the believers will never return to their families, and this seemed fine to your hearts; and you harbored evil thoughts, and were uncivilized people. (Quran, 48:12)
He who does not believe in Allah and His Messenger—We have prepared for the disbelievers a Blazing Fire. (Quran, 48:13)
To Allah belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth. He forgives whomever He wills, and He punishes whomever He wills. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 48:14)
Those who lagged behind will say when you depart to collect the gains, “Let us follow you.” They want to change the Word of Allah. Say, “You will not follow us; Allah has said so before.” Then they will say, “But you are jealous of us.” In fact, they understand only a little. (Quran, 48:15)
Say to the Desert-Arabs who lagged behind, “You will be called against a people of great might; you will fight them, unless they submit. If you obey, Allah will give you a fine reward. But if you turn away, as you turned away before, He will punish you with a painful punishment.” (Quran, 48:16)
There is no blame on the blind, nor any blame on the lame, nor any blame on the sick. Whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger—He will admit him into gardens beneath which rivers flow; but whoever turns away—He will punish him with a painful punishment. (Quran, 48:17)
Allah was pleased with the believers, when they pledged allegiance to you under the tree. He knew what was in their hearts, and sent down serenity upon them, and rewarded them with an imminent conquest. (Quran, 48:18)
And abundant gains for them to capture. Allah is Mighty and Wise. (Quran, 48:19)
Allah has promised you abundant gains, which you will capture. He has expedited this for you, and has restrained people’s hands from you; that it may be a sign to the believers, and that He may guide you on a straight path. (Quran, 48:20)
And other things, of which you were incapable, but Allah has encompassed them. Allah is Capable of everything. (Quran, 48:21)
If those who disbelieve had fought you, they would have turned back and fled, then found neither protector nor helper. (Quran, 48:22)
It is Allah’s pattern, ongoing since the past. You will never find any change in Allah’s pattern. (Quran, 48:23)
It is He who withheld their hands from you, and your hands from them, in the valley of Mecca, after giving you advantage over them. Allah is Observer of what you do. (Quran, 48:24)
It is they who disbelieved, and barred you from the Sacred Mosque, and prevented the offering from reaching its destination. Were it not for faithful men and faithful women, whom you did not know, you were about to hurt them, and became guilty of an unintentional crime. Thus Allah admits into His mercy whomever He wills. Had they dispersed, We would have punished those who disbelieved among them with a painful penalty. (Quran, 48:25)
Those who disbelieved filled their hearts with rage—the rage of the days of ignorance. But Allah sent His serenity down upon His Messenger, and upon the believers, and imposed on them the words of righteousness—of which they were most worthy and deserving. Allah is aware of everything. (Quran, 48:26)
Allah has fulfilled His Messenger’s vision in truth: “You will enter the Sacred Mosque, Allah willing, in security, heads shaven, or hair cut short, not fearing. He knew what you did not know, and has granted besides that an imminent victory.” (Quran, 48:27)
It is He who sent His Messenger with the guidance and the religion of truth, to make it prevail over all religions. Allah suffices as Witness. (Quran, 48:28)
Muhammad is the Messenger of Allah. Those with him are stern against the disbelievers, yet compassionate amongst themselves. You see them kneeling, prostrating, seeking blessings from Allah and approval. Their marks are on their faces from the effects of prostration. Such is their description in the Torah, and their description in the Gospel: like a plant that sprouts, becomes strong, grows thick, and rests on its stem, impressing the farmers. Through them He enrages the disbelievers. Allah has promised those among them who believe and do good deeds forgiveness and a great reward. (Quran, 48:29)
O you who believe! Do not place your opinions above that of Allah and His Messenger, and fear Allah. Allah is Hearing and Knowing. (Quran, 49:1)
O you who believe! Do not raise your voices above the voice of the Prophet, and do not speak loudly to him, as you speak loudly to one another, lest your works be in vain without you realizing. (Quran, 49:2)
Those who lower their voices before Allah’s Messenger—those are they whose hearts Allah has tested for piety. They will have forgiveness and a great reward. (Quran, 49:3)
Those who call you from behind the chambers—most of them do not understand. (Quran, 49:4)
Had they remained patient until you came out to them, it would have been better for them. But Allah is Forgiving and Merciful. (Quran, 49:5)
O you who believe! If a troublemaker brings you any news, investigate, lest you harm people out of ignorance, and you become regretful for what you have done. (Quran, 49:6)
And know that among you is the Messenger of Allah. Had he obeyed you in many things, you would have suffered hardship. But Allah has given you the love of faith, and adorned it in your hearts, and made disbelief, mischief, and rebellion hateful to you. These are the rightly guided. (Quran, 49:7)
A Grace and Favor from Allah. Allah is Knowing and Wise. (Quran, 49:8)
If two groups of believers fight each other, reconcile between them. But if one group aggresses against the other, fight the aggressing group until it complies with Allah’s command. Once it has complied, reconcile between them with justice, and be equitable. Allah loves the equitable. (Quran, 49:9)
The believers are brothers, so reconcile between your brothers, and remain conscious of Allah, so that you may receive mercy. (Quran, 49:10)
O you who believe! No people shall ridicule other people, for they may be better than they. Nor shall any women ridicule other women, for they may be better than they. Nor shall you slander one another, nor shall you insult one another with names. Evil is the return to wickedness after having attained faith. Whoever does not repent—these are the wrongdoers. (Quran, 49:11)
O you who believe! Avoid most suspicion—some suspicion is sinful. And do not spy on one another, nor backbite one another. Would any of you like to eat the flesh of his dead brother? You would detest it. So remain mindful of Allah. Allah is Most Relenting, Most Merciful. (Quran, 49:12)
O people! We created you from a male and a female, and made you races and tribes, that you may know one another. The best among you in the sight of Allah is the most righteous. Allah is All-Knowing, Well-Experienced. (Quran, 49:13)
The Desert-Arabs say, “We have believed.” Say, “You have not believed; but say, ‘We have submitted,’ for faith has not yet entered into your hearts. But if you obey Allah and His Messenger, He will not diminish any of your deeds. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.” (Quran, 49:14)
The believers are those who believe in Allah and His Messenger, and then have not doubted, and strive for Allah’s cause with their wealth and their persons. These are the sincere. (Quran, 49:15)
Say, “Are you going to teach Allah about your religion, when Allah knows everything in the heavens and the earth, and Allah is aware of all things?” (Quran, 49:16)
They regarded it a favor to you that they have submitted. Say, “Do not consider your submission a favor to me; it is Allah who has done you a favor by guiding you to the faith, if you are sincere.” (Quran, 49:17)
Allah knows the secrets of the heavens and the earth, and Allah is seeing of everything you do. (Quran, 49:18)
Qaf. By the Glorious Quran. (Quran, 50:1)
They marveled that a warner has come to them from among them. The disbelievers say, “This is something strange. (Quran, 50:2)
When we have died and become dust? This is a farfetched return.” (Quran, 50:3)
We know what the earth consumes of them, and with Us is a comprehensive book. (Quran, 50:4)
But they denied the truth when it has come to them, so they are in a confused state. (Quran, 50:5)
Have they not observed the sky above them, how We constructed it, and decorated it, and it has no cracks? (Quran, 50:6)
And the earth, how We spread it out, and set on it mountains, and grew in it all kinds of delightful pairs? (Quran, 50:7)
A lesson and a reminder for every penitent worshiper. (Quran, 50:8)
And We brought down from the sky blessed water, and produced with it gardens and grain to harvest. (Quran, 50:9)
And the soaring palm trees, with clustered dates. (Quran, 50:10)
As sustenance for the servants. And We revive thereby a dead town. Likewise is the resurrection. (Quran, 50:11)
Before them the people of Noah denied the truth, and so did the dwellers of Russ, and Thamood. (Quran, 50:12)
And Aad, and Pharaoh, and the brethren of Lot. (Quran, 50:13)
And the Dwellers of the Woods, and the people of Tubba. They all rejected the messengers, so My threat came true. (Quran, 50:14)
Were We fatigued by the first creation? But they are in doubt of a new creation. (Quran, 50:15)
We created the human being, and We know what his soul whispers to him. We are nearer to him than his jugular vein. (Quran, 50:16)
As the two receivers receive, seated to the right and to the left. (Quran, 50:17)
Not a word does he utter, but there is a watcher by him, ready. (Quran, 50:18)
The daze of death has come in truth: “This is what you tried to evade.” (Quran, 50:19)
And the Trumpet is blown: “This is the Promised Day.” (Quran, 50:20)
And every soul will come forward, accompanied by a driver and a witness. (Quran, 50:21)
“You were in neglect of this, so We lifted your screen from you, and your vision today is keen.” (Quran, 50:22)
And His escort will say, “This is what I have ready with me.” (Quran, 50:23)
“Throw into Hell every stubborn disbeliever. (Quran, 50:24)
Preventer of good, aggressor, doubter. (Quran, 50:25)
Who fabricated another god with Allah; toss him into the intense agony.” (Quran, 50:26)
His escort will say, “Our Lord, I did not make him rebel, but he was far astray.” (Quran, 50:27)
He will say, “Do not feud in My presence—I had warned you in advance. (Quran, 50:28)
The decree from Me will not be changed, and I am not unjust to the servants.” (Quran, 50:29)
On the Day when We will say to Hell, “Are you full?” And it will say, “Are there any more?” (Quran, 50:30)
And Paradise will be brought closer to the pious, not far away. (Quran, 50:31)
“This is what you were promised—for every careful penitent. (Quran, 50:32)
Who inwardly feared the Most Gracious, and came with a repentant heart. (Quran, 50:33)
Enter it in peace. This is the Day of Eternity.” (Quran, 50:34)
Therein they will have whatever they desire—and We have even more. (Quran, 50:35)
How many generations before them, who were more powerful than they, did We destroy? They explored the lands—was there any escape? (Quran, 50:36)
In that is a reminder for whoever possesses a heart, or cares to listen and witness. (Quran, 50:37)
We created the heavens and the earth and what is between them in six days, and no fatigue touched Us. (Quran, 50:38)
So endure what they say, and proclaim the praises of your Lord before the rising of the sun, and before sunset. (Quran, 50:39)
And glorify Him during the night, and at the end of devotions. (Quran, 50:40)
And listen for the Day when the caller calls from a nearby place. (Quran, 50:41)
The Day when they will hear the Shout in all truth. That is the Day of Emergence. (Quran, 50:42)
It is We who control life and death, and to Us is the destination. (Quran, 50:43)
The Day when the earth will crack for them at once. That is an easy gathering for Us. (Quran, 50:44)
We are fully aware of what they say, and you are not a dictator over them. So remind by the Quran whoever fears My warning. (Quran, 50:45)
